+++
title = "६"
+++




\(6.1\)





## kali-dharma-nirūpaṇaṁ



**maitreya uvāca—**

**vyākhyātā bhavatā arga-vaṁśa-manvantara-sthitiḥ |**

**vaṁśānucaritaṁ caiva vistareṇa mahā-mune ||1||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **śrīmate rāmānujāya namaḥ | atha viṣṇucittī | vyākhyāteti prathamāṁśe sarga uktaḥ | dvitīyādiṣu vaṁśa-manvantara-vaṁśānucarita-rūpā sthitir uktā ||1||



**śrīdharaḥ : **śrī-ganeśāya namaḥ | 



sac-cid-ānanda-rūpāya kṛṣṇāyākliṣṭa-kāriṇe |

namo vedānta-vedyāya gurave buddhi-sākṣiṇe ||

sargādi-phalam ākhyātum uktam ātyantikaṁ layam | 

ṣaṣṭhe’ṁśe’nya-virāgāya layāntara-nirūpaṇam ||



prathamāṁśārambhoktam artham anuvadan bubhutsitam arthaṁ pṛcchati maitreyaḥ—vyākhyātety-ādi dvābhyām ||1||



**śrotum icchāmy ahaṁ tvatto yathāvad upaṁhṛtim |**

**mahā-pralaya-saṁsthānaṁ kalpānte ca mahāmune ||2||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **atha kalpānte upasaṁhṛtiṁ mahā-pralayam saṁjñām upasaṁhṛtiṁ ca śrotum icchāmi ||1||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yathāvad sarvathā upasaṁhṛtim ātyantikaṁ pralayam ity arthaḥ | kalpānte brahmaṇo dinānte ||2||



**parāśara uvāca—**

**maitreya śrūyatāṁ matto yathāvad upasaṁhṛtiḥ | **

**kalpānte prākṛte caiva pralayo jāyate yathā ||3||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **prākṛta-pralaya iti śeṣaḥ | dviparārdhaka iti vakṣyamāṇe yathopasaṁhṛtir jāyate tathā yathāvat paramārthataḥ śrūyatām ||3||



**śrīdharaḥ : **prākṛte mahā-pralaye ||3||



**aho-rātraṁ pitṝṇāṁ tu māso’bda tridivaukasām |****857**

**caturyuga-sahasre tu brahmaṇo dve dvijottama ||4||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **aho-rātram iti | mānuṣo māsaḥ pitṝṇām aho-rātram | abdo devānāṁ divye catur-yuga-sahasre dve brahmaṇo'ho-rātram ||4||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kalpa-pramāṇaṁ darśayann āha—aho-rātra iti | manuṣyāṇāṁ māsaḥ pitrṝṇām ahorātraḥ | manuṣyāṇām abdo devānām aho-rātraḥ | dve caturyuga-ahare brahmaṇo’ho-rātraḥ ||4||



**kṛtaṁ tretā dvāparaś ca kaliś caiva caturyugam |**

**divyair varṣa-sahasrais tu tad dvādaśabhir ucyate ||5||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **caturyuga-mānam āha—kṛtam iti ||5|| 



**caturyugāṇy aśeṣāṇi adṛśāni svarūpataḥ |**

**ādyaṁ kṛta-yugaṁ m uktvā maitreyānte tathā kalim ||6||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **caturyugāṇīti | svarūpataḥ parimāṇa-dharmādharmādibhiḥ | yathoktaṁ śrī-harivaṁśe—



kṛte dharmaś catuṣpāt syād adharmaḥ pāda-bhāg atha |

dvābhyām adharmaḥ pādābhyāṁ tribhir dharma tataḥ sthitaḥ ||

dvābhyāṁ dharmaḥ sthitaḥ padbhyām adharma tribhir ucchritaḥ ||

kalāv adharmaś catuṣpāt yād dharmaḥ pāda-śeṣagaḥ || iti ||



ayam arthaḥ—kṛte kṛta-yuge ādau pāda-bhāk | atha kṛtānte krameṇādharmaḥ pāda-bhāg bhavati tatas tretāyām ||6||



**śrīdharaḥ : **caturyuga-varūpam āha—caturyugāṇīti ||6||



**ādye kṛta-yuge sargo brahmaṇā kriyate yathā |**

**kriyate copasaṁhāra tathānte ca kalau yuge ||7||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ādya iti | brahmaṇā caturmukha-śarīrakeṇa bhagavatā, bhogi-śayyā-gataḥ śete trailokya-grāsa-bṛṁhitaḥ iti vacanāt | ādy-antayor yugayoḥ sṛṣṭi-saṁhārād eva viśeṣaḥ ||7||



**śrīdharaḥ : **ādyaṁ tayor vaisādṛśye hetum āha—ādya iti ||7||



**maitreya uvāca—**

**kaleḥ svarūpaṁ bhagavan vistarād vaktum arhasi |**

**dharmaś catuṣpād bhagavan yasmin viplavam ṛcchati ||8||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **aparyavaita eva pūrva-praśanayottare labdhāvaro’nyat pṛcchati kaler iti | viplavaṁ nāśam ||8||



**parāśara uvāca—**

**kaleḥ svarūpaṁ maitreya yad bhavān praṣṭum icchati |**

**tan nibodha samāsena vartate yan mahāmune ||9||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **uttaram āha—kaler ity-ādinā yāvad uttarādhyāya-samāpti ||9||



**varṇāśramācāravatī pravṛttir na kalau nṝṇām |**

**na sāma-ṛg-yajur-veda-viniṣpādana-hetukā ||10||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **varṇāśrameti | varṇāśramety-ādi-smārta-pravṛtti-viṣayam sāma-rg-yajur iti śrauta-pravṛtti-viṣaya-trayī-parasparāgni-hotrādi-dharma-viniṣpādanaṁ yasyāḥ pravṛtteḥ || hetuḥ prayojanam sā tathoktā, sā ca nety arthaḥ ||10||



**śrīdharaḥ : **varṇānām āśramāṇāṁ ca ya ācāra tad-anuāriṇī nṝṇāṁ pravṛttir na bhavati | sāmādi-vedokta-karma-viniṣpādanaṁ hetur yayā sā | tathā-bhūtā ca na bhavati, kintu artha-kāma-pradhānair vety arthaḥ ||10||



**vivāhā na kalau dharmyā na śiṣya-guru-saṁsthitiḥ |**

**na dāmpatya-kramo naiva vahni-daivātmakaḥ kramaḥ ||11||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **vivāhā iti | dāpatya-kramaḥ dampatyor dharmaḥ | dampatī eva dāmpatyam | vahni-devātmakaḥ vahnau deva-yajña-kriyātmakaḥ | kramo'nuṣṭhānam ||11||



**śrīdharaḥ : **dharmyā iti brāhmaṇādiṣu vivāheṣu yo vihitaḥ, sa eva tayeti vyavasthā nāstīty arthaḥ | śiṣyasya guroś ca samyak sthitiḥ śuśrūṣānugraha-rūpā nāsti | dāmpatye yaḥ kramaḥ paraspara-niyamo nāsti | vahnau homādi-prakāra-niyamo deveṣu pūjādi-kramaś ca nāsti ||11||



**yatra kutra****858**** kule jāto balī sarveśvaraḥ kalau |**

**sarvebhya eva varṇebhyo yogyaḥ kanyāvarodhane ||12||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **varṇebhyaḥ varṇānāṁ dhanī yogyaḥ, na tu vṛtta-vidyādimān ||12||



**śrīdharaḥ : **sarveśvaro niyantā daṇḍa-dhara iti yāvat | sa eva sarva-varṇebhyaḥ kanyāyā avarodhane parigrahe yogyo bhaviṣyati | kanyāvarodhanīti pāṭhe sa-varṇatvādi-niyamaṁ vinā sarvebhyo’pi varṇebhyo dhanī dhanavān kanyā-varo yogyo bhaviṣyatīty arthaḥ ||12||



**yena kena ca yogena dvijātir dīkṣitaḥ kalau |**

**yaiva saiva ca maitreya prāyaścittaṁ kalau kriyā ||13||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **yena kena ca śruti-smṛtibhyām anukalpatayoktena yogena prakāreṇa dīkṣīto bhavati ||13||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yena kenāpy upāyena niṣiddha-dravyādināpi dīkṣitaḥ syāt ||13||



**sarvam eva kalau śāstraṁ yasya yad-vacanaṁ dvija |**

**devatā ca kalau sarvā sarvaḥ sarvasya cāśramaḥ ||14||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **devatā ca ā avaidikī kālyādiḥ aḥ asya cāśramaḥ brahmacarya-vairāgyādi-rahitasyāpi ||14||



**upavāsas tathāyāso vittotsargas tapaḥ kalau |**

**dharmo yathābhirucitair anuṣṭhānair anuṣṭhitaḥ ||15||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **āyāsaḥ tīrtha-yātrādi-kāya-kleśaḥ | upavāsādiḥ svābhirucitānuṣṭhānānuṣṭhito dharmo bhavati ||15||



**śrīdharaḥ : **vidhi-kramaṁ vinā yathābhirucitair anuṣṭhānaiḥ kṛta upavāsādir dharmaḥ syāt | āyāsaḥ kṛcchrādir api ||15||



**vittena bhavitā puṁsāṁ svalpenāḍhya-madaḥ kalau |**

**strīṇāṁ rūpa-madaś caiva keśair eva bhaviṣyati ||16||**

**suvarṇa-maṇi-ratnādau vastre copakṣayaṁ gate |**

**kalau striyo bhaviṣyanti tadā keśair alaṅkṛtā ||17||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **keśaiḥ praśastaiḥ suvarṇādi-bhūṣaṇa-saha-pāṭhāt ||16-17||



**parityakṣyanti bhartāraṁ vitta-hīnaṁ tathā striyaḥ |**

**bhartā bhaviṣyati kalau vittavān eva yoṣitām ||18||**

**yo vai dadāti bahulaṁ svam sa svāmī sadā nṛṇām |**

**svāmitva-hetuḥ sambandho na cābhijanatā tathā ||19||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **svāmitva-hetur iti bahv-artha-dhanādinā sambandha eva svāmitva-hetur bhāvī, na tv abhijanaḥ svāmitva-hetuḥ sambandho bhavitā | abhijana iti pāṭhe svāmitva-hetur vasu-dānādi-sambandhaḥ, sa evābhijanaḥ na tu mahā-kulīnatvam | hīna-varṇo'py arthado mahā-kulīnavat sevya ity arthaḥ ||19||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yaḥ ko'pi bahu-dhanaṁ dadāti sa svāmī uttamānām api | tatra hetuḥ—dravya-dānādinā yaḥ sambandhaḥ sa eva svāmitve hetur bhāvī | na tv abhijana-satkulatvam | svāmitva-hetuḥ sambandho bhavitābhijanaḥ iti pāṭhe | svāmitva-hetunā bahu-dhanādinā yaḥ sambandhaḥ sa evābhijano mahākulīnatvaṁ bhaviṣyatīty arthaḥ ||19||



**gṛhāntā dravya-saṅghātā dravyāntā ca tathā matiḥ |**

**arthāś cātmopabhogyāntā bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ||20||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **buddheḥ ādhyaṁ dhanārjanaṁ, na tv ātma-jñānādi | tac ca dhanaṁ gṛha-nirmāṇārthaṁ, na tu yāgādhānādy-artham | te cārthā gṛha-rūpāḥ sva-deha-bhogārthāḥ ||20||



**śrīdharaḥ : **dravyāṇāṁ saṅghātāḥ saṁcayā api | gṛha evāntaḥ samāptir yeṣāṁ te tathā | bahu-dhanādi-saṅgrahā api gṛha-nirmāṇādiṣv evopakṣīṇā bhaviṣyati, na tu dharmopayogina ity arthaḥ | nṝṇāṁ matiś ca dravyāntā dravyārjana-mātra-niṣṭhā | na tv ātma-jñānopayoginī | arthāś ca bhogyāḥ srak-candanādayaḥ | ātmopabhogyāntāḥ sva-bhoga-mātra-paryavasāyinaḥ | na tv atithi-devatārthā bhaviṣyanti ||20||



**striyaḥ kalau bhaviṣyanti svairiṇyo lalita-spṛhāḥ |**

**anyāyād āpta-vitteṣu puruṣāḥ spṛhayālavaḥ ||21||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **laliteṣu puruṣeṣu spṛhā yāsāṁ tā tathoktāḥ ||21||



**śrīdharaḥ : **vairiṇyāḥ puṁścalyaḥ | tatra hetuḥ—lalite sundare spṛhā yāsāṁ tāḥ ||21||



**abhyarsthitāpi suhṛdā svārtham eva nirīkṣyate859 |**

**paṇārdhārdhārdha-mātre’pi kariṣyanti tathā spṛhām860 ||22||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **abhyarsthitāpi, abhyarsthitā api | atra ārṣaḥ sandhiḥ | devāpi yaṁ na paśyantītivat | paṇaḥ kapardikāśītiḥ | pañca-guñjātulitaṁ varṇaṁ vā ||22||



**śrīdharaḥ : **paṇaṁ varāṭikā tad-arthaṁ vā kācaḥ, tad-ardhārdha-mātre'pi viṣaye | svārthasya hāniṁ na kariṣyanti | kapardikāṁśikam api na tyakṣyantīty arthaḥ | paṇaḥ kapardikāśītiḥ pañca-guñjātulitaṁ varṇaṁ vā paṇaḥ, tatrāpīti draṣṭavyam | kariṣyanti kaliṁ dvija iti pāṭhe kaliṁ kalaham ||22||



**samāna-pauruṣaṁ ceto bhāvi vipreṣu vai kalau |**

**kṣīra-pradāna-sambandhi bhāvi goṣu ca gauravam ||23||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **samāna-pauruṣam ity apara-varnāḥ śūdrādayo viprān sva-samāna-tejaskān manyante ity arthaḥ | samāna-paruṣam iti pāṭhe sa-garva-niṣṭhuraṁ ca ceta iti ||23||



**śrīdharaḥ : s**amāna-pauruṣam asmāsu vipreṣu ca puruṣatvam samānam | tad asmatto vipreṣu ko viśeṣaḥ ? ity anādara-yuktaṁ cittaṁ śūdrāder bhaviṣyatīty arthaḥ | samāna-paruṣam iti pāṭhe sa-garva-niṣṭhuraṁ ca ceta iti | kṣīra- iti | mahiṣyādiṣv iva kṣīra-pradānato goṣu satkāro bhaviṣyati ||23||



**anāvṛṣṭi-bhaya-prāyāḥ prajāḥ kṣud-bhaya-kātarāḥ |**

**bhaviṣyanti tadā sarve gaganāsakta-dṛṣṭayaḥ ||24||**



**śrīdharaḥ :**kṣud-bhayena kātarāḥ vyākulāḥ prajāḥ megha-pratīkṣayā gagane āsakta-dṛṣṭayo bhaviṣyanti ||24||



**kanda-mūla-phalāhārā tāpasā iva mānavāḥ |**

**ātmānaṁ ghātayiṣyanti hy anāvṛṣṭy-ādi-duḥkhitāḥ ||25||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ:**ghātayiṣyanti kleśayiṣyanti ||25||



**durbhikṣam eva satataṁ tathā kleśam anīśvarāḥ |**

**prāpsyanti vyāhata-sukha-pramodā mānavāḥ kalau ||26||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ:**pramoda ullāsaḥ ||26||



**śrīdharaḥ :**anīśvarā nirdayāḥ | vyāhataṁ sukhaṁ pramodo harṣaś ca yeṣāṁ te ||26||



**asnāna-bhojino nāgni-devatātithi-pūjanam |**

**kariṣyanti kalau prāpte na ca piṇḍodaka-kriyām ||27||**

**lolupā hrasva-dehāś ca bahv-annādana-tatparāḥ |**

**bahu-prajālpa-bhāgyāś ca bhaviṣyanti kalau striyaḥ ||28||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**ubhābhyām api pāṇibhyāṁ śiraḥ-kaṇḍūyanaṁ striyaḥ |**

**kurvantyo guru-bhartṝṇām ājñāṁ bhetsyanty anādarāḥ ||29||**



**śrīdharaḥ :**anādarā ādara-śūnyāḥ ||29||



**sva-poṣaṇa-parāḥ kṣudrā deha-saṁskāra-varjitāḥ |**

**paruṣānṛta-bhāṣiṇyo bhaviṣyanti kalau striyaḥ ||30||**



**śrīdharaḥ :**paruṣam anṛtaṁ bhāṣituṁ śīlaṁ ca yāsāṁ tāḥ ||30||



**duḥśīlā duṣṭa-śīleṣu kurvantyaḥ satataṁ spṛhām |**

**asad-vṛttā bhaviṣyanti puruṣeṣu kulāṅganāḥ ||31||**



**śrīdharaḥ :**duḥśīleṣv asad-vṛtteṣu spṛhāṁ kurvantyo'sad-vṛttā vyabhicāriṇyo bhaviṣyanti ||31||.



**vedādānaṁ kariṣyanti baṭavaś cākṛta-vratāḥ |**

**gṛhathāś ca na hoṣyanti na dāsyanty ucitāny api ||32||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ:**akṛta-vratāḥ veda-vrata-rahitāḥ ||32||



**śrīdharaḥ :**āśramāṇāṁ viplavam āha—vedādānam iti | akṛta-vratā veda-vratādi-hīnāḥ | baṭavo brahmacāriṇaḥ | vedādānaṁ vedādhyayanaṁ kariṣyanti ||32||



**vānaprasthā bhaviṣyanti grāmyāhāra-parigrahāḥ |**

**bhikṣavaś cāpi mitrādi-sneha-sambandha-yantraṇāḥ ||33||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ:**vana-vāsinaḥ vānaprasthāḥ ||33||



**śrīdharaḥ :**vānaprasthā balkala-vāsasaḥ | grāmyāhāra-parigrahā bhaviṣyanti, na tu vanyāhāra-parigrahāḥ | bhikṣavaḥ saṁnyāsinaḥ | pitṛ-bhrātr-ādīn vihāya anyān mitrādīn sampādya teṣu sneha-bandhena yantraṇaṁ tad-vaśatvaṁ yeṣāṁ te tathā-bhūtā bhaviṣyanti ||33||



**arakṣitāro hartāraḥ śulka-vyājena pārthivāḥ |**

**hāriṇo jana-vittānām samprāpte tu kalau yuge ||34||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ:**śulka-vyājena śulkam iti vyapadiśya śulka-vyatiriktair dehaiś ca ||34||



**śrīdharaḥ :**pārthivā arakṣitāraḥ prajā-pālanam akurvanta eva hartāraḥ kara-grāhiṇaḥ | tathā vaṇig-jana-vittānāṁ ca apahāriṇo bhaviṣyanti ||34||



**yo yo’śva-ratha-nāgāḍhyaḥ sa sa rājā bhaviṣyati |**

**yaś ca yaś cābalaḥ sarvaḥ sa sa bhṛtyaḥ kalau yuge ||35||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**vaiśyāḥ kṛṣi-vaṇijyādi santyajya nija-karma yat |**

**śūdra-vṛttyā pravartsyanti kāru-karmopajīvinaḥ ||36||**



**śrīdharaḥ :**śūdra-vṛttyā sevayā pravartsyanti prakarṣeṇa vartsyanti, vāsaṁ kariṣyanti vartiṣyanta ity arthaḥ | kārūnām ambu-tuṣādīnām | karma kaṭa-kriyādi tenopajīvituṁ śīlaṁ yeṣāṁ te ||36||



**bhaikṣa-vrata-parāḥ śūdrāḥ pravrajyāliṅgino’dhamāḥ |**

**pāṣaṇḍa-saṁśrayāṁ vṛttim āśrayiṣyanti satkṛtāḥ ||37||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**durbhikṣa-kara-pīḍābhir atīvopadrutā janāḥ |**

**go-dhūmānna-yavānnāḍhyān deśān yāsyanti duḥkhitāḥ ||38||**



**śrīdharaḥ :**go-dhūmādy-annāḍhyān deśān yāsyanti ||38||



**veda-mārge pralīne ca pāṣaṇḍāḍhye tato jane |**

**adharma-vṛddhyā lokānām alpam āyur bhaviṣyati ||39||**

**aśāstra-vihitaṁ ghoraṁ tapyamāneṣu vai tapaḥ |**

**nareṣu nṛpa-doṣeṇa bālye mṛtyur bhaviṣyati ||40||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**bhavitā yoṣitāṁ sūtiḥ pañca-ṣaṭ-sapta-vārṣikī |**

**navāṣṭa-daśa-varṣāṇāṁ manuṣyāṇāṁ tathā kalau ||41||**

**palitodbhavaś ca bhavitā tathā dvādaśa-vārṣikaḥ |**

**nātijīvati vai kaścit kalau varṣāṇi viṁśatiḥ ||42||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ:**viṁśatiṁ nātijīvati | kaler ante trayoviṁśatim iti caturthoktaṁ jīvanam itaḥ pūrvam ||42||



**śrīdharaḥ :**manuṣyāṇāṁ puṁsāṁ sūtiḥ ||41|| viṁśati-varṣāṇy atikramya na jīvati ||42||



**alpa-prajñā vṛthā-liṅgā duṣṭāntaḥkaraṇāḥ kalau |**

**yatas tato vinaṅkṣyanti kālenālpena mānavāḥ ||43||**

**yadā yadā hi maitreya hānir dharmasya lakṣyate |**

**tadā tadā kaler vṛddhir anumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ||44||**

**yadā yadā hi pāṣaṇḍa-vṛddhir maitreya lakṣyate |**

**tadā tadā kaler vṛddhir anumeyā mahātmabhiḥ ||45||**

**yadā yadā satāṁ hānir veda-mārgānusāriṇām |**

**tadā tadā kaler vṛddhir anumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ||46||**

**prārambhāś cāvasīdanti yadā dharma-bhṛtāṁ nṛṇām |**

**tadānumeyaṁ prādhānyaṁ kaler maitreya paṇḍitaiḥ ||47||**

**yadā yadā ca yajñānām īśvaraḥ puruṣottamaḥ |**

**ijyate puruṣair yajñais tadā jñeyaṁ kaler balam ||48||  
na prītir veda-vādeṣu pāṣaṇḍeṣu yadā ratiḥ |**

**kaler vṛddhis tadā prājñair anumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ||49||**

**kalau jagat-patiṁ viṣṇuṁ sarva-sraṣṭāram īśvaram |**

**nārcayiṣyanti maitreya pāṣaṇḍopahatā janāḥ ||50||**



\(45-50\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.* 



**kiṁ devaiḥ kiṁ dvijair vedaiḥ kiṁ śaucenāmbu-janmanā |**

**ity evaṁ vipra vakṣyanti pāṣaṇḍopahatā janāḥ ||51||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **ambujanmanā vāriṇā kṛtena śaucena kim ||51||



**svalpāmbu-vṛṣṭīḥ parjanyaḥ sasyaṁ svalpa-phalaṁ tathā |**

**phalaṁ tathālpa-sāraṁ ca vipra prāpte kalau yuge ||52||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **alpa-sāraṁ nirvīryam ||52||



**śāṇī-prāyāṇi vastrāṇi śamī-prāyā mahīruhāḥ |**

**śūdra-prāyās tathā varṇā bhaviṣyati kalau yuge ||53||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **śāṇaḥ śāṇī vā śaṇa-vikāraḥ | śāṭīti pāṭhe hrasva-sthūlam ||53||



**śrīdharaḥ : **śāṇī śaṇa-sūtra-mayī paṭṭikā \#\#\# vā tat-tulyāni vastrāṇi ||53||



**aṇu-prāyāṇi dhānyāni cājya-prāyaṁ tathā payaḥ |**

**bhaviṣyati kalau prāpte hy auśīraṁ cānulepanam ||54||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **uśīraṁ surabhi-tṛṇa-viśeṣaḥ ||54||



**śvaśrū-śvaśura-bhūyiṣṭhā guravaś ca nṛṇāṁ kalau |**

**śyālādyā hāri-bhāryāś ca suhṛdo muni-sattama ||55||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **hāri-bhāryāḥ hāriṇyaḥ hṛdyā bhāryāḥ | bahuvrīhir vā hāriṇyo bhāryā yeṣāṁ te te suhṛdayḥ | bhartṝṇāṁ jārāṇāṁ ca ramya-bhāryā hi suhṛdaḥ ||55||



**śrīdharaḥ : **śyālāḥ patnī-bhrātaraḥ | hāriṇyo manoharāḥ bhāryā yeṣāṁ te tathā-vidheṣu nṛṣu sarūpaṁ bhavati ||55||



**kasya mātā pitā kasya yathā karmānugaḥ pumān |**

**iti codāhariṣyanti śvaśurānugatā narāḥ ||56||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **\#karmānugaḥ sva-karmādhīnaḥ ||56||



**vāṅ-manaḥ-kāyagair doṣair abhibhūtāḥ punaḥ punaḥ |**

**narāḥ pāpāny anudinaṁ kariṣyanty alpa-medhasaḥ ||57||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**niḥsattvānām aśaucānāṁ nihrīkāṇāṁ tathā nṛṇām |**

**yad yad duḥkhāya tat sarvaṁ kali-kāle bhaviṣyati ||58||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **yad yad vastu tat sarvaṁ duḥkhārtham eva bhaviṣyati ||58||



**niḥsvādhyāya-vaṣaṭ-kāre svadhā-svāhā-vivarjite |**

**tadā praviralo dharmaḥ kvacil loke nivatsyati ||59||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **kvacit kīkaṭādau ||59||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kvacit niṣkuṭādau ||59||



**tatrālpenaiva yatnena puṇya-skandham anuttamam |**

**karoti yaḥ kṛta-yuge kriyate tapasā hi saḥ ||60||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tatra kalau | alpenaiva yatnena hari-kīrtanādinā | anuttamaṁ puṇya-skandhaṁ puṇya-rāśiṁ karoti puruṣaḥ | yaḥ puṇya-skandhaḥ kriyate sa kṛta-yuge tapasā hi kriyate ||60||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kaler ekam mahāntaṁ guṇam āha—tatreti | alpenaiva yatnena hari-kīrtanādinā | anuttamaṁ puṇya-skandhaṁ puṇya-rāśiṁ yo naraḥ karoti sa hi kṛta-yuge tapasā mahatā kriyate | ya iti pāṭhe yaḥ ko'pi atimalino'pīty arthaḥ | ato'nenaiva guṇena kaliḥ sarva-śreṣṭha ity arthaḥ | "karoti yaṁ kṛta-yuge kriyate tapasā hi saḥ" iti pāṭhaḥ sugamaḥ ||60||



|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe ṣaṣṭhe’ṁśe prathamo’dhyāyaḥ ||



—o\)0\(o—



\(6.2\)





## veda-vyāsena kali-yugasya śūdrāṇāṁ striyāṁ ca mahattvasya varṇanaṁ



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**vyāsaś cāha mahā-buddhir yad atraiva hi vastuni |**

**tac chrūyatāṁ mahābhāga gadato mama tattvataḥ ||1||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **atra vastuni alpa-yatnena puṇya-skandha-prāptau ||1||



**śrīdharaḥ : **nikṛṣṭo'pi kalit atyāyāsena mahā-phala-prada iti prasaṅgān nikṛṣṭayoḥ strī-śūdrayor api guṇādhikyaṁ vakutm itihāsaṁ prastauti vyāsa ity ādinā | vyāsaś ceti | vastuni arthe ||1||



**kasmin kāle’lpako dharmo dadāti sumahat phalam |**

**munīnāṁ puṇya-vādo’bhūt kaiś cāsau kriyate sukham ||2||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **puṇya-vādaḥ puṇya-viṣaya-vicāraḥ ||2||



**śrīdharaḥ : **vādo vicāraḥ | kaiś cāpi jātibhiḥ | asau dharmaḥ | sukham anāyāsena kriyate ||2||



**sandeha-nirṇayārthāya veda-vyāsaṁ mahāmunim |**

**yayus te saṁśayaṁ praṣṭuṁ maitreya muni-puṅgavāḥ ||3||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **saṁśayaṁ saṁśayitam arthaṁ praṣṭum ||3||



**śrīdharaḥ : **saṁśaya-viṣaya-bhūtam arthaṁ praṣṭum yayuḥ ||3||



**dadṛśus te muniṁ tatra jāhnavī-salile dvija |**

**veda-vyāsaṁ mahā-bhāgam ardha-snātam sutaṁ mama ||4||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**nānāvasānaṁ te taya pratīkṣanto maharṣayaḥ |**

**tasthus tīre mahānadyās taru-ṣaṇḍam upāśritāḥ ||5||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **snānāvasānaṁ snāna-samāpti-pratīkṣamāṇāḥ | tarūṇāṁ ṣaṇḍaṁ samūham | upāśritāḥ tasthuḥ sthitāḥ ||5||



**magno’tha jāhnavī-toyād utthāyāha suto mama |**

**śūdraḥ sādhuḥ kaliḥ sādhur ity evaṁ śṛṇvatāṁ vacaḥ ||6||**

**teṣāṁ munīnāṁ bhūyaś ca mamajja sa nadī-jale |**

**sādhu sādhv iti cotthāya śūdra dhanyo'si cābravīt ||7||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **śūdraḥ sādhuḥ kaliḥ sādhur iti vacanāt | sādhu sādhu śūdra śūdro dhanyo'sīty uktiḥ | hṛdaya-sannidheḥ pratyakṣoktir iva bhātīti ||6-7||



**śrīdharaḥ : **unmajjya utthāya | teṣāṁ munināṁ śṛṇvatām | kaliḥ sādhuḥ śūdraḥ sādhur ity evaṁ-vaco vacanāt | sādhu sādhu śūdra śūdro dhanyo'sīty uktiḥ | hṛdaya-sannidheḥ pratyakṣoktir iva bhātīti ||6-7||



**nimagnaś ca samutthāya punaḥ prāha mahā-muniḥ |**

**yoṣitaḥ sādhu dhanyās tās tābhyo dhanyataro’sti kaḥ ||8||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tābhyo yoṣidbhyaḥ | kalau sādhutvaṁ śūdre dhanyatvaṁ yoṣitāṁ dhanyataratvaṁ ceti | tad-guṇa-tāratamyād viramya tridhoktiḥ ||8||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tābhyo yoṣidbhyaḥ | dhanyataraḥ kaḥ prāṇy asti ? na ko'pīty arthaḥ | atas tā eva dhanyatarāḥ | atra ca kaleḥ sādhutvam | śūdrasya sādhutvaṁ dhanyatvam | yoṣitāṁ dhanyataratvaṁ ceti | yathottaraṁ guṇādhikyam | tatra gaṅgāyām avamarṣaṇe bhagavad-dhyāna-pūte citte pratītam iti | unmajjyonmajjya pada-trayoktyā darśitam | unmajjyeti ca pāṭhaḥ ||8||



**tataḥ snātvā yathā-nyāyam ācāntaṁ ca kṛta-kriyam |**

**upatasthur mahā-bhāgaṁ munayas te sutaṁ mama ||9||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**kṛta-saṁvandanāṁś cāha kṛtāsana-parigrahān |**

**kim-artham āgatā yūyam iti satyavatī-sutaḥ ||10||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kṛtaṁ saṁvandanaṁ yais tān kṛta-saṁvandanān ||10||



**tam ūcuḥ saṁśayaṁ praṣṭuṁ bhavantaṁ vayam āgatāḥ |**

**alaṁ tenāstu tāvan naḥ kathyatām aparaṁ tvayā ||11||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tena pravivakṣitārthena alam astu, tan-nivṛttir astu ||11||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tena tāvad alam astu, tat tāvad āstām ity arthaḥ ||11||



**kaliḥ sādhv iti yat proktaṁ śūdraḥ sādhv iti yoṣitaḥ |**

**yad āha bhagavān sādhu dhanyāś ceti punaḥ punaḥ ||12||**

**tat sarvaṁ śrotum icchāmo na ced guhyaṁ mahā-mune |**

**tat kathyatāṁ tato hṛt-sthaṁ pṛcchāmas tvāṁ prayojanam ||13||**



\(12-13\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**ity ukto munibhir vyāsaḥ prahasyedam athābravīt |**

**śrūyatāṁ bho muni-śreṣṭhā yad uktam sādhu sādhv iti ||14||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **prahasyeti | dhig astv itivat | sva-praśnottaraṁ dattam apy abuddhān punaḥ pṛcchato munīn prati hāsaḥ ||14||



**śrīdharaḥ : **hṛt-stha-praśnasyottaraṁ | dattam apy avijñāya pṛcchantīti prahasyedam abravīt ||14||



śrī-vyāsa uvāca—

**yat kṛte daśabhir varṣais tretāyāṁ hāyanena tat |**

**dvāpare tac ca māsena hy aho-rātreṇa tat kalau ||15||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **tad eva sphuṭayati yat kṛte daśabhir ity ādi dvābhyām | kṛte kṛta-yuge hāyanena varṣeṇa ||15||



**tapaso brahmacaryasya japādeś ca phalaṁ dvijāḥ |**

**prāpnoti puruṣas tena kaliḥ sādhv iti bhāṣitam ||16||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**dhyāyan kṛte yajan yajñais tretāyāṁ dvāpare’rcayan |**

**yad āpnoti tad āpnoti kalau saṅkīrtya keśavam ||17||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **kṛte citta-śuddhi-sambhavād dhyānena phala-prāptiḥ | tretāyāṁ tad abhāve'pi citta-śuddhyā yajñaiḥ phala-siddhiḥ, dvāpare tayor abhāve'pi ācāra-śuddhyārcanena siddhiḥ | sandhyā-hīno'śucir nityam ity-ādi-vacanāt | kalau tu teṣām abhāve'pi bhagavan-nāma-saṅkīrtanenaiva phala-siddhir iti kaleḥ sādhutvam ||17||



**śrīdharaḥ : **alpena kālena dharmaḥ siddhyatīty āha—dhyāyan kṛte ity ādi dvābhyām ||17|| 



**dharmotkarṣam atīvātra prāpnoti puruṣaḥ kalau |**

**alpāyāsena dharmajñās tena tuṣṭo’my ahaṁ kaleḥ ||18||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **etad eva vivṛṇoti—dharmeti | svalpāyāsena saṅkīrtanādinā ||18||



**śrīdharaḥ : **alpāyāsena saṅkīrtanādineti kaleḥ sādhutvam uktam ||18||



**vrata-caryā-parair grāhyā vedāḥ pūrvaṁ dvijātibhiḥ |**

**tataḥ svadharma-samprāptair yaṣṭavyaṁ vidhivad dhanaiḥ ||19||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **vrata-caryety-ādi śūdra-sādhutvasya upodghātaḥ ||19||



**śrīdharaḥ : **śūdrasyālpāyāsena puruṣārtha-siddhim ca vaktuṁ traivargikāṇāṁ tatrātikleśam āha—vrata-caryā-parair ity ādi caturbhiḥ | vrata-caryopaharaṇaiḥ iti pāṭhe upaharaṇam upahāraḥ | gurave sarva-lābhārpaṇair ity arthaḥ ||19||



**vṛthā kathā vṛthā bhojyaṁ vṛthejyā ca dvijanmanām |**

**patanāya tato bhāvyaṁ tais tu saṁyamibhiḥ sadā ||20||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **vṛthā kathā śrī-kṛṣṇa-kīrtana-rahitā | vṛthā bhojyaṁ harer aniveditam ||20||



**asamyak-karaṇe doṣas teṣām sarveṣu vastuṣu |**

**bhojya-peyādikaṁ caiṣāṁ necchā-prāpti-karaṁ dvijāḥ ||21||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **icchaiva prāptikarī yasya tad-icchā-prāptikaram | icchayā prāpyaṁ ca ||21||



**śrīdharaḥ : **icchayā prāpti-karaṁ prāpyaṁ na bhavati, kintu codanayā ||21||



**pāratantryam samasteṣu teṣāṁ kāryeṣu vai yataḥ |**

**jayanti te nijān lokān kleśena mahatā dvijāḥ ||22||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tatra hetuḥ—pāratantryam iti | vidhi-pāratantryam ||22||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tatra hetuḥ—pāratantryam iti | vidhi-pāratantryam ||22||



**dvija-śuśrūṣayaivaiṣa pāka-yajñādhikāravān |**

**nijān jayati vai lokān śūdro dhanyataras tataḥ ||23||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **pāka-yajñādhikāravān śūdrasyāpy amantraka-pakva-homādiṣv adhikāraḥ | asmai sādhu-caritam iti śeṣaḥ ||23||



**śrīdharaḥ : **śūdrasya tādṛk-kleśābhāvena dhanyatvam uktam ity āha—dvija-śuśrūṣayety-ādi dvābhyām ||23||



**bhakṣyābhakṣyeṣu nāyāti peyāpeyeṣu vai yataḥ |**

**niyamo muni-śārdūlā tenāsau sādhv itīritaḥ ||24||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**sva-dharmasyāvirodhena narair labdhaṁ dhanam sadā |**

**pratipādanīyaṁ pātreṣu yaṣṭavyaṁ ca yathā-vidhi ||25||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **sva-dharmasyeti strī-sādhutvasya prastāvaḥ ||25||



**śrīdharaḥ : **strīṇām anāyāsena śreyaḥ-prāptyā dhanyatvaṁ vaktuṁ puruṣāṇāṁ tat-prāptau kleśam āha—sva-dharmasyety-ādi tribhiḥ ||25||



**tasyārjane mahā-kleśaḥ pālane ca dvijottamāḥ |**

**tathāsad-viniyogena vijñātaṁ gahanaṁ nṛṇām ||26||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **gahanaṁ kleśaḥ ||26||



**śrīdharaḥ : **evaṁ nṛṇāṁ mahān kleśaḥ ||26||



**evam anyais tathā kleśaiḥ puruṣā dvija-sattamāḥ |**

**nijān jayanti vai lokān prājāpatyādikān kramāt ||27||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**yoṣic chuśrūṣaṇād bhartuḥ karmaṇā manasā girā |**

**taddhitā śubham āpnoti tat-sālokyaṁ yato dvijāḥ ||28||**

**nātikleśena mahatā tān eva puruṣo yathā |**

**tṛtīyaṁ vyāhṛtaṁ tena mayā sādhv iti yoṣitaḥ ||29||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tān eveti | puruṣo yathā prājāpatyādikān prāpnoti, tathā yoṣit tān eva prāpnotīty arthaḥ ||28-29||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yoṣitāṁ tādṛk kleśo nāstīty āha—yoṣid ity-ādi dvābhyām | puruṣo yathā mahatā kleśena prājāpatyādikān lokān prāpnoti, tathā tān eva lokān nātikleśena yoṣit prāpnotīty arthaḥ ||28-29||



**etad vaḥ kathitaṁ viprā yan nimittam ihāgatāḥ |**

**tat pṛcchata yathā-kāmam sarvaṁ vakṣyāmi vaḥ sphuṭam ||30||**

**ṛṣayas te tataḥ procur yat praṣṭavyaṁ mahā-mune |**

**asminn eva ca tat praśne yathāvat kathitaṁ tvayā ||31||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**tataḥ prahasya tān āha kṛṣṇa-dvaipāyano muniḥ |**

**vismayotphulla-nayanāṁs tāpasāṁs tān upāgatān ||32||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **idānīṁ mad-uktam etair jñātam iti punaḥ prahasyāha | apṛṣṭenaiva vyāsena katham evaṁ nirṇayaḥ kṛta iti ? vismayenotphulle nayane yeṣāṁ tān ||32||



**mayaiṣa bhavatāṁ praśno jñāto divyena cakṣuṣā |**

**tato'haṁ vaḥ prasaṅgena sādhu sādhv iti bhāṣitam ||33||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**svalpena hi prayatnena dharmaḥ siddhyati vai kalau |**

**narair ātma-guṇāmbhobhiḥ kṣālitākhila-kilbiṣaiḥ ||34||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **uktam arthaṁ nigamayati—svalpeneti | ātmano hareḥ guṇā evāmbhāṁsi taiḥ | abhikṣālitam akhilaṁ kilbiṣaṁ yeṣāṁ taiḥ kartṛbhiḥ | dharmaḥ sidhyati ||34||



**śūdraiś ca dvija-śuśrūṣā-tatparair dvija-sattamāḥ |**

**tathā strībhir anāyāsāt pati-śuśrūṣayaiva hi ||35||**

**tatas tritayam apy etan mama dhanyataraṁ matam |**

**dharma-sampādane kleśo dvijātīnāṁ kṛtādiṣu ||36||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**bhavadbhir yad abhipretaṁ tad etat kathitaṁ mayā |**

**aspṛṣṭenāpi dharmajñāḥ kim anyat kriyatāṁ dvijāḥ ||37||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **yad abhipretam jñātum iṣṭam ||37||



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**tataḥ sampūjya te vyāsaṁ praśaśaṁsuḥ punaḥ punaḥ |**

**yathāgataṁ dvijā jagmur vyāsokti-kṛta-niścayāḥ ||38||**

**bhavato’pi mahābhāga rahasyaṁ kathitaṁ mayā |**

**atyanta-duṣṭasya kaler ayam eko mahān guṇaḥ |**

**kīrtanād eva kṛṣṇasya mukta-bandhaḥ paraṁ vrajet ||39||861**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**yac cāhaṁ bhavatā pṛṣṭo jagatām upasaṁhṛtim |**

**prākṛtām antarālāṁ ca tām apy eṣa vadāmi te ||40||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **punaḥ prāsaṅgikaṁ parisamāpya prastutam anusandhatte—yac cāham iti | antarālāṁ brahmaṇo dine dine bhavām ||40||



iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe ṣaṣṭhe’ṁśe dvitīyo’dhyāyaḥ



—o\)0\(o—



\(6.3\)





## nimeṣādi-kāla-mānasya naimittika-pralayasya ca varṇanam



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**sarveṣām eva bhūtānāṁ trividhaḥ pratisañcaraḥ |**

**naimittikaḥ prākṛtikas tathaivātyantiko layaḥ ||1||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **pratisañcaraḥ pralayaḥ ||1||



**brāhmo naimittikas teṣāṁ kalpānte pratisañcaraḥ |**

**ātyantikas tu mokṣākhyaḥ prākṛto dviparārdhakaḥ ||2||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **prākṛtodviparārdhaka iti jalpanāt parārdha-dvayātmake brahmāyuṣi pūrṇe prakṛtau tat-kāryasya layaḥ prākṛtaḥ ||1||



**śrīdharaḥ : **prākṛtodviparārdhaka iti jalpanāt parārdha-dvayātmake brahmāyuṣi pūrṇe prakṛtau tat-kāryasya layaḥ prākṛtaḥ ||1||



**śrī-maitreya uvāca—**

**parārdha-saṅkhyāṁ bhagavan mamācakṣva yayā tu saḥ |**

**dviguṇīkṛtayā jñeyaḥ prākṛtaḥ pratisañcaraḥ ||3||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **prathamāṁśe parārdha-mānam uktam eva | tathāpi kiṁ tad eva mānaṁ parārdhasya uta prakārāntaram apy astīty āśayena punaḥ pṛcchati—parārdheti ||3||



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**sthānāt sthānaṁ daśa-guṇam ekasmād gaṇyate dvija |**

**tato’ṣṭādaśame bhāge parārdham abhidhīyate ||4||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ekaṁ daśa śatam asmāt sahasram ayutaṁ tataḥ paraṁ lakṣam |

prayutaṁ koṭim arthārbudam abja kharvaṁ tato nikharvaṁ ca |

tasmān mahā-sarojaṁ śaṅkuṁ saritāṁ patiṁ tataś cāntyam |

madhyaṁ parārdham āhur yathottaraṁ daśa-guṇaṁ hi vai taj-jñāḥ ||



evaṁ dviparārdha-mānuṣa-vatsare tu mahā-saṁhāraḥ ||4||



**śrīdharaḥ : **prakārāntaram apy astīty āha—sthānāt sthānam iti | yathāha vāyuḥ—



koṭi-koṭi-sahasrāṇi parārdham iti kīrtyate |

parārdha-dviguṇaṁ cāpi param āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||

sthānaṁ daśa-guṇaṁ vidyād ekaṁ daśa-śataṁ tataḥ |

sahasram ayutaṁ tasmān niyutaṁ prayutaṁ tataḥ ||

arbudaṁ nyarbudaṁ caiva vṛndaṁ caiva tataḥ param |

kharvaṁ caiva nikharvaṁ ca śaṅkhaṁ padmaṁ tathaiva ca ||

samudro madhyam antaś ca parārdhaṁ param eva ca |

evam aṣṭādaśaitāni padāni gaṇanā-vidhau ||

kalpa-saṅkhyā-pravṛttas tu parārdho brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |

tāvac ceṣo'sya kālasya tad-ante pratisṛjyate || iti |



ekaṁ daśa-guṇaṁ daśa, daśa daśa-guṇaṁ śataṁ, śataṁ daśa-guṇaṁ sahasram ity evam eka-sthānādīnāṁ mānato vṛddhyā aṣṭādaśa-sthāne parārdhaṁ bhavati kalpāś cātra sāṅkhyeyāḥ | kalpa-saṅkhyā-pravṛttas tu parārdho brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ iti vāyūkteḥ | 



tataś ca kalpānāṁ koṭi-koṭi-sahasrāṇi parārdham | tad-dviguṇaṁ paraṁ brahmāyur ity uktaṁ bhavati | yat tūktaṁ prathamāṁśe—



nijena tasya mānena āyur varṣa-śataṁ smṛtam |

tat-parākhyaṁ tad-ardhaṁ ca parārdham abhidhīyate || \[1.3.5\]



evaṁ tu brahmaṇo varṣam evaṁ varṣa-śataṁ smṛtam | \[1.3.26\] ity ādi |



tasmin pakṣe kalpānāṁ ṣaṭ-triṁśat-sahasrāṇi brahmaṇa āyur ity uktaṁ syāt | anayoś ca pakṣayor mahā-kalpa-bhedena vyavasthā | yad vā, yathokta-kalpa-śabdena lakṣaṇayā tad-aṁśa-bhūta-divya-mānuṣa-varṣādibhiḥ parārdha-mānena virodha iti sampādanīyam ||4||



**parārdha-dviguṇaṁ yat tu prākṛtaḥ sa layo dvija |**

**tadāvyakte’khilaṁ vyaktaṁ sva-hetau layam eti vai ||5||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**nimeṣo mānuṣo yo’sau mātrāmātrā-pramāṇataḥ |**

**taiḥ pañcadaśabhiḥ kāṣṭhā triṁśat-kāṣṭhā kalā smṛtā ||6||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **yaḥ prāg-uktao nimeṣaḥ, asau mātrety ucyate mātra-pramāṇatvāt | eka-mātra-laghv-akṣaroccāraṇa-kāla-saṁmito hy asau ||6||



**śrīdharaḥ : **naimittikaṁ layaṁ prapañcayiṣyan nimeṣādi-krameṇa prathamāṁśoktam eva kalpa-pramāṇam anusārayati—nimeṣa ity ādi saptabhiḥ | mātraiva mātrā saiva pramāṇaṁ yasya saḥ eka-mātra-laghv-akṣaroccāraṇa-mātra-kāla-sammito nimeṣaḥ | nimeṣa-kāla-tulyo hi mātrā laghv akṣaraṁ ca yat iti brahmāṇḍokteḥ ||6||



**nāḍikā tu pramāṇena sā kalā daśa paṁ ca ca |**

**unmānenāmbhasaḥ sā tu palāny ardha-trayodaśa ||7||**

**māgadhena tu mānena jala-prasthas tu sa smṛtaḥ |**

**hema-māṣaiḥ kṛta-cchidraś caturbhiś caturaṅgulaiḥ ||8||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tulayā mitasyāmbhasordhva-trayodaśa-palāni, ardhaṁ trayodaśaṁ yeṣāṁ tāni ardha-trayodaśa sārdha-dvādaśety arthaḥ | sā nāḍikā upacārāt tair nāḍikā jñātavyā ity arthaḥ | 



katham ? ity āha—hemeti | māṣaḥ pañca-guñjā-mānam | jalasyaitat sārdhaṁ pala-dvādaśakaṁ magadha-deśya prasthaṁ pūrayati | sa ca prasthaś caturguṇaḥ sann nāḍī-jñāpaka iti śeṣaḥ | yathāha vāyuḥ—



unmānenāmbhasaś cāpi palāny ardha-trayodaśa |

māgadhena tu mānena jala-prastho vidhīyate ||

ete cāpy udaka-prasthāś catvāro nāḍikā ghaṭaḥ |

hema-māṣaiḥ kṛta-cchidraś caturbhiś caturaṅgulaiḥ || iti |



evaṁ catur-māṣa-suvarṇa-racita-caturaṅgula-sūcīkṛtādhaś chidrād āḍhaka-jala-pūṛṇāt pañcāśat-parimāṇād ghaṭāt tac-chidreṇa pañcāśat-palaṁ jalaṁ yāvatā kālena niḥsarati tāvat-kālo nāḍīty uktaṁ bhavati | 



athavā aho-rātreṇa jalasya pūraṇaṁ niḥsaraṇaṁ vā ṣaṣṭhi-vāraṁ yathā syāt tathā tat-pātra-mānaṁ kāryam | anye tu catur-māṣa-hema-nirmitayā catur-aṅgulayā sūcyā kṛta-cchidre sārdha-dvādaśa-pale tāmra-pātre tat-pramāṇaṁ jalaṁ tac-chidreṇa yāvatā kāle praviśati sa kāla ekā nāḍikā tāni palāni māgadha-mānena jala-prastha iti varṇayanti | 



kṛta-cchidrair iti ca paṭhanti | tatrāyam anvayaḥ—sā nāḍikā caturbhir hema-māṣaiḥ kṛta-cchidrair niṣpannāny ambahsordhva-trayodaśa-palānīti ||8||



**śrīdharaḥ : **nāḍikājñānopāyam āha unmānenety-ādinārdhena | ambhasaḥ unmānena unmīyate anenety unmānaṁ pātram | ardhonāni trayodaśa sārdha-dvādaśety arthaḥ | unmāna-rūpeṇa ghaṭitāni sārdha-dvādaśa-palāni sā nāḍikā | sārdha dvādaśa-pala-tāmra-nirmita-pātrān nāḍikā jñātety arthaḥ | 



kiṁ-pramāṇaṁ tat pātraṁ kāryam ? tatrāha—māgadheneti | māgadhena pramāṇena jala-prasthas tu sa smṛtaḥ iti | sārdha-dvādaśa-pala-jalena hi magadha-deśyaḥ prasthaḥ pūryate, tāvat pramāṇaṁ pātraṁ kāryam ity arthāt siddham |



nanu tathāpi pātreṇa kathaṁ nāḍikājñānaṁ kriyā-paricchedyatvāt kālasyety āśaṅkya kriyā-siddhaye prasthaṁ viśinaṣṭi—hemeti | māṣaḥ pañca-guñjaḥ hema-māṣaiś caturbhiḥ caturaṅgula-śalākā-rūpeṇa kṛtaiḥ kṛta-cchidraḥ | tad uktaṁ bhavati—sārdha-dvādaśa-pala-tāmra-mayaṁ māgadha-prastha-sammitam ūrdhvāyanaṁ pātraṁ catur-māṣa-catur-aṅgula-hema-śalākayā kṛta-cchidraṁ jale sthāpitaṁ tena cchidreṇa yāvatā kālena pūryate tāvat-kālo nāḍiketi | tathā ca śukaḥ—



dvādaśārdha-palonmānaṁ caturbhiś catur-aṅgulaiḥ |

svarṇa-māṣaiḥ kṛta-cchidraṁ yāvat prastha-jala-plutam || \[bhā.pu. 3.11.9\] iti ||8||



**nāḍikābhyām atha dvābhyām muhūrto dvija-sattama |**

**aho-rātraṁ muhūrtās tu triṁśan māso dinais tathā ||9||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **tathā triṁśatā dinaiḥ māsa ity arthaḥ ||9||



**māsair dvādaśabhir varṣam aho-rātraṁ tu tad divi |**

**tribhir varṣa-śatair varṣaṁṣaṣṭhyā caivāsura-dviṣām ||10||**

**tais tu dvādaśa-sāhasraiś catur-yugam udāhṛtam |**

**caturyuga-sahasraṁ tu kathyate brahmaṇo dinam ||11||**

**sa kalpas tatra manavaś caturdaśa mahā-mune |**

**tad-ante caiva maitreya brāhmo naimittiko layaḥ ||12||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**tasya svarūpam atyugraṁ maitreya gadato mama |**

**śṛṇuṣva prākṛtaṁ bhūyas tava vakṣyāmy ahaṁ layam ||13||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **naimittika-laya-prakāram āha—tasya svarūpam ity ādinā yāvad-adhyāya-parisamāpti ||13||



**caturyuga-sahasrānte kṣīṇa-prāye mahī-tale |**

**anāvṛṣṭir atīvāgrā jāyate śatavārṣikī ||14||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kṣīṇa-prāye durbhikṣādibhiḥ ||14||



**tato yāny alpa-sārāṇi tāni sattvāny aśeṣataḥ |**

**kṣayaṁ yānti muni-śreṣṭha pārthivāny anupīḍanāt ||15||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**tataḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇū rudra-rūpa-dharo’vyayaḥ |**

**kṣayāya yatate kartum ātma-sthāḥ sakalāḥ prajāḥ ||16||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **kṣayāya rudra-rūpa-dharo bhūtvā ||16||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kṣayāya rudra-rūpa-dharaḥ san | ātma-sthāḥ svasmin līnāḥ prajāḥ kartuṁ yatate prayatate ||16||



**tataḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇur bhānoḥ saptasu raśmiṣu |**

**sthitaḥ pibaty aśeṣāṇi jalāni muni-sattama ||17||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **sapta raśmayaḥ | 



suṣumno harikeśaś ca viśvakarmā tathaiva ca | 

viśvavyacā svadhā saṁyad-vasur arvāg-vasus tathā || ity uktāḥ ||17||



**śrīdharaḥ : **sapta-raśmayaḥ pūrvoktāḥ | 



suṣumno harikeśaś ca viśvakarmā tathaiva ca | 

viśvavyacā svadhā saṁyad-vasur arvāg-vasus tathā || iti ||17||



**pītvāmbhāṁsi samastāni prāṇi-bhūmi-gatāny api |**

**śoṣaṁ nayati maitreya samastaṁ pṛthivī-talam ||18||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **prāṇi-gatāni rakta-vasādīni | bhūmi-gatāni taṭākā-sthitāni ||18||



**samudrān saritaḥ śaila-nadī-prasravaṇāni ca |**

**pātāleṣu ca yat toyaṁ tat sarvaṁ nayati kṣayam ||19||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**tatas tasyānubhāvena toyāhāropabṛṁhitāḥ |**

**ta eva raśmayaḥ sapta jāyante sapta bhāskarāḥ ||20||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **bhāskarā ārogo bhrāja ity ādayaḥ ||20||



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhāskarāḥ sapta | ārogo bhrājaḥ paṭaraḥ pataṅgaḥ svarṇa-ro;gyattiṣīmān vibhāsaḥ iti sapta sūryāḥ śrut-uktāḥ ||20||



**adhaś cordhvaṁ ca te dīpās tataḥ sapta divākarāḥ |**

**dahanty aśeṣaṁ trailokyaṁ sapātāla-talaṁ dvija ||21||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**dahyamānaṁ tu tair dīptais trailokyaṁ dvija bhāskaraiḥ |**

**sādri-nady-arṇavābhogaṁ nisneham abhijāyate ||22||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **ābhogo vistāraḥ | nisneham atirūkṣam ||22||



**tato nirdagdha-vṛkṣāmbu trailokyam akhilaṁ dvija |**

**bhavaty eṣā ca vasudhā kūrma-pṛṣṭhopamākṛtiḥ ||23||**

**tataḥ kālāgni-rudro’sau bhūtvā sarva-haro hariḥ |**

**śeṣāhi-śvāsa-sambhūtaḥ pātālāni dahaty adhaḥ ||24||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**pātālāni samastāni sa dagdhvā jvalano mahān |**

**bhūmim abhyetya sakalaṁ babhasti****862**** vasudhā-talam ||25||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **babhasti bhakṣayati | bhas bhakṣaṇe dīptyoḥ ||25||



**śrīdharaḥ : **hinasti bhasmīkaroti ||25||



**bhuvar-lokaṁ tataḥ sarvaṁ svar-lokaṁ ca sudāruṇaḥ |**

**jvālā-mālā-mahāvartas tatraiva parivartate ||26||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**ambarīṣam ivābhāti trailokyam akhilaṁ tadā |**

**jvālāvarta-parīvāram upakṣīṇa-carācaram ||27||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ambarīṣaṁ mārjana-bhāṇḍam ||27||



**tatas tāpa-parītās tu loka-dvaya-nivāsinaḥ |**

**kṛtādhikārā gacchanti maharlokaṁ mahā-mune ||28||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **kṛtādhikārā manv-ādayaḥ | daśāvṛttyā sapta-pātālāni trayo lokā iti daśa teṣv āvṛttyā vṛtty-abhāvena | yad vā, tāpa-daśāyā āvṛttyā | paraiṣiṇaḥ para-sthānaiṣiṇaḥ | athavā trailokye ye kṛtādhikārā manv-ādyāḥ, te hṛtādhikārā bhogāt prakṣīṇa-tad-deśa-bhogya-karmāṇaḥ santo mahar-lokaṁ prāpya tasmād api taptāt tal-loka-vāsibhiḥ saha sa-śarīrāḥ jana-lokaṁ yānti | teṣāṁ madhye ye pariṣiṇaḥ paraṁ prāptum icchavas te daśa-vārāvṛttyaiva tapaḥ-satya-prāpti-dvārā tataḥ param īśvaraṁ viśanti | anye trailokya-sthā jīvāḥ svātmani saṁlīyante | yathāha vāyuḥ—



pitṛbhir manubhiś caiva sādhyaiḥ saptarṣibhis tathā |

yajvānaś caiva te'py anye tad-bhaktāś caiva taiḥ saha ||

mahar-lokaṁ gamiṣyanti tyaktvā trailokyam īśvarāḥ |

mahar-lokaṁ parityajya gaṇās te'pi caturdaśa |

sa-śarīrāś ca yānty anye jana-lokaṁ sahānugaiḥ |

evaṁ devāḥ sa-pitara ṛṣayo mānavāś ca ye |

mitraiḥ sahordhvaṁ gacchanti vyāvartate ca taiḥ saha ||

jana-lokāt surāḥ sarve daśa-kalpān punaḥ punaḥ |

paryāya-kāle samprāpte sambhūtāni dhaneṣv iha |

avaśya-bhāvinārthena sambadhyante tathā tu te |

nivartante tathā vṛttyā teṣāṁ sadyo na nistaraḥ |



mahar-janaṁ cāpi janāt tapaṁ ca 

hy ekāntatas tāni bhavanti satye |

manvantarāṇāṁ parivartanāni 

muñcanti satyena tapoparāṇi ||



tapobhir yogād viṣaya-prahāṇād

viśanti te'pīśvaram eva devam || iti |



atha ātmani mahā-tejāḥ sarvam ādhāya sarva-kṛt |

tataḥ sa rātriṁ svapiti tamasy ekārṇave jale || iti ||



hatādhikārā gacchantīti ca pāṭhaḥ ||28||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tata ity ādi śloka-dvayasyaikānvayaḥ | daśāvṛttyā gabhasti-gata-svīya-niyoga-daśāyāḥ tatratya-phala-bhogāvasthāyāḥ | āvṛttyā parivṛttyā | paraiṣiṇaḥ ūrdhva-lokaiṣiṇaḥ | anye tv āhuḥ—trailokye'pi ye kṛtādhikārā manv-ādyāḥ, te hṛtādhikārā bhoga-prakṣīṇa-karmāṇaḥ santaḥ mahar-lokaṁ prāpya tasmād abhitaptāḥ tad-vāsibhiḥ saha sa-gaṇaṁ janaṁ yānti | teṣāṁ manv-ādīnāṁ madhye ye pariṣiṇaḥ para-vastu prāptum icchantaḥ, te daśa-vāram āvṛttyā ākramya tad-vyāpti-dvārā tataḥ param īśvaraṁ viśanti | anye tu trailokyasthā jīvāḥ ātmani saṁlīyante | yathāha vāyuḥ—\[*viṣṇucitta-ṭīkā draṣṭavyā*\] ... ||28||



**tasmād api mahā-tāpa-taptā lokāt tataḥ param |**

**gacchanti jana-lokaṁ te daśāvṛttyā paraiṣiṇaḥ ||29||**

**tato dagdhvā jagat sarvaṁ rudra-rūpī janārdanaḥ |**

**hrasva-niḥśvāsajān meghān karoti muni-sattama ||30||**

**tato gajakula-prakhyās taḍitvanto’tinādinaḥ |**

**uttiṣṭhanti tathā vyomni ghorāḥ saṁvartakā ghanāḥ ||31||**

**kecin nīlotpala-śyāmāḥ kecit kumuda-sannibhāḥ |**

**dhūmra-varṇā ghanāḥ kecit kecit pītāḥ payodharāḥ ||32||**

**kecid rāsabha-varṇābhā lākṣā-rasa-nibhās tathā |**

**kecid vaiḍūrya-saṅkāśā indranīla-nibhāḥ kvacit ||33||**

**śaṅka-kunda-nibhāś cānye jāty-añjana-nibhāḥ pare |**

**indragopa-nibhāḥ kecit tataḥ śikhi-nibhās tathā ||34||**



\(29-34\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**manaḥ-śilābhāḥ kecid vai haritāla-nibhāḥ pare |**

**cāṣa-patra-nibhā kecid uttiṣṭhante mahā-ghanāḥ ||35||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **cāṣo nīla-pakṣaḥ śakuniḥ ||35||



**kecit puravarākāraḥ kecit parvata-sannibhāḥ |**

**kūṭāgāra-nibhāś cānye kecit sthala-nibhā ghanāḥ ||36||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kūṭāgāraṁ gṛha-viśeṣaḥ ||36||



**mahā-rāvā mahā-kāyāḥ pūrayanti nabhaḥ-sthalam |**

**śamayanty akhilaṁ vipra trailokyāntara-dhiṣṭhitam ||37||**

**naṣṭe cāgnau ca satataṁ varṣamāṇā hy ahar-niśam |**

**plāvayanti jagat sarvam ambhobhir muni-sattama ||38||**

**dhārābhir atimātrābhiḥ plāvayitvākhilaṁ bhuvam |**

**bhuvar-lokaṁ tathaivordhvaṁ plāvayanti hi te dvija ||39||**

**andhakārī-kṛte loke naṣṭe sthāvara-jaṅgame |**

**varṣanti te mahā-meghā varṣāṇām adhikaṁ śatam ||40||**

**evaṁ bhavati kalpānte samastaṁ muni-sattama |**

**vāsudevasya māhātmyān nityasya paramātmaḥ ||41||**



\(37-41\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe ṣaṣṭhe’ṁśe tṛtīyo’dhyāyaḥ



—o\)0\(o—



\(6.4\)





## prākṛta-pralaya-varṇanam



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**saptarṣi-sthānam ākramya sthite’mbhasi mahāmune |**

**ekārṇavaṁ bhavaty etat trailokyam akhilaṁ tataḥ ||1||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **tad evaṁ naimittikaṁ trailokya-pralayaṁ nirūpya tat-kālīnāṁ sthitiṁ nirūpayann āha—saptarṣi-sthānam ity ādinā janāvṛṣṭyety-antaḥ prāktanena granthena ||1||



**mukha-niḥśvāsajo viṣṇor vāyus tān jaladāṁs tataḥ |**

**nāśayan vāti maitreya varṣāṇām aparaṁ śatam ||2||**

**sarva-bhūta-mayo’cintyo bhagavān bhūta-bhāvanaḥ |**

**anādir ādir viśvasya pītvā vāyum aśeṣataḥ ||3||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**ekārṇave tatas tasmin śeṣa-śayy āgataḥ prabhuḥ |**

**brahma-rūpa-dharaḥ śete bhagavān ādikṛd dhariḥ ||4||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **brahma-rūpa-dharaḥ iti prathamāṁśe vyākhyātaṁ nanūttaratra brahmādīnāṁ śubhāśrayatvaṁ niṣidhyate tat katham atra brahma-rūpa-dharasya mumukṣubhiś cintyamānatvam ucyate | dhāraṇāsiddhy-arthaṁ tatra śubhāśraya uktaḥ | niṣpanna-samādhīnāṁ tu jagad-rūpatayā bhagavad-anusandhānam aviruddhaṁ yathā, mattaḥ sarvam ahaṁ sarvam ahaṁ manur abhavam ity ādi | kiṁ ca, paraśurāma-kalky-ādivad anupraveśāvatāratvāc cetanāvirodhaḥ ||4|| 



**śrīdharaḥ : **śeṣa eva śayyā, tāṁ gataḥ śete ||4||



**jana-loka-gataiḥ siddhaiḥ sanakādyair abhiṣṭutaḥ |**

**brahma-loka-gataiś caiva cintyamāno mumukṣubhiḥ ||5||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**ātma-māyā-mayīṁ divyāṁ yoga-nidrāṁ samāsthitaḥ |**

**ātmānaṁ vāsudevākhyaṁ cintayan madhusūdanaḥ ||6||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ātma-māyā-mayīṁ mūla-prakṛty-abhimāni-devatām | yoga-nidrāṁ yoga-rūpāṁ nidrām | etad vivṛṇoti ātmānaṁ cintayann iti yat ||6||



**eṣa naimittiko nāma maitreya pratisañcaraḥ |**

**nimittaṁ tatra yac chete brahma-rūpa-dharo hariḥ ||7||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **nimittaṁ tatreti | tatra brahmaṇo dinānte ||7||



**yadā jāgarti sarvātmā sa tadā ceṣṭate jagat |**

**nimīlaty etad akhilaṁ māyā-śayyāṁ gate’cyute ||8||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **sa yadā jāgarti tadā jagac ceṣṭate sṛṣṭy-unmukhaṁ bhavati ||8||



**padmayoner dinaṁ yat tu catur-yuga-sahasravat |**

**ekārṇavīkṛte loke tāvatī rātrir iṣyate ||9||**



**śrīdharaḥ :**kiyantaṁ kālaṁ śete ? kadā vā prabudhyate sa jagatpatiḥ ? ity āha—padmayoner ity ādi dvābhyām ||9||



**tataḥ prabuddho rātryante punaḥ sṛṣṭiṁ karoty ajaḥ |**

**brahma-svarūpa-dhṛg viṣṇur yathā te kathitaṁ purā ||10||**

**ity eṣa kalpa-saṁhāro’vāntara-pralayo dvija |**

**naimittikas te kathitaḥ prākṛtaṁ śṛṇvataḥ param ||11||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**anāvṛṣṭy-ādi-samparkāt kṛte saṁkṣālane mune |**

**samasteṣv eve lokeṣu pātāleṣv akhileṣu ca ||12||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **samasteṣu lokeṣu pātāleṣu ca saṁkṣālane nāśe kṛte ||12||



**mahad-āder vikārasya viśeṣāntasya saṅkṣaye |**

**kṛṣṇecchākārite tasmin pravṛtte pratisañcare ||13||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tasmin prākṛte pratisañcare mahad-āder viśeṣāntasya vikārasya saṁkṣaye ca pravṛtte prastute ||13||



**śrīdharaḥ : **mahad-āder viśeṣāntasya saṅkṣaye nimitte pratisañcare pravṛtta ity arthaḥ ||13||



**āpo grasanti vai pūrvaṁ bhūmer gandhātmakaṁ guṇam |**

**ātta-gandhā tato bhūmiḥ pralayatvāya kalpate ||14|||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **pralayatvāya prakṛṣṭo layo yasyāḥ sā pralayā tad-bhāvāya ||14||



**śrīdharaḥ : **āttaḥ apahṛto gandho yasyāḥ sā | ātma-gandheti pāṭhe'py evam evārthaḥ | pralayatvāya līnatvāt salilenaiva lokā vyāptā āsann iti tṛtīyenānvayaḥ ||14||



**praṇaṣṭe gandha-tanmātre bhavaty urvī jalātmikā |**

**āpas tadā pravṛddhās tu vegavatyo mahāsvanāḥ ||15||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **atra tanmātra-grahaṇaṁ viśeṣasyāpy upalakṣaṇam ||15||



**sarvam āpūrayantīdaṁ tiṣṭhanti vicaranti ca |**

**salilenormi-mālena ālokāntāt****863**** samantataḥ ||16||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **salilena oghena ālokāntāt lokāntaṁ yāvat | ālokas tejo vā ||16||



**śrīdharaḥ : **salilenaivormitā vyāptā lokāḥ | samantata iti ca pāṭhaḥ ||16||



**apām api guṇo yas tu jyotiṣā pīyate tu saḥ |**

**naśyanty āpas tatas tāś ca rasa-tanmātra-saṅkṣayāt ||17||**

**tataś cāpo hṛta-rasā jyotiṣaṁ prāpnuvanti vai |**

**agny-avasthe tu salile tejasā sarvato vṛte ||18||**

**sa cāgniḥ sarvato vyāpya cādatte taj-jalaṁ tathā |**

**sarvam āpūryate rcibhis tadā jagad idaṁ śanaiḥ ||19||**



\(17-19\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**arcibhiḥ saṁvṛte tasmiṁs tiryag ūrdhvam adhas tadā |**

**jyotiṣo’pi paraṁ rūpaṁ vāyur atti prabhākaram ||20||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **prabhākaraṁ prakāśa-karaṁ rūpaṁ vāyur atti grasate ||20||



**pralīne ca tatas tasmin vāyu-bhūte’khilātmani |**

**praṇaṣṭe rūpa-tanmātre hṛta-rūpo vibhāvasuḥ ||21||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**praśāmyati tadājyotir vāyur dodhūyate mahān |**

**nirāloke tathā loke vāyv-avasthe ca tejasi ||22||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ajyotir iti pada-cchedaḥ | tac ca vāyu-viśeṣaṇam | jyotir-virodhī ||22||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tadā ājyotiḥ jyotir-yuktaḥ vāyur dodhūyate pracalati ||22||



**tatas tu mūlam āsādya vāyuḥ sambhavam ātmanaḥ |**

**ūrdhvaṁ cādhaś ca tiryak ca dodhavīti diśo daśa ||23||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tumulaṁ sa-śabdam | ātmanaḥ sambhavaṁ kham ||23||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tumulaṁ sa-śabdam | ātmanaḥ sambhavaṁ kāraṇam ākāśam āsādya pūrvādyāḥ daśa diśo'pi dodhavīti kampayati ||23||



**vāyor api guṇaṁ sparśam ākāśo grasate tataḥ |**

**praśāmyati tato vāyuḥ khaṁ tu tiṣṭhaty anāvṛtam ||24||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**arūpa-rasam asparśam agandhaṁ na ca mūrtimat |**

**sarvam āpūrayac caiva sumahat tat prakāśate ||25||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **na ca mūrtimat niravayavam ||25||



**parimaṇḍalaṁ ca suṣiram ākāśaṁ śabda-lakṣaṇam |**

**śabda-mātraṁ tad ākāśaṁ sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati ||26||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**tataḥ śabda-guṇaṁ tasya bhūtādir grasate punaḥ |**

**bhūtendriyeṣu yugapad bhūtādau saṁsthiteṣu vai |**

**abhimānātmako hy eṣa bhūtādis tāmasaḥ smṛtaḥ ||27||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ahaṅkārāvacchinnatayā parimāṇa-niṣedhāyogāt bhūtādi-śabdena trividhāhaṅkārasya grahaṇam ||27||



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhūtādi grasata ity anenātra na tāmasa-mātrasya kiṁ tu tamaḥ-pradhānatvena sāmānyato'haṅkāra-mātrasya | ata eva bhūtānām indriyāṇāṁ ca yugapat tatra layokter devānām apy upalakṣaṇam | abhimāna-viṣayāṇāṁ bhūtādīnāṁ līnatvāt kevalābhimānātmakasya cāvaraṇaika-bhāvatvād eṣa bhūtādis tamaḥ pradhānaḥ smṛta ity arthaḥ ||27||



**bhūtādiṁ grasate cāpi mahān vai buddhi-lakṣaṇaḥ ||28||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **buddhi-lakṣaṇaḥ sattva-pradhānatvāt ||28||



**ūrvī mahāṁś ca jagataḥ prānte’ntar bāhyatas tathā ||29||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **urvī mhaṁś ca | antaḥ aṇḍasyāntaḥ | sthitasya jagataḥ prānte carama-koṭyāṁ prathama-koṭyāṁ ca tathā bāhyataḥ aṇḍād bahir api tathā pṛthivy-eka-prānte mahān itara-prānte ||29||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yathā sṛṣṭi-krama-prātilomyena pṛthivy-āder mahat-tattva-paryanto laya uktaḥ | tathā āvaraṇeṣv apy ayam eva laya-krama iti vaktuṁ brahmāṇḍāntar-vartinaḥ kāryasya jagataḥ koṭiṁ darśayati urvī mahāṁś ceti | brahmāṇḍasyāntar yathā jagataḥ pṛthivī mahat-tattvaṁ ca prānte ādy-anta-sīmnor bhavataḥ, tathā brahmāṇḍād bāhyato'pi ||29||



**evaṁ sapta mahā-buddhe kramāt prakṛtayaḥ smṛtāḥ |**

**pratyāhāre tu tāḥ sarvāḥ praviśanti parasparam ||30||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ayam āvaraṇa-laya-viṣayaḥ ślokaḥ | mahad-ādayaḥ sapta-kramād ahaṅkārādīnāṁ prakṛtayaḥ smṛtāḥ, tāḥ pratyāhāre tu parasparaṁ svaṁ svaṁ kāraṇam evaṁ pūrvokta-laya-krameṇa praviśanti ||30||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tataḥ kim ? ata āha—evam iti | yathā carama-sṛṣṭāṁ pṛthivīm ārabhya prathama-sṛṣṭa-mahat-tattva-paryantaṁ prātilomyena sva-sva-kāraṇe layam eṣyanti | kāraṇa-bhūtā api yāḥ pṛthivy-ādyāḥ sapta prakṛtayaḥ, tā api pratyāhāreparasparaṁ svaṁ svaṁ kāraṇaṁ praviśanti ||30||



**yenedam āvṛtaṁ sarvam aṇḍam apsu pralīyate |**

**sapta-dvīpa-samudrāntaṁ sapta-lokaṁ sa-parvatam ||31||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **etad eva prapañcayati—yeneti | evaṁ-bhūtam idam aṇḍaṁ yenāvṛtaṁ tat pṛthivy-āvaraṇam apsu līyate ||31||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tadāha yenety-ādi tribhiḥ | yena sapta-dvīpādikam āvṛtam āsīt tad aṇḍa-kaṭāha-rūpā pṛthivī svāvaraṇa-rūpāsv apsu pralīyata ity arthaḥ ||31||



**udakāvaraṇaṁ yat tu jyotiṣā pīyate tu tat |**

**jyotir vāyau layaṁ yāti yāty ākāśe samīraṇaḥ ||32||**

**ākāśaṁ caiva bhūtādir grasate taṁ tathā mahān |**

**mahāntam ebhiḥ sahitaṁ prakṛtir grasate dvija ||33||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**guṇa-sāmyam anudriktam anyūnaṁ ca mahāmune |**

**procyate prakṛtir hetuḥ pradhānaṁ kāraṇaṁ param ||34||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **prakṛti-svarūpaṁ darśayan tat-kāryaṁ tasmin layam upasaṁharati—guṇa-sāmyam ity ādi dvābhyām ||34||



**ity eṣā prakṛtiḥ sarvā vyaktāvyakta-svarūpiṇī |**

**vyakta-svarūpam avyakte tasmān maitreya līyate ||35||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **vyaktāvastham api prakṛti-dravyam eva na dravyāntaraṁ tasmād vyaktam avyakte līyate | tasyā iti pāṭhe svarūpam iy anuṣaṅgaḥ ||35||



**śrīdharaḥ : **vyaktāvyakta-svarūpiṇī kārya-kāraṇa-rūpā ||35||



**ekaḥ śuddho’kṣaro nityaḥ sarva-vyāpī tathā pumān |**

**so’py aṁśaḥ sarva-bhūtasya maitreya paramātmaḥ ||36||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ekaḥ śuddhaḥ prakṛtivad anekatvānarhaḥ vaicitryānarhaś ca | anekatva-bodhaka-vaicitryārha-sattvādi-guṇamayatvābhāvāt, ata ekākṣaro nityaś ca | tatra hetum āha—sarva-vyāpīti | sūkṣmatvāt prakṛter api vyāpana-svabhāvaḥ, so'pi pumān paramātmano'ṁśaḥ | yathā prakṛtiḥ atra laya-sthānatvena prakṛteḥ prakṛtatvāt prasaṅgāt puruṣa-paramātmanoḥ prastāvaḥ ||36||



**śrīdharaḥ : **prakṛti-puruṣayor api paramātmani layaṁ vaktuṁ tayos tad-aṁśatvam āha—eka iti | sarva-vyāpī prakṛtes tat-kāryasya cādhiṣṭhātā so'pīty api-śabdāt prakṛtir api sarva-bhūtasya prakṛty-ādi-sarvātmakasya paramātmanaḥ aṁśaḥ ||36||



**na santi yatra sarveśe nāma-jāty-ādi-kalpanāḥ |**

**sattā-mātrātmake jñeye jñānātmany ātmanaḥ pare ||37||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **param āha—na santīti | nanv aṁśatva-vacanāt puruṣasya paramātmaika-dravyatvaṁ syāt ? naivaṁ, samasta-heya-rahitaṁ sa sarva-bhūta-prakṛtiṁ vikārān, viṣṇuḥ samastendriya-deha-dehī kṣetrajña-śaktiḥ sāveṣṭitā, nityo nityānāṁ, pṛthag ātmānaṁ preritāraṁ ca matvā, uttamaḥ puruṣas tv anyaḥ \[gītā 15.17\] ity ādibhis tayor atyanta-vailakṣaṇyasyoktatvāt | 



katham aṁśatvam ? ity āśaṅkya, prakāśādivan naivaṁ paraḥ ity ādinā sūtrakāraḥ prakāśa-jāti-guṇa-dehavad ātmano'pi śarīra-bhūtasya tiṣṭhataḥ paramātmaika-dehatvāt aṁśatvam upapāditavān sattā-mātrātmaka iti vikāra-niṣedhaḥ jñeye nārāyaṇaṁ mahā-jñeyam ity ādinā ātmanaḥ pare yasyātmā śarīram iti śarīratvenoktatvāt baddhān muktāc cātmano'tyanta-vilakṣaṇe prakāśa-tadvator iva jagad-brahmaṇoḥ śarīra-śarīri-bhāvaḥ svābhāvikaḥ na jīvavat karma-kṛtaḥ | tatpuruṣasya viśvam ājānam agre, vedātma-śaktiṁ svāc charīrāt ity ādeḥ ||37||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kaḥ punaḥ paramātmā ? ity atrāha—na santīty-ādi dvābhyām | ātmanaḥ puruṣāt pare ||37||



**tad brahma paramaṁ dhāma paramātmā sa ceśvaraḥ |**

**sa viṣṇuḥ sarvam evedaṁ yato nāvartate yatiḥ ||38||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**prakṛtir yā mayā khyātā vyaktāvyakta-svarūpiṇī | **

**puruṣaś cāpy ubhāv etau līyete paramātmanī ||39|| **



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **prakṛteḥ paramātmani layaḥ puruṣe laya-dvārā, avyaktam akṣare līyate akṣaraṁ tamasi līyate tamaḥ pare deva ekībhavati iti śruteḥ ||39||



**śrīdharaḥ : **paramātmani puruṣottame līyate līnāvatiṣṭhate ||39||



**paramātmā ca sarveṣām ādhāraḥ parameśvaraḥ | **

**viṣṇu-nāmā sa vedeṣu vedānteṣu ca gīyate ||40||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **viṣṇu-nāmā sa vedeṣu vedānteṣu ca gīyate | viṣṇu-nāmā sa eva pūrvata evaśarīro vedeṣu vedānteṣu ca sad-brahmādi-śabdair gīyate ||40||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tasya tu nāsti laya ity āha—paramātmeti | sarveṣām ādhāraḥ tasmāt sa eva parama īśvaraḥ puruṣottama ity arthaḥ ||40||



**pravṛttaṁ ca nivṛttaṁ ca dvividhaṁ karma vaidikam |**

**tābhyām ubhābhyām puruṣaiḥ sarva-mūrtiḥ sa ijyate ||41||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **katham indrādi-yāgair asyejyatvam ity atrāha—sarva-mūrtir iti ||41||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tat prāpty-artham eva sarva-sādhana-jātam ity āha—pravṛttaṁ ceti ||41||



**ṛg-yajuḥ-sāmabhir mārgaiḥ pravṛttair ijyate hy asau |**

**yajñeśvaro yajña-pumān puruṣaiḥ puruṣottamaḥ ||42||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kaiḥ katham ity ata ity atrāha—ṛg ity ādi dvābhyām | pravṛttair aviraktaiḥ puruṣaiḥ ṛg-vedādi-vihitaiḥ karmabhir mārga-bhūtair ijyate ||42||



**jñānātmā jñāna-yogena jñāna-mūrtiḥ sa cejyate |**

**nivṛtte yogibhir mārge viṣṇur mukti-phala-pradaḥ ||43||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **jñānātmā jñāna-svarūpaḥ jñāna-mūrtiḥ jñānātmikā mūrtir vigraho yasya | nivṛtte mārge jñāna-yogena jñāna-yoga-pradhānena karmaṇejyate mukti-phala-pradaḥ nivṛtti-mārgeṇeṣṭa eva ||43||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yogibhiḥ karmabhir viśuddha-cittaiḥ nivṛtte mārge sthitair iti śeṣaḥ | jñāna-yogenejyata ity arthaḥ ||43||



**hrasva-dīrgha-plutair yat tu kiñcid vastv abhidhīyate |**

**yac ca vācām aviṣayaṁ tat sarvaṁ viṣṇur avyayaḥ ||44||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **hrasvādi-śabdair abhidheyam acid-vastu vācām aviṣayaṁ cid-vastu tat sarvaṁ viṣṇuḥ tad-ātmakam ||44||



**śrīdharaḥ : **jñāna-yoga-svarūpam āha—hrasva-dīrghety-ādi dvābhyām ||44||



**vyaktaḥ sa eva vāvyaktaḥ sa eva puruṣo’vyayaḥ |**

**paramātmā ca viśvātmā viśva-rūpa-dharo hariḥ ||45||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **vyaktādi-sāmānādhikaraṇya-hetur viśvātmā viśva-rūpa-dhara iti puruṣaḥ kārya-kāraṇa-rūpobhayāvasthaḥ paramātmā muktaḥ | vyaktaṁ sa eva cāvyaktam iti ca pāṭhaḥ ||45||



**vyaktāvyaktātmikā tasmin prakṛtiḥ sampralīyate |**

**puruṣaś cāpi maitreya vyāpiny avyāhatātmani ||46||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **uktasyaivānuvādo guṇāntara-vidhy-arthaḥ | avyāhṛtātmani avikṛta-svarūpe ||46||



**śrīdharaḥ : **sa sarvaṁ viṣṇur eva na tu tasmād vyatiriktam astīty atra hetum āha—vyaktāvyaktātmiketi ||46||



**dviparārdhātmakaḥ kālaḥ kathito yo mayā tava |**

**tad ahas tasya maitreya viṣṇor īśasya kathyate ||47||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **viṣṇoḥ sarvotkarṣa-pratipatty-arthaṁ sarvātiśāyinīm aho-rātra-kalpanām āha—dviparārdhātmaka ity ādi dvābhyām ||47||



**vyakte ca prakṛtau līne prakṛtyāṁ puruṣe tathā |**

**tatra sthite niśā cāsya tat-pramāṇā mahā-mune ||48||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **prakṛtyāṁ puruṣe līnāyām iti śeṣaḥ | tathā tatra sthite tathā-bhūte puruṣe tatra paramātmani sthite dvayor yugapal laya-pakṣe granthaḥ sugamaḥ | vyakta iti punar layānuvādaḥ paramātmano rātry-ādi-kalpanā-vidhy-arthaḥ ||48||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tathā tatra puruṣe parameśvare sthite sati prakṛtyāṁ ca tatra sthitāyām ity arthaḥ ||48||



**naivāhas tasya na niśā nityasya paramātmaḥ |**

**upacāras tathāpy eṣa tasyeśasya dvijocyate ||49||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **nityasya paramātmanaḥ iti atra svarūpa-nityatvasya brahmādīnām api sādhāraṇyād vigrahavattvasya nityatvam abhipretam, sadaika-rūpa-rūpāya ity ādibhir vigraha-nityatvasya pratipādanāt ||49||



**śrīdharaḥ : **etac ca na vāstavam ity āha—naiveti | upacāraḥ sarvotkarṣa-pratipattaye ucyate kriyate ity arthaḥ ||49||



**ity eṣa tava maitreya kathitaḥ prākṛto layaḥ |**

**ātyantikam atho brahman nibodha pratisañcaram ||50||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **prākṛtaṁ layam upasaṁharan ātyantikaṁ layam upakṣipati—itīti ||50||



iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe ṣaṣṭhe’ṁśe caturtho’dhyāyaḥ



—o\)0\(o—



\(6.5\)





## ādhyātmikādi-trividha-tāpa-varṇanam, bhagavān vāsudevaś ceti śabda-dvayasya vyākhyā, bhagavataḥ pāramārthika-svarūpa-varṇanaṁ ca



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**ādhyātmikādi maitreya jñātvā tāpa-trayaṁ budhaḥ |**

**utpanna-jñāna-vairāgyaḥ prāpnoty ātyantikaṁ layam ||1||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **ātyantika-layo nāma sarvātmanaḥ ajñāna-tat-kārya-nāśātmako mokṣaḥ ātmānaṁ deha-sandhānaṁ ca nimittīkṛtya bhavatīty-ādhyātmikaḥ ||1||



**ādhyātmiko’pi dvividhaḥ śārīro mānasas tathā |**

**śārīro bahubhir bhedair bhidyate śrūyatāṁ ca saḥ ||2||**



śrīdharaḥ :



**śiro-roga-pratiśyāya-jvara-śūlabhagandaraiḥ |**

**gulmārśaḥ-śvayathu-śvāsa-cchardyādibhir anekadhā ||3||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ, śrīdharaḥ : **pratiśyāyaḥ pīnasaḥ | śvayathuḥ śophaḥ864 ||3||



**tathākṣi-rogātīsāra-kuṣṭhāṅgāmaya-saṁjñitaiḥ |**

**bhidyate dehajas tāpo mānasaṁ śrotum arhasi ||4||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **aṅgāmayo vāta-rogādiḥ ||4||



**kāma-krodha-bhaya-dveṣa-lobha-moha-viṣādajaḥ |**

**śokāsūyāvamānerṣyā-mātsaryādi-mayas tathā ||5||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **dveṣaḥ aprītiḥ | moho mūrcchā | viṣādaḥ sattva-saṅkṣayaḥ | śokaḥ priya-virahajaḥ | īrṣyā para-sampad-akṣamā ||5||



**śrīdharaḥ : **viṣādo duḥkham | śoko'nuśocanam | asūyā guṇeṣu doṣāropaḥ | īrṣyā kṣamā-rāhityam | mātsaryaṁ parotkarṣāsahiṣṇutvam asahanam ||5||



**mānaso’pi dvija-śreṣṭha tāpo bhavati naikadhā |**

**ity evam ādibhir bhedais tāpo hy ādhyātmikaḥ smṛtaḥ ||6||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**mṛga-pakṣi-manuṣyādyaiḥ piśācoraga-rākṣasaiḥ |**

**sarīsṛpādyaiś ca nṛṇāṁ jāyate cādhibhautikaḥ ||7||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhūtāni nimittatvenādhikṛtya bhavatīty ādhibhautikaḥ, tam āha—mṛgeti | mṛgādibhiḥ yo jāyate sa ādhibhautikaḥ ||7||



**śīta-vātoṣṇa-varṣāmbu-vaidyutādi-samudbhavaḥ |**

**tāpo dvija-vara śreṣṭhaiḥ kathyate cādhidaivikaḥ ||8||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kevalaṁ daivam evādhikṛtya bhavatīty ādhidaivikaḥ | tam āha—śīta-vāteti ||8||



**garbha-janma-jarājñāna-mṛtyu-nārakajaṁ tathā |**

**duḥkhaṁ sahasraśo bhedair bhidyate muni-sattama ||9||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **nārakajaṁ narakajaṁ, syān nārakas tu narakaḥ ity amaraḥ ||9||



**śrīdharaḥ : **etad eva tāpa-trayam āgarbhādy-avasthā-bhedena sahasraśaḥ prapañcayati—garbhety-ādinā | iti saṁsāra-duḥkhārka- \[6.5.57\] ity ataḥ prāktanena granthena ||9||



**sukumāra-tanur garbhe jantur bahumalāvṛte |**

**ulba-saṁveṣṭito bhugna-pṛṣṭha-grīvāsthi-saṁhatiḥ ||10||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ulbaṁ garbha-veṣṭana-carma ||10||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tatra garbha-duḥkham āha—sukumārety-ādi caturbhiḥ | ulbaṁ garbha-veṣṭana-māṁsaṁ bhugnaṁ cakrī-bhūtaṁ pṛṣṭhādi yasya saḥ ||10||



**atyamla-kaṭu-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-lavaṇair mātṛ-bhojanaiḥ |**

**atyanta-tāpair aty arthaṁ vardhamānātivedanaḥ ||11||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **atyantam amlādibhir vardhamānā ativedanā yasya ||11||



**prasāraṇākuñcanādau nāṅgānāṁ prabhur ātmanaḥ |**

**śakṛn-mūtra-mahā-paṅka-śāyī sarvatra pīḍitaḥ ||12||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **aṅgānām ātmano'ṅgānāṁ prasaraṇādau na prabhuḥ asamarthaḥ ||12||



**nirucchvāsaḥ sa-caitanyaḥ smarañ janma-śatāny atha |**

**āste garbhe’tiduḥkhena nija-karma-nibandhanaḥ ||13||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**jāyamānaḥ puīrṣāsṛṅ-mūtra-śukrāvilānanaḥ |**

**prājāpatyena vātena pīḍyamānāsthi-bandhanaḥ ||14||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **prājāpatyena brahmaṇā niyuktena gātra-saṅkocakena, tasmāj jyāyān sagarbhaḥ kanīyāṁsaṁ sūti-yonim ajānāno hinasti brahmaṇā hi sakṛtaḥ iti śruteḥ ||14||



**śrīdharaḥ : **janma-duḥkham āha—jāyamāna ity-ādi dvābhyām | purīṣādibhir āvilaṁ klinnam ānanaṁ yasya saḥ prājāpatyena prajāpati-yuktena garbha-saṅkocena, tasmāj jyāyān sagarbhaḥ kanīyāṁsaṁ sūti-yonim ajānāno hinasti brahmaṇā hi sakṛtaḥ iti śruteḥ ||14||



**adho-mukho vai kriyate prabalaiḥ sūti-mārutaiḥ |**

**kleśān niṣkrāntim āpnoti jaṭhārān mātur āturaḥ ||15||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ, śrīdharaḥ : **sūti-mārutaiḥ sūty-arthaṁ garbha-prerakaiḥ ||15||



**mūrcchām avāpya mahatīṁ saṁspṛṣṭo bāhya-vāyunā |**

**vijñāna-bhraṁśam āpnoti jātaś ca muni-sattama ||16||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **janmāntara-duḥkham āha—mūrcchām ity ādi caturbhiḥ ||16||



**kaṇṭakair iva tunnāṅgaḥ krakacair iva dāritaḥ |**

**pūti-vraṇān nipatito dharaṇyāṁ krimiko yathā ||17||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tunnāṅgaḥ vyathita-dehaḥ | pūti-vraṇāt durgandha-vraṇāt yoner ity arthaḥ ||17||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tunnāṅgaḥ vyathita-gātraḥ | krakacaiḥ dāraṇa-yantraiḥ | pūti-vraṇād durgandha-vraṇa-tulyād yoneḥ ||17||



**kaṇḍūyane’pi cāśaktaḥ parivarte’py anīśvaraḥ |**

**snāna-pānādikāhāram apy āpnoti parecchayā ||18||**

**aśuci-prastare suptaḥ kīṭa-daṁśādibhis tathā |**

**bhakṣyamāṇo’pi naivaiṣāṁ samartho vinivāraṇe ||19||**



\(18-19\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**janma-duḥkhāny anekāni janmano’nantarāṇi ca |**

**bāla-bhāve yad āpnoti hy ādhibhautādikāni ca ||20||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **kaṇḍūyanenety-ādinoktāni janmano'nantarāṇi kīṭa-daṁśādibhiḥ bāla-bhāve yad āpnoti tad apy anekam iti śeṣaḥ ||20||



**ajñāna-tamasācchanno mūḍhāntaḥ-karaṇo naraḥ |**

**na jānāti kutaḥ ko’haṁ kvāhaṁ gantā kim ātmanaḥ ||21||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **kāmāndhatvād ādhikyād yauvane ajñānajaṁ duḥkhaṁ viśiṣyāha—ajñānety-ādinā ||21||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yauvana-duḥkhāny āha—ajñānety-ādi caturbhiḥ | ajñānam iha kāma-mohādy-abhiniveśaḥ, tena tamasā channaḥ andhībhūtaḥ | kāryākārye laukike kartavyākartavye vaidike ||21||



**kena bandhena baddho’haṁ kāraṇaṁ kim akāraṇam |**

**kiṁ kāryaṁ kim akāryaṁ vā kiṁ vācyaṁ kiṁ ca nocyate ||22||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **kāryaṁ kāraṇa-janyam ||22||



**ko dharmaḥ kaś ca vādharmaḥ kasmin varte’tha vā katham |**

**kiṁ kartavyam akartavyam kiṁ vā kiṁ guṇa-doṣavat ||23||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ko vā kasmin vā varte tat sarvaṁ ca katham iti na jānātīti pūrveṇānvayaḥ ||23||



**evaṁ paśu-samair mūḍhair ajñāna-prabhavaṁ mahat |**

**avāpyate narair duḥkhaṁ śiśnodara-parāyaṇaiḥ ||24||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**ajñānaṁ tāmaso bhāvaḥ kāryārambha-pravṛttayaḥ |**

**ajñānināṁ pravartante karma-lopās tato dvija ||25||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ajñānaṁ tamaso vikāraḥ, tenājñānināṁ tad-anuguṇa-kāryārambheṣu pravṛttayo bhavanti | ato vaidika-karma lopāḥ pravartante ||25||



**śrīdharaḥ : **ajñāna-svarūpaṁ tat-phalaṁ ca darśayati—ajñānam ity ādi dvābhyām | ajñānaṁ tamaso bhāvaḥ, yato jñānināṁ vihiteṣv api kāryārambheṣv apravṛttayo nihita-kāryārambheṣu pravṛttayaś ca syus tataḥ karma-lopāḥ pravartante ||25||



**narakaṁ karmaṇāṁ lopāt phalam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ |**

**tasmād ajñānināṁ duḥkham iha cāmutra cottamam ||26||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **tataḥ karma-lopāt naraka-prāptir iti uttamam adhikaṁ duḥkham ||26||



**jarā-jarjara-dehaś ca śithilāvayavaḥ pumān |**

**vigalac chīrṇa-daśano bali-snāyu-śirāvṛtaḥ ||27||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **balisnāyuśirāvṛta iti balis tvak-taraṅgaḥ rakta-vahā nāḍī sirā saiva bandhanī snāyuḥ ||27||



**śrīdharaḥ : **sthāvira-duḥkhāny āha—jarā-jarjarety-ādibhiḥ | baliḥ lambamāna-tvak-śirā-rakta-vasādiḥ saiva snāyuḥ asthi-bandhanī ||27||



**dūra-praṇaṣṭa-nayano vyomāntar-gata-tārakaḥ |**

**nāsāvivara-niryāta-loma-puñjaś calad-vapuḥ ||28||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **dūra-praṇaṣṭa-nayanaḥ adhika-praṇaṣṭa-nayana-śaktiḥ | vyomāntargata-tārakaḥ dṛg-golakākāśā-nimagna-kanīnakaḥ ||28||



**śrīdharaḥ : **dūre dūrasthe arthe praṇaṣṭaṁ nayanaṁ grahaṇāsamarthaṁ cakṣur yasya sa vyomni cakṣur-golākāśe antar-gate tārake kanīnike yasya saḥ ||28||



**prakaṭī-bhūta-sarvāsthir nata-pṛṣṭhāsthi-saṁhatiḥ |**

**utsanna-jaṭharāgnitvād alpāhāro’lpa-ceṣṭitaḥ ||29||**

**kṛcchrāc caṅkramaṇotthāna-śayanāsana-ceṣṭitaḥ |**

**mandībhavac-chrotra-netraḥ sraval-lālāvilānanaḥ ||30||**



\(29-30\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**anāyattaiḥ samastaiś ca karaṇair maraṇonmukhaḥ |**

**tat-kṣaṇe’py anubhūtānām asmartākhila-vastunām ||31||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **anāyattaiḥ pravṛtty-akṣamaiḥ ||31||



**śrīdharaḥ : **anāyattaiḥ asvādhīnaiḥ karaṇaiḥ ||31||



**sakṛd uccārite vākye samudbhūta-mahāśramaḥ |**

**śvāsa-kāśa-samudbhūta-mahāyāsa-prajāgaraḥ ||32||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **kāśaḥ śleṣmā ||32||



**anyenotthāpyate’nyena tathā saṁveśyate jarī |**

**bhṛtyātma-putra-dārāṇām avamānāspadīkṛtaḥ ||33||**

**prakṣīṇākhila-śaucaś ca vihārāhāra-saspṛhaḥ |**

**hāsyaḥ parijanasyāpi nirviṇṇāśeṣa-bāndhavaḥ ||34||**



\(33-34\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**anubhūtam ivānyasmin janmany ātma-viceṣṭitam |**

**saṁsmaran yauvane dīrghaṁ niḥśvasaty abhitāpitaḥ ||35||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **yauvane yad ātmanaḥ vividhaṁ ceṣṭitaṁ tad anyajanmānubhūtam iva saṁsmaran dīrgha-śvāsaṁ muñcati ||35||



**evam ādīni duḥkhāni jarāyām anubhūya vai |**

**maraṇe yāni duḥkhāni prāpnoti śṛṇu tāny api ||36||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**ślathad-grīvāṅghri-hasto’tha vyāpto vepathunā bhṛśam |**

**muhur glāni-paravaśo muhur jñāna-lavānvitaḥ ||37||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **maraṇa-duḥkhāny āha—ślathad-grīvety-ādi sārdhaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ | vepathunā kampena ||37||



**hiraṇya-dhānya-tanaya-bhāryā-bhṛtya-gṛhādiṣu |**

**ete kathaṁ bhaviṣyantīty atīva-mamatākulaḥ ||38||**

**marma-bhidbhir mahā-rogaiḥ krakacair iva dāruṇaiḥ |**

**śarair ivāntakasyograiś chidyamānāsu-bandhanaḥ ||39||**



\(38-39\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**parivartitārākṣo hasta-pādaṁ muhuḥ kṣipan |**

**saṁśuṣyamānatālvoṣṭha-puṭo ghuraghurāyate ||40||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **ghuraghurāyate ghuraghura ity eva śabdaṁ karoti ||40||



**niruddha-kaṇṭho doṣaughair udāna-śvāsa-pīḍitaḥ |**

**tāpena mahatā vyāptas tṛṣā cārtas tathā kṣudhā ||41||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **doṣo vātādiḥ | 



uraḥ sthānam udānasya nāsā-nābhi-galāṁś caret |

vāk-pravṛtti-prayatnorjā bala-varṇa-smṛti-kriyaḥ || 



asya gala-sañcāritvāt udānaḥ kaṇṭha-deśa-sthaḥ ity amaraḥ ||41||



**śrīdharaḥ : **doṣoghaiḥ śleṣma-saṅghaiḥ niruddhaḥ kaṇṭho yasya saḥ | ata eva ghuraghurāyata iti pūrveṇānvayaḥ ||41||



**kleśād utkrāntim āpnoti yama-kiṅkara-pīḍitaḥ |**

**tataś ca yātanādehaṁ kleśena pratipadyate ||42||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **yātanādehaṁ yatanārtham anya-deha-grahaṇam ||42||



**etāny anyāni cāgrāṇi duḥkhāni maraṇe nṛṇām |**

**śṛṇuṣva narake yāni prāpyante puruṣair mṛtaiḥ ||43||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **naraka-duḥkhāny āha—śṛṇuṣvety-ādi sārdhaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ ||43||



**yāmya-kiṅkara-pāśādi-grahaṇaṁ daṇḍa-tāraṇam |**

**yamasya darśanaṁ cogram ugra-mārga-vilokanam ||44||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **yāmya-kiṅkaraiḥ pāśādibhir grahaṇam ||44||



**karambha-bālukā-vahni-yantra-śastrādi-bhīṣaṇe |**

**pratyekaṁ narake yāś ca yātanā dvija duḥsahāḥ ||45||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **bhajyamāna-karambha-sama-bālukā karambhādi-bhīṣaṇa-vastubhir yutā yātanā duḥsahā ||45||



**śrīdharaḥ : **karambha-bālukā tapta-bālukā ||45||



**krakacaiḥ pāṭhyamānānāṁ mūṣāyāṁ cāpi dahyatām |**

**kuṭhāraiḥ kṛtyamānānāṁ bhūmau cāpi nikhanyatām ||46||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **dahyatāṁ khanyatām ity ādi parasmaipadam ārṣam | kṛtyamānānāṁ chidyamānānām ||46||



**śūleṣv āropyamāṇānāṁ vyāghra-vaktre praveśyatām |**

**gṛdhraiḥ sambhakṣyamāṇānāṁ dvīpibhiś copabhujyatām ||47||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **dvīpibhir vyāghraiḥ ||47||



**kvāthyatāṁ taila-madhye ca klidyatāṁ kṣāra-kardame |**

**uccān nipātyamānānāṁ kṣipyatāṁ kṣepa-yantrakaiḥ ||48||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**narake yāni duḥkhāni pāpa-hetūdbhavāni vai |**

**prāpyante nārakair vipra teṣāṁ saṅkhyā na vidyate ||49||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **pāpam eva hetuḥ, tad-udbhavāni ||49||



**ne kevalaṁ dvija-śreṣṭha narake duḥkha-paddhatiḥ |**

**svarge’pi pāta-bhītasya kṣayiṣṇor nāsti nirvṛtiḥ ||50||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **svarge’pi duḥkham evāha—na kevalam iti | svarge’pi nirvṛtir nāsti duḥkha-paddhatir evāstīty arthaḥ ||50||



**punaś ca garbhe bhavati jāyate ca punaḥ punaḥ |**

**garbhe vilīyate bhūyo jāyamāno’stam eti vai ||51||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **svarga-naraka-bhogānantaraṁ punar garbhādi-duḥkham āha—punaś cety -ādi ṣaḍbhiḥ ||51||



**jāta-mātraś ca mriyate bāla-bhāve’tha yauvane |**

**madhyamaṁ vā vayaḥ prāpya vārdhake vātha vā mṛtiḥ ||52||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**yāvaj jīvati tāvac ca duḥkhair nānā-vidhaiḥ plutaḥ |**

**tantu-kāraṇa-plakṣmaughair āste kārpāsa-bījavat ||53||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tantu-kāraṇeti | pakṣmāṇi aṁśavaḥ ||53||



**śrīdharaḥ : **duḥkhaiḥ pluto vyāptaḥ āste tantūnāṁ karmaṁ pakṣmāṇi aṁśavaḥ teṣām oghaiḥ samūhaiḥ kārpāsa-bījaṁ yathā vyāptaṁ tadvat ||53||



**dravya-nāśe tathotpattau pālane ca sadā nṛṇām |**

**bhavanty aneka-duḥkhāni tathaiveṣṭa-vipattiṣu ||54||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **utpattau dravyasyārjane ||54||



**yad yat prīti-karaṁ puṁsāṁ vastu maitreya jāyate |**

**tad eva duḥkha-vṛkṣasya bījatvam upagacchati ||55||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**kalatra-putra-mitrārtha-gṛha-kṣetra-dhanādikaiḥ |**

**kriyeta na tathā bhūri sukhaṁ puṁsāṁ yathā’sukham ||56||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **asukhaṁ duḥkham ||56||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kalatrādikair yathā asukhaṁ bhūri kriyate na tathā sukhaṁ kriyate ||56||



**iti saṁsāra-duḥkhārka-tāpa-tāpita-cetasām |**

**vimukti-pādapa-cchāyāmṛte kutra sukhaṁ nṛṇām ||57||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **evaṁ duḥkhānusandhāna-labdha-viveka-vairāgyasya puṁso mumukṣaiva yuktety-āśayenāha—itīty-ādi caturbhiḥ ||57||



**tad asya trividhasyāpi duḥkha-jātasya vai mama |**

**garbha-janma-jarādyeṣu sthāneṣu prabhaviṣyataḥ ||58||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **garbhādi-sthāneṣu prakarṣeṇa bhaviṣyato duḥkha-jātasya bhagavat-prāptir eva mama matā sammatety uttaratrānvayaḥ ||58||



**nirastātiśayāhlāda-sukha-bhāvaika-lakṣaṇā |**

**bheṣajaṁ bhagavat-prāptir ekāntātyantikī matā ||59||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **sukhāntarasyātiśayo nirasto yena tan-nirastātiśayam āhlāda-rūpaṁ sukham | āhlāda-sukham āhlādo moha-sambhedaḥ sukhāntarānubhavākṣamatvāpādakotkarṣavat sukham | bhāva-śabdena sukhasya duḥkha-nivṛtti-rūpatā vyāvartyate |evaṁ niratiśayāhlāda-rūpa-sukhatvam eva bhagavat-prāpti-svarūpam ity uktam | ekāntā duḥkhāsambhinnā ātyantikī antam atītya vartamānā nityā | atra bhagavac-chabdena prāpyasya heya-pratyanīkāśeṣa-kalyāṇa-guṇātmakatvaṁ vakṣyamāṇaṁ sūcayatā tat-prāpter nirastātiśety-ādy ucyamānaṁ vaiśiṣṭyaṁ pratipāditam ||59||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kathaṁ-bhūtā tat-prāptiḥ ? tad āha—nirastātiśayeti | nirastātiśayaḥ āhlādo nirvṛtir yasmin sukhe tad-bhāvas tad-ātmatvam eva ekaṁ lakṣaṇaṁ yasyāḥ sā tathā | kiṁ ca, ekāntā bhagavan-niṣṭhā-mātreṇāvaśyambhāvinī na tu ṛtvig-ādi-vaiguṇyena karma-phalavad anityā | ātyantikī antam atītya vartamānā ||59|| 



**tasmāt tat-prāptaye yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ paṇḍitair naraiḥ |**

**tat-prāpti-hetur jñānaṁ ca karma coktaṁ mahā-mune ||60||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **yasmād bhagavat-prāptir eva tāpa-traya-nivṛtti-hetuḥ, tasmāt tat-prāptaye yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ iti buddheḥ kṣema-prāpaṇam iti mokṣopāya-jñānam abhidheyam iti vadato nirasyati prāpty-upāyaṁ ca darśayati | jñānaṁ ca karma ceti | atra jñānam eva sākṣāt prāpty-upāyaḥ karma tu tad-aṅgatvena na tu viparyayaḥ samuccayo vā, brahma-vidyām adhiṣṭhāya iyāya so'pi subahūn \[vi.pu. 6.6.12\] iti hi vakṣyati ||60||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tat-prāpty-upāyam āha—tad iti | atas tat-prāpty-upāyaḥ karma-citta-śuddhi-dvārā tad-aṅgatvena, jñānaṁ tu sākṣāt ||60||



**āgamotthaṁ vivekāc ca dvidhā jñānaṁ tathocyate865| **

**śabda-brahmāgama-mayaṁ paraṁ brahma vivekajam ||61||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : ācāre karma-svarūpam uktam | jñānaṁ dvidhā vibhajya darśayati—āgamottham iti | vivekajaṁ vivekād yogāj janyam | tatrāgamotthaṁ jñānaṁ śabda-brahmeti vivekajaṁ para-brahmeti ca manvādibhir ucyata ity āha—śabda-brahmeti ||61||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tatra dvividham āha—āgameti | tad vivṛṇoti—śabda-brahmeti | āgama-mayam āgamotthaṁ jñānaṁ śabda-brahma-śabdāt, satyaṁ jñānam anantaṁ brahma iti vākyāj jñāyamānaṁ śabda-śravaṇaṁ jñānam āgamottham ity arthaḥ | dehādi-viviktāvikārād citta-vṛttyā nididhyāsanākhyayā prakāśamānaṁ paraṁ brahma vivekajaṁ jñānam ity arthaḥ | vṛtti-vyaktasya brahmaṇa eva jñānābhidhānatvād brahma-jñānam ity uktam ||61||



**andhaṁ tama ivājñānaṁ dīpavac cendriyodbhavam |**

**yathā sūryas tathā jñānaṁ yad viprarṣe vivekajam ||62||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **atha brahma-viṣayam idaṁ jñāna-dvayaṁ praśaṁsati kudṛṣṭi-nirasanāya tasya jñāna-dvayasya vaiṣamyaṁ ca darśayati—andhaṁ tama iti | ajñānam āgama-śravaṇāt pūrvam | ātmanām avidyākhya-karma-tirohita-svarūpatvād ātma-paramātma-yāthātmyasyāparijñānam | anyathājñānaṁ vā | tac ca jñāna-virodhitvād andhaṁ tama iva āgama-janyaṁ jñānaṁ śrotrendriya-gṛhītāgama-janyatvād indriyodbhavam ity ucyate | tac cājñāna-tamo-virodhitvād dīpavad iti | ataḥ āgamotthaṁ jñānaṁ tamasi dīpavad anyathā-jñāna-saṁvalitam alpam ca | atha ajñāna-tan-mūlāvidyā-rūpa-sarva-tamo-nirasanatvāt āgamotthād api viśadatama-pratyakṣa-rūpatvāc ca vivekajaṁ sūryavad ity ucyate ||62|| 



**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu śabda-śravaṇād api brahma-jñānam evotpadyate tenaivājñāna-nivṛttyā bhagavat-prāpti-siddheḥ kiṁ viveka-janya-jñānenety āśaṅkyāha—andhaṁ niviḍaṁ tama ivājñānaṁ vyāpakam ivāvaraṇaṁ śrotrendriya-grāhya-śabdādi-dvārā janyaṁ jñānaṁ dīpavat asambhāvanādy-abhibhūtaṁ na sarvātmanā ajñāna-nivartakaṁ vivekajaṁ tu jñānaṁ sūryavat sarvājñāna-nivartakam ity arthaḥ ||62||



**manur apy āha vedārthaṁ smṛtvā yan muni-sattama |**

**tad etac chrūyatām atra sambandhe gadato mama ||63||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ukte'rthe manu-vacanaṁ pramāṇayati—manur apīti | atra sambandhe mokṣa-tat-sādhana-sambandhe ||63||



**śrīdharaḥ : **ukta-lakṣaṇe jñāna-dvaye manu-sammatim āha—manur apīty-ādi dvābhyām | atra sambandhe asmin prasaṅge ||63||



**dve brahmaṇī veditavye śabda-brahma paraṁ ca yat |**

**śabda-brahmaṇi niṣṇātaḥ paraṁ brahmādhigacchati ||64||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **vidyātaḥ puruṣārtho na karmaṇa iti manu-vacanam evodāharati—dve iti | paraṁ ca yat brahmeti śeṣaḥ | śabda-brahmaṇi śāstra-janya-jñāne niṣṇātaḥ nipuṇaḥ paraṁ brahma pratyakṣa-rūpaṁ vivekajaṁ jñānaṁ labhate ||64||



**śrīdharaḥ : **śabda-brahmaṇi niṣṇātaḥ vivekajena paraṁ brahma adhigacchati prāpnoti ||64||



**dve vai vidye veditavye iti cātharvaṇī śrutiḥ |**

**parayā tv akṣara-prāptir ṛg-vedādi-mayāparā ||65||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **manu-vacana-mūla-śrutim udāharati—dve vidye iti | vidye āgama-vivekotthe parayā vivekotthayā akṣarasya para-brahmaṇaḥ prāptir yathā tad akṣaram adhigamyate iti śruteḥ | anena vākyārtha-jñānāt karmaṇo vā mokṣaṁ vadanto nirastāḥ | vākyārtha-jñānān mokṣaṁ vadataḥ, tac chāstrair vipratiṣiddhaṁ buddheś ceti kṣema-prāpaṇam ihaiva na duḥkham upalabheta iti sūtra-virodhaḥ pratyakṣa-virodhaś ca | atra prakaraṇe svoktasyārthasya vedavid-agresara-manu-vacana-prāmāṇikād āgama-vivekaja-padayor ekāyanādy-ukto'rtho na vivakṣita iti veditavyam ||65||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tat-prāpti-hetuḥ jñānaṁ ca karma coktam ity atra śruti-sammatim āha—dve vidye iti | vidyā-śabdena tad-dhetu-karma brahma-viṣayau veda-bhāgau gṛhīte | tad āha—parayeti | akṣara-pratipādaka-parākhya-veda-bhāgād itaraḥ karma-bhāgaḥ ṛg-vedādi-śabdenocyate | brāhmaṇa-parivrājakādivat sā tv aparā sānana-viṣayatvāt ||65||



**yat tad avyaktam ajaram acintyam ajam akṣayam |**

**anirdeśyam arūpaṁ ca pāṇi-pādādy-asaṁyutam ||66||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **atha para-vidyopāsyasya prāpya-bhūtasya brahmaṇaḥ svarūpam āha—yat tad iti | yathāha śrutiḥ—yakṣad adṛśyam ity ādinā śruti-vyatiriktaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ na vyajata iti avyaktam | vedāham etaṁ nāvedavin manute taṁ bṛhantam iti ajaram ajam ity ādinā ṣad-bhāva-vikāra-rāhityam uktam | acintyam anirdeśyam iti vāṅ-mānasāgocaratvam | arūpaṁ deva-manuṣyādi-rūpa-rahitam | anyathā rūpavattva-śruty-ādi-virodhāt ||66||



**śrīdharaḥ : **atha parā sā yayā tad akṣaram adhigamyate | yat tad adṛśyam agrāhyam ity ādy ātharvaṇa-śruty-uktaṁ para-vidyā-viṣayam akṣarākhyaṁ paraṁ tattvam āha—yat tad ity-ādi tribhiḥ ||66||



**vibhu sarva-gataṁ nityaṁ bhūta-yonim akāraṇam |**

**vyāpy-avyāptaṁ yataḥ sarvaṁ tad vai paśyanti sūrayaḥ ||67||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **vibhu sarva-gataṁ vitatya vyāpi vibhutvam iyantṛtvaṁ vā akāraṇaṁ svayaṁ kāraṇa-rahitaṁ vyāpya-vyāpaka-rūpeṇāvasthitaṁ sarvaṁ jagad yataḥ bhūta-yonir iti jīvābhiprāyam atra para-vidyā-viṣayasyākṣarasya bhūtayonitva-vibhutvādi-viśeṣaṇaiḥ para-vidyā nirguṇa-brahma-viṣayety etan nirastaṁ, yad vai paśyanti sadā paśyanti iti śruteḥ ||67||



**śrīdharaḥ : **vibhu prabhu | sarva-gatam anavacchinnaṁ vyāpi sarva-kāryānugatam | avyāptaṁ svayam anyenāvyāptam | yataḥ sarvaṁ bhavati ||67||



**tad brahma paramaṁ dhāma tad dhyeyaṁ mokṣa-kāṅkṣiṇām |**

**śruti-vākyoditaṁ sūkṣmaṁ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṁ padam ||68||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **dhāma tejo-mayaṁ, tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṁ padam iti śruti-vākyoditaṁ sūkṣmaṁ tat-paraṁ brahma mokṣa-kāṅkṣibhir dhyeyam ||68||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tat-paraṁ brahmaiva svecchaāviṣkṛta-ṣāḍguṇyaṁ parameśvarākhyam ||68||



**tad etad bhagavad-vācyaṁ svarūpaṁ paramātmanaḥ |**

**vācako bhagavac-chabdas tasyādy asyākṣarātmanaḥ ||69||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ukta-guṇa-viśiṣṭaṁ tad eva brahma bhagavac-chabda-vācyam ity āha—tad eveti | idaṁ vacanaṁ dhyāna-kriyābhyāṁ, bhagavān sarva-vyāpī ca bhagavān nārāyaṇo bhagavān prajāpatiḥ | vāsudevāya dhīmahi | om ity ātmānaṁ yuñjīta | namo rucāya brāhmaye ity ādi vedānta-sāroddhāra-rūpaṁ dvādaśākṣara-cintakā itipūrvam uktaṁ mantra-viśeṣam abhipretyābhihitam | sakala-heya-pratyanīka-kalyāṇa-guṇātmakaṁ jagat-kāraṇaṁ para-vidyādhigamyam uktaṁ para-brahmaiva bhagavac-chabda-vācyaṁ nānyad ity avadhārayati tad eveti | manur api tataḥ svayaṁ-bhūr bhagavān ity ādinā jagat-kāraṇam eva bhagavac-chabda-vācyam ity āha—atha brahmaṇaḥ svarūpa-rūpa-guṇa-vibhavair anantasya yāthātmya-vacana-samartho'yaṁ śabda ity āha—vācaka iti ||69||



**śrīdharaḥ : **dvādaśākṣarādi-para-vidyopāsanayā bhaktaiḥ sulabha-dṛśyaṁ bhagavac-chabda-vācyaṁ tad evety āha—tad eveti ||69||



**evaṁ nigaditārthasya sa-tattvaṁ tasya tattvataḥ |**

**jñāyate yena tat jñānaṁ param anyat trayī-mayam ||70||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **evaṁ bhagavac-chabdenābhihitasya nigadita-bhūtayonitvādy-arthasya tasya brahmaṇas tattvaṁ svarūpaṁ yena vivekaja-jñānena tattvato yad jñāyate dṛśyate tat puṣkala-sākṣātkāra-rūpa param anyad uddeśataḥ śāstrajaṁ parokṣa-rūpam aparam ity upasaṁharati ||70||



**śrīdharaḥ : **īdṛg-viṣayaṁ ca jñānaṁ para-vidyety āha—evam iti | nigaditārthasya dvādaśākṣarādibhir uktārthasyeśvarasya tattvaṁ svarūpaṁ tattvataḥ apracyuta-brahma-svarūpeṇa yena dvādaśākṣarādinā jñāyate tat paraṁ jñānaṁ parā vidyā trayī-mayaṁ tv anyat aparā vidyā karmākhyā ||70||



**aśabda-gocarasyāpi tasyaiva brahmaṇo dvija |**

**pūjāyāṁ bhagavac-chabdaḥ kriyate hy aupacārikaḥ ||71||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **sarva-kāraṇe pare brahmaṇi bhagavac-chabdo mukhyaḥ, anyatropacārata iti vakṣyan mukte tāvad upacārata ity āha—aśabdeti | mukto hy aśabda-gocaraḥ nāma-rūpād vimuktaḥ, na śabda-gocare yasya, yac ca vācām aviṣaye, agocaraṁ vacasām ity ādibhyaḥ upaniṣat-prasiddhyā tasyeti muktasya parāmarśaḥ, brahmatvaṁ ca brahma-sāmyāt pūjāyāṁ nimitta-bhūtāyāṁ tasyopacārato bhagavac-chabdaḥ kriyate | asya ślokasya bhagavad-viṣayatve vyāhatiḥ syāt | tatra śabdo'yaṁ nopacāreṇa tv anyatra hy upacārataḥ ity anantaraṁ vakṣyamāṇatvāt tad eva bhagavad-vācyam ity-āder uktatvāc ca ||71||



**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu yadīśvaro brahmaiva kathaṁ tarhi tasyānirdeśasya bhagavac-chabda-vācyatvam ity āśaṅkyāha—aśabda-gocarasyeti | pūjāyāṁ nimitta-bhūtāyām āviṣkṛta-ṣāḍguṇyena tad abhedaṁ prayujya upacārārthāya prayujyate ||71||



**śuddhe mahā-vibhūty-ākhye pare brahmaṇi vartate |**

**maitreya bhagavac-chabdaḥ sarva-kāraṇa-kāraṇe ||72||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **parama-kāraṇe pare brahmaṇi śabdo'yam anupacārataḥ śabdyata ity āha—śuddha iti | śuddhir mala-pratyanīkatvam mahā-vibhūty-ākhye mahā-vibhūti-saṁjñe mahā-vibhūtir hi brahmaṇaḥ, anyatra mukhyatvāsambhava-jñāpanāya ||72||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tad-bheda-bhūta-vivakṣāyāṁ tv artha-bhūto mukhya eva bhagavac-chabdārtha ity āha—śuddha iti | śuddhe asaṅge mahā-vibhūty-ākhye acintyaiśvarye ||72||



**sambharteti tathā bhartā bha-kāro’rtha-dvayānvitaḥ |**

**netā gamayitā sraṣṭā ga-kārārthas tathā mune ||73||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **bhagavac-chabdaṁ nirvakti—sambharteti | sambharaṇaṁ prakṛteḥ kārya-yogyatā-karaṇam | bhartā svāmī poṣakaś ca netā goptā gamayitā ātmānaṁ gamayitā saṁhartety arthaḥ | sraṣṭā ātmānam udgamayitā evaṁ gupeḥ gupty-arthatvāt gaty-arthatvāt gameś ca ga-kāro niruktaḥ | jñānārthatvād vā gamer ga-kāraḥ, tad aikṣata iti saṅkalpa-rūpekṣaṇasya kartety arthaḥ | gamayitā jñāpayiteti vā ga-kāraḥ | tathāhy ekāyana-niuktaṁ bha ity asmād bha-kārād bhartā sambharteti dvau dhātv-arthau gamyete | ga iti punar asmād ga-śabdād gamayitā netā sraṣṭā paratra gamanaṁ vā punar avyaya ity ato gaḥ so'sau bhartṛ-sambartṛ-netṛ-gamanavānetadvān bhagavān ity eva bhavatīti | tathātharva-śirasi—yaḥ sarvān bhagavān īkṣaty ātma-jñānān nirīkṣāyati yogaṁ gamayati tasmād ucyate sa bhagavān iti ||73||
