**śrīdharaḥ : **akṣarokta-niruktyā bhagavac-chabdasya parameśvara-vācakatvam āha—sambhartety-ādinā || sambhartā poṣakaḥ | bhartā nity-ādhāra ity artha-dvayānvitaḥ artha-dvayenānvitaḥ | netā karma-jñāna-phala-prapatter netṛtvaṁ prayojya-gamana-garbham iti ga-kārārthaḥ | gamayitā pralaye kāryāṇāṁ pratihartā | punar api teṣām udgamayitā sarga-karteti vā ga-kārārthaḥ ||73|| 



**aiśvaryasya samagrasya vīryasya yaśasaḥ śriyaḥ |**

**jñāna-vairāgyayoś caiva ṣaṇṇāṁ bhaga itīṅganā ||74||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **atha samudāya-niruktiḥ—aiśvaryasya iti | samagra-padaṁ sarvatra sambadhyate | bhagaḥ ṣāḍguṇyaṁ tadvān bhagavān ity abhiprāyaḥ ||74||



**śrīdharaḥ : **idānīṁ bhaga ity akṣara-dvayātmakasya padasyārtham āha—aiśvaryasya iti | bhaga itīraṇā saṁjñety arthaḥ ||74||



**vasanti tatra bhūtāni bhūtātmany akhilātmani |**

**sa ca bhūteṣv aśeṣeṣu va-kārārthas tato’vyayaḥ ||75||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **va-kārārtham āha—vasantīti | bhūtātmani bhūta-śarīre akhilātmani akhilasyātma-bhūte bhūtāni vasanti tatreti jagad-ādhāratvam uktam | sadāyatanā ity ādi śruteḥ | sa ca bhūtetyantarātmatvam | aitadātmyam idaṁ sarvam iti śruteḥ | ato vaḥ matupo vateś ca tantreṇāyaṁ va-kāraḥ ||75||



**śrīdharaḥ : **va-kārārtham āha—vasantīti | vasanti yatra bhūtāni iti ca pāṭhaḥ | yatrādhiṣṭhāna-bhūte bhūtāni vasanti sa ca bhūteṣu vasatīti va-kārasyārthaḥ ||75||



**evam eṣa mahā-śabdo bhagavān iti sattama |**

**parama-brahma-bhūtasya vāsudevasya nānyagaḥ ||76||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **evam ukta-prakāreṇāvayavārtha-yogād ayaṁ śabdo vāsudevasyaiva ||76|| 



**śrīdharaḥ : **evam eva-śabdo vāsudevasya vācakaḥ na tv anyasyety arthaḥ | bhaś cāsau gaś ca bhagavān ity akṣara-sāmyān niruktiḥ ṣāḍguṇyaṁ bhaga-saṁjñaṁ tadvān bhagavān ity anuṣaṅga eva ||76||



**tatra pūjya-padārthokti-paribhāṣā-samanvitaḥ |**

**śabdo’yaṁ nopacāreṇa hy anyatra hy upacārataḥ ||77||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **rūḍhi-śaktyāpi tasyaivety āha—tatreti | tatra bhavān bhagavān iti śabdo vṛddhiḥ prayujyate pūjye iti naighaṇṭuka-prasiddhyā ayaṁ śabdo loke pūjya-padārthasyoktau yā paribhāṣā tayā samanvito'pi viṣṇau niyataḥ nārāyaṇa-viṣṇv-ādi-śabdavat nopacāreṇa tasya sarva-kāraṇatayā sarva-guṇa-paripūrṇatayā parama-pūjyatayā cāyaṁ śabdo naupacārikaḥ | anyatra jīva-viśeṣe tv āpekṣika-pūjyatvād amukhyaḥ ||77||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tad evaṁ parameśvare niratiśayaiśvaryādi-yukte mukhyo'yaṁ śabdaḥ | anyatra tu gauṇa ity āha—tatreti | pūjyasya jyeṣṭhasya padārthasyoktā yā paribhāṣā saṅketa-rūpa-sambandha-grahaḥ tat-samanvito'yaṁ śabdaḥ | tatra para-brahmaṇi ataḥ nopacāreṇa vartate | anyatra tu devādau upacāreṇa vartate ||77||



**utpattiṁ pralayaṁ caiva bhūtānām āgatiṁ gatim |**

**vetti vidyām avidyāṁ ca sa vācyo bhagavān iti ||78||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **anyatropacārataḥ pravṛttau jñāna-viśeṣo nimittam ity āha—utpattim iti ||78||



**śrīdharaḥ : **upacāra-bījam āha—utpattim iti ||78||



**jñāna-śakti-balaiśvarya-vīrya-tejāṁsy aśeṣataḥ |**

**bhagavac-chabda-vācyāni vinā heyair guṇādibhiḥ ||79||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ : **atha bhagavato'nvaya-viśeṣaṇa-bhūtānāṁ satyakāmatvādīnāṁ guṇāntarāṇām ukteṣu guṇeṣv antarbhāvaṁ vyatireka-viśeṣaṇānāṁ sattvādi-guṇānāṁ bhagavān ity atra na-kāra-vācyatvaṁ cāha—jñāna-śaktīti | aśeṣataḥ aśeṣaiḥ sva-vistāra-bhūtair guṇāntaraiḥ saha na-kārasyārtham āha—vinā heyair iti | guṇādibhiḥ trguṇa-tat-kārya-kleśādibhiḥ nikhila-heya-pratyanīkatvaṁ samasta-kalyāṇa-guṇakatvaṁ ca ubhaya-liṅgaṁ kṛtsnaṁ bhagavac-chabda-vācyam ity anusandheyam iti | evaṁ bhagavaty āpti-sādhana-para-vidyāṅgatvenokta-śrīmad-dvādaśākṣara-mantre bhagavac-chabdo niruktaḥ | veda-śākhā-bheda-prakaraṇe praṇavārtha uktaḥ ||79||



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhagavac-chabda-vācyaṁ ṣāḍguṇyaṁ prakārāntareṇāha—jñāneti | heyaiḥ prakṛti-guṇaiḥ sat-kāryaiḥ karmabhis tat-phalaiś ca vinā ||79||



**sarvāṇi tatra bhūtāni vasanti paramātmani |**

**bhūteṣu ca sa sarvātmā vāsudevas tataḥ smṛtaḥ ||80||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ : **atha vāsudeva-śabdārtham āha—sarvāṇīti | bhūtāni jīvāḥ, vasanāt sarva-bhūtānāṁ vasutvād deva-yonitaḥ | vāsudevas tato jñeyaḥ ity udyoga-parvaṇi, vasanād devanāc caiva vāsudevaṁ tato viduḥ iti mokṣa-dharme | devanād dyotanād veti devaḥ vāsuś cāsau devaś ca vāsudevaḥ vasanty asmin deve bhūtānīty ekāyana-niruktam ||80||



**śrīdharaḥ : **dvādaśākṣarāntargata-bhagavac-chabdasyārtham uktvā vāsudeva-śabdasyārtham āha—sarvāṇīti | vasanād vāsanāc ca vāsuḥ, sādhanāt sādhur itivat | dyotanād devaḥ | vāsuś cāsau devaś ceti vāsudevaḥ | tad uktaṁ mokṣa-dharme—vasanād devanāc caiva vāsudevaṁ tato viduḥ iti ||80||



**khāṇḍikya-janakāyāha pṛṣṭaḥ keśi-dhvajaḥ purā |**

**nāma-vyākhyām anantasya vāsudevasya tattvataḥ ||81||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ : **uktam eva vāsudeva-śabda-nirvacanaṁ jñāna-niṣṭhair janakādibhir api parigṛhītam ity āha—khāṇḍikyeti ||81||



**śrīdharaḥ : **janakādayo’pi bhagavan-nāmālocana-niṣṭhayaiva brahma-jñānaṁ prāptā iti darśayann āha—khāṇḍikyety-ādi-ṣaḍbhiḥ ||81||



**bhūteṣu vasate so’ntar vasanty atra ca tāni yat |**

**dhātā vidhātā jagatāṁ vāsudevas tataḥ prabhuḥ****866**** ||82||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ : **nairuktaṁ deva-śabda-nirvacanaṁ darśayati—dhāteti | dadhāter va-kāraḥ niruktasyānuvādaḥ vāsudevas tata iti ||82||



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhūteṣu so’ntar iti vāsu-śabdo vyākhyātaḥ | dhātā vidhātety-ādinā deva-śabdo diver dhātoḥ anekārtha-prapañcena vyākhyāta iti jñeyam ||82||



**sa sarva-bhūta-prakṛtiṁ vikārān **

**guṇādi-doṣāṁś ca mune vyatītaḥ |**

**atīta-sarvāvaraṇo’khilātmā **

**tenāstṛtaṁ yad bhuvanāntarāle ||83||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ : **atha vidyā-dvaya-viṣaya-bhūta-dvādaśākṣara-pratipādatayā darśitam arthaṁ buddhi-sthemne prapañcayati—sa sarvety-ādi-caturbhiḥ | sarva-bhūta-prakṛtir avyaktaṁ vikārā mahad-ādyāḥ guṇāḥ sattvādyāḥ | ādi-śabdena tat-kārya-duḥkhājñānādaya uktāḥ vyatītāḥ tebhyo vilakṣaṇaḥ karma-kṛt tat-sambandha-rahitaś ca anena citas tat-saṁsṛṣṭāc ca vyāvṛttiḥ | atīta-sarvāvaraṇa iti | muktāt mukto hi saṁsāra-daśāyām avidyādy-āvṛtaḥ | akhilātmeti nity-ād vyāvṛttiḥ | akhilātmatvam upapādayati—tenāstṛtam iti | yat-sad-asad-vastu-jātam āstṛtam antar bahiś ca vyāptam ||83||



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhuvanāntarāle yad asti, tat sarvaṁ tenāstṛtaṁ cchannaṁ vyāptam iti yāvat ||83||



**samasta-kalyāṇa-guṇātmako’sau **

**sva-śakti-leśāvṛta-bhūta-vargaḥ |**

**icchā-gṛhītābhimatoru-dehaḥ**

**saṁsādhitāśeṣa-jagad-dhito yaḥ ||84||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ : **atrātma-śabdaḥ svabhāva-vacanaḥ | nijecchayā gṛhītābhimata-pūjya-dehaḥ | yad vā, jagad-dhitāyāvatāra-kāseṣv icchayā gṛhīta-tat-tat-kāryocitāneka-dehaḥ ||84||



**tejo-balaiśvarya-mahā-bodha-**

**suvīrya-śakty-ādi-guṇaika-rāśiḥ |**

**paraḥ parāṇāṁ sakalā na yatra **

**kleśādayaḥ santi parāvareśaḥ ||85||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ : **bhagavān iti śabda-sthana-kārasyārtham api vistareṇāha—na yatreti | kleśāḥ avidyā-smitādayaḥ | ādi-śabdena karma-vipākāśayā uktāḥ | āśayo vāsanā ||85||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kalyāṇa-guṇān evāha—tejo-baleti ||85||



**sa īśvaro vyaṣṭi-samaṣṭi-rūpo **

**vyakta-svarūpo’prakaṭa-svarūpaḥ |**

**sarveśvaraḥ sarva-dṛk sarva-vic ca **

**samasta-śaktiḥ parameśvarākhyaḥ ||86||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ : **vyūha-vibhavādi-rūpeṇa ca vyaṣṭi-samaṣṭi-rūpaḥ para-rūpeṇāvyakta-rūpaḥ, vyūhādi-rūpeṇa vyakta-rūpaḥ | evaṁ sarvāvastha-cid-acit-svarūpatve'pi sarveśvaraḥ, na tu para-vaśaḥ | sarva-dṛk, tac cakṣur deva-hitam, cakṣur devānām uta trailokyasyaika-cakṣuṣaḥ itivat | yad vā, yaḥ sarva-jñaḥ sarva-viditavat sarvaṁ veti sarva-prakāreṇa vettīti | athavā kāraṇam antareṇa karaṇaiś ca jānātīti, vidḷ lābhe ity ato vettīti vā | samasta-śaktiḥ sa paraḥ sarva-śaktīnāṁ samastāḥ śaktayaś ceti ||86||



**śrīdharaḥ : **prakṛtam upasaṁharati—sa iti ||86||



**saṁjñāyate yena tad-asta-doṣaṁ**

**śuddhaṁ paraṁ nirmalam eka-rūpam |**

**saṁdṛśyante vāpy avagamyate vā **

**taj-jñānam ajñānam ato’nyad uktam ||87||**



**viṣṇu-cittaḥ : **atha para-vidyāṁ praśaṁsann upasaṁharati—saṁjñāyata iti | sa jñāyate yeneti ca pāṭhaḥ | sa ity ukta-lakṣaṇaḥ puruṣottamaḥ parāmṛśyate tad iti hetau yasmād bhagavat-prāptir eva tāpa-trayasya bheṣajaṁ tasmāt sa yena āgamotthena jñānena jñāyate yena vivekajena sandṛśyate, yena ca darśana-samānākāreṇa bhakti-rūpāpannena gamyate, tad eva jñānam ajñānam ato'nyat bhagavad-vyatirikta-viṣayam ajñānam avidyā-rūpaṁ bandhakam ity arthaḥ | asta-doṣam iti vikārāspadācid-viṣayād vyāvṛttiḥ | śuddham iti tat-saṁsṛṣṭa-cetana-viṣayāt paraṁ nirmalam iti heyārham ukta-viṣayāt eka-rūpam iti | sūri-viṣayāt teṣām aneka-rūpatvāt, tam eva vidvān, tam eva viditvā nānyaḥ panthā ity ādi-śrutibhir ittham uktam iti ||87||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yena jñāyate parokṣa-vṛttyā | sandṛśyate sākṣātkriyate | adhigamyate niḥśeṣāvidyā-nivṛttyā prāpyate, taj jñānam, parā vidyā | anyad ajñānam avidyāntar-vāsinī aparā vidyety arthaḥ ||87||



|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe ṣaṣṭhe’ṁśe pañcamo’dhyāyaḥ ||



—o\)0\(o—



\(6.6\)





## keśidhvaja-khāṇḍīkyayor vivaraṇam



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**svādhyāya-saṁyamābhyām sa dṛśyate puruṣottamaḥ |**

**tat-prāpti-kāraṇaṁ brahma tad etad iti paṭhyate ||1||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **evam upāsya-bhūtaṁ bhagavat-svarūpam uktam | idānīm upāsana-paryāyaṁ sāṅgopāṅgaṁ vaktum ārabhate—svādhyāyeti | svādhyāya-śabdena vedānta-dvādaśākṣara-praṇavādīnāṁ tattva-parāṇāṁ mīmāṁsā-sahitānāṁ vākyānāṁ nirdeśaḥ sa ity ukta-guṇa-vibhūti-vigrahādi-viśiṣṭaḥ puruṣottamaḥ parāmṛśyate | svādhyāya-saṁyama-janitaṁ brahma-viṣayatvād brahma-śabda-vācyam | tad etaj jñānaṁ na kevalaṁ darśana-sādhanam api tu prāpti-sādhanaṁ cocyate ity āha—tat-prāptīti | tat-prāpti-kāraṇaṁ tad etaj jñānaṁ brahmeti paṭhyata iti vā yojanā ||1||



**śrīdharaḥ : **pūrvādhyāyānte saṁjñāyate yenety atra paramātmaḥ jñāna-sandarśana-prāptaye yad bhavati tatparaṁ jñānam ity uktam | tad dṛḍha-jñānaṁ manana-sahakṛtena vedānta-vākya-śravaṇena bhavatīti prasiddham eva | atas tad ullaṅghya darśana-prāptau kāraṇam āha—svādhyāyeti | svādhyāyaḥ praṇavādi-japaḥ | saṁyamo yogaḥ | tābhyāṁ sa puruṣottamo dṛśyate | tasya prāptāv api tad eva dvayaṁ kāraṇam | ata eva tad eva dvayaṁ darśana-dvārā brahma-prāpti-hetutvād brahmety abhidhīyate ||1||



**svādhyāyād yogam āsīta yogāt svādhyāyam āvaset |**

**svādhyāya-yoga-sampattyā paramātmā prakāśate ||2||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **samīmāṁsāt svādhyāyāt arthaṁ paricchidhya yogam āsīta guṇa-traya-mayatvena manasaḥ pramāda-sambhavāt anyathopāsana-parihārāya yogāt svādhyāyam āvaset | yogāt svādhyāyam āmaned iti ca pāṭhaḥ | yathā bālo mātṛkā-patrikāṁ vīkṣya lipi-vinyāsam abhyasyati tadvat kapilānusāribhir hi kevala-yogāvalambanāj jagataḥ pradhāna-paramāṇv-ādi-kāraṇatva-nirīśvaratvādikaṁ dṛṣṭam | vedānusāribhis tu brahma-kāraṇatva-brahmātmakatvādi-yogo dṛṣṭaḥ | sampattiḥ pauṣkayam ||2|| 



**śrīdharaḥ : **tad-anuṣṭhāna-prakāram āha—svādhyāyād iti | svādhyāyānantaraṁ yogam abhyaset | yogānantaraṁ ca svādhyāyaṁ kuryāt | evaṁ tayoḥ sampattyā samṛddhyā paramātmā prakāśate | tathā ca yoga-śāstraṁ—



japāc chrāntaḥ punar dhyāyed dhyānāc chrāntaḥ punar japet |

japa-dhyānādi-yogena paśyed ātmānam ātmani || iti ||2||



**tad-īkṣaṇāya svādhyāyaś cakṣur yogas tathā param |**

**na māṁsa-cakṣuṣā draṣṭuṁ brahma-bhūtaḥ sa śakyate867 ||3||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **etad upapādayati—tad-īkṣaṇāya svādhyāyaś cakṣur iti | yogaḥ paraṁ cakṣuḥ pradhānaṁ cakṣuḥ aparokṣa-rūpatvāt ||3||



**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu cakṣur-ādibhir apy ātmana eva sphuraṇāt katham idam eva dvayaṁ tat-prakāśakam ucyate ? tatrāha—tad-īkṣaṇāyeti | viṣayāvacchedaṁ vinā pūrṇa-brahma-bhūto māṁsa-mayaś cakṣur-ādibhir draṣṭuṁ na śakyata ity arthaḥ ||3||



**śrī-maitreya uvāca—**

**bhagavaṁs tam ahaṁ yogaṁ jñātum icchāmi taṁ vada |**

**jñāte yatrākhilādhāraṁ paśyeyaṁ parameśvaram ||4||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **yatra yasmin yoge jñāte jñātvānuṣṭhite satīty arthaḥ ||4||



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**yathā keśidhvajaḥ prāha khāṇḍikyāya mahātmane |**

**janakāya purā yogaṁ tam ahaṁ kathayāmi te ||5||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**śrī-maitreya uvāca—**

**khāṇḍikyaḥ ko’bhavad brahman ko vā keśidhvajaḥ kṛtī |**

**kathaṁ tayoś ca saṁvādo yoga-sambandhavān abhūt ||6||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **yoga-sambandha-kāraṇāt yogena sambandho yoga-sambandhaḥ | kṛtī paṇḍitaḥ ||6||



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**dharmadhvajo vai janakas tasya putro’mitadhvajaḥ |**

**kṛtadhvajaś ca nāmnāsīt sadādhyātma-ratir nṛpa ||7||**

**kṛtadhvajasya putro’bhūt khyātaḥ keśidhvajo nṛpa |**

**putro’mitadhvajasyāpi khāṇḍikya-janako’bhavat ||8||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**karma-mārgeṇa khāṇḍikyaḥ pṛthivyām abhavat kṛtī |**

**keśidhvajo’py atīvāsīd ātma-vidyā-viśāradaḥ ||9||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **pūrvādhyāyopakṣiptam evetihāsaṁ yoga-nirūpaṇārtham anuvartayati—keśidhvaja ity ādinā yāvad-uttarādhyāya-samāptiḥ ||9||



**tāv ubhāv api caivāstāṁ vijigīṣū parasparam |**

**keśidhvajena khāṇḍikyaḥ svarājyād avaropitaḥ ||10||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **avaropitaḥ bhraṁśitaḥ ||10||



**purodhasā mantribhiś ca samaveto’lpa-sādhanaḥ |**

**rājyān nirākṛtaḥ so’tha durgāraṇya-caro’bhavat ||11||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **alpa-sādhanaḥ svalpa-parikaraḥ ||11||



**iyāja so’pi subahūn yajñān jñāna-vyapāśrayaḥ |**

**brahma-vidyām adhiṣṭhāya tartuṁ mṛtyum avidyayā ||12||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **svādhyāya-pravacane eva iti śruteḥ svādhyāyasya vidyāṅgatvam uktam | idānīṁ yajñādi-śruter yajñāṅgatvam ucyate—iyājeti | so'pi keśidhvajaḥ jñāna-vyapāśrayaḥ ātma-jñānavān brahma-vidyām adhiṣṭhāya brahmopāsana-niṣṭha eva iyāja | kim artham ? ity āha—tartum iti | mṛtuḥ para-vidyotpatti-virodhi-prācīna-karma avidyayā karmaṇā avidyā karma-saṁjñeti vakṣyati ||12||



**śrīdharaḥ : **so'pi keśidhvajo jñāna-vyapāśrayaḥ jñāna-niṣṭho'pi brahma-vidyām adhiṣṭhāya brahmārpaṇa-nyāyena kartṛ-karmādikaṁ sarvaṁ brahmaiveti dṛṣṭyā bahūn yajñān iyāja | kim-artham ? avidyayā karma-lakṣaṇayā mṛtyuṁ saṁsāra-hetuṁ kāmādikāśeṣaṁ tartuṁ kṣapayitum ||12||



**ekadā vartamānasya yāge yoga-vidāṁ vara | **

**gharma-dhenuṁ jaghānograḥ śārdūlo vijane vane ||13||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **gharmaḥ pravargya-haviḥ tad-dogdhrīti gharma-dhenuḥ ||13||



**śrīdharaḥ : **gharma-dogdhrīm iti pāṭhe pravargyo havir viśeṣo gharmas tad-arthaṁ payo-dogdhrī, śārdūlo vyāghraḥ ||13||



**tato rājā hatāṁ śrutvā dhenuṁ vyāghreṇa ca rtvijaḥ |**

**prāyaścittaṁ sa prapaccha kim atreti vidhīyatām ||14||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kim atra prāyaścittaṁ vidhīyatām iti papraccha ||14||



**te’py ūcur na vayaṁ vidmaḥ kaśeruḥ pṛcchyatām iti |**

**kaśerur api tenoktas tathaiva prāha bhārgavam ||15||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **tathaiva tenoktaḥ kaśerur api śunakaṁ pṛcchety āhety uttareṇānvayaḥ ||15||



**śunakaṁ pṛccha rājendra nāhaṁ vedmi sa vetsyati |**

**sa gatvā tam apṛcchac ca so’py āha śṛṇu yan mune ||16||**

**na kaśerur na caivāhaṁ na cānyaḥ sāmprataṁ bhuvi |**

**vetty eka eva tvac-chatruḥ khāṇḍikyo yo jitas tvayā ||17||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**sa cāha taṁ vrajāmy eṣa praṣṭum ātma-ripuṁ mune |**

**prāpta eva mahā-yajño yadi māṁ sa haniṣyati ||18||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **prāpta eveti | dharmārtham udyuktasyāntarā vipattau satyām api tat-phala-siddheḥ śāstra-siddhatvāt ||18||



**śrīdharaḥ : **ātma-ripum api taṁ prāyaścittaṁ praṣṭum eṣo'haṁ vrajāmi yadi māṁ sa haniṣyati tarhi mahā-yajñaḥ prāpta eva mahā-yajña-phalaṁ prāptam eva mayety arthaḥ | tathā ca—dharmārthaṁ yatamānas tu antarā ced vipadyate | sa dharma-phalam āpnoti iti vacanāt ||18||



**prāyaścittam aśeṣeṇa sa cet pṛṣṭo vadiṣyati |**

**tataś cāvikalo yāgo muni-śreṣṭha bhaviṣyati ||19||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **mayā pṛṣṭaḥ sa prāyaścittam aśeṣeṇa vakṣyati cet, tataś ca yāgo'vikalo bhaviṣyati | tataś cety uktyā prāyaścitta-kathane'pi vā madīya-yāgaḥ saphalo bhaviṣyatīty abhiprāyeṇāheti pūrveṇānvayaḥ ||19||



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**ity uktvā ratham āruhya kṛṣṇājina-dharo nṛpaḥ |**

**vanaṁ jagāma yatrāste sa khāṇḍikyo mahā-matiḥ ||20||**

**tam āpatantam ālokya khāṇḍikyo ripum ātmanaḥ |**

**provāca krodha-tāmrākṣaḥ samāropita-kārmukaḥ ||21||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**khāṇḍikya uvāca—**

**kṛṣṇājinaṁ tvaṁ kavacam ābadhyāsmān haniṣyati |**

**kṛṣṇājina-dhare vetsi na mayi prahariṣyati ||22||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **mayi na prahariṣyatīti vetsīty anvayaḥ | atreti śabdo'dhyāhāryaḥ ||22||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kṛṣṇājina-kavaca-bandhe tasyābhiprāyam utprekṣate kṛṣṇājina-dhare mayi khāṇḍikyo na prahariṣyatīti vetsi manyase ||22||



**mṛgāṇāṁ vada pṛṣṭheṣu mūḍha kṛṣṇājinaṁ na kim |**

**yeṣāṁ mayā tvayā cogrāḥ prahitāḥ śita-sāyakāḥ ||23||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **tad vyartham ity āha—mṛgāṇām iti | yeṣāṁ pṛṣṭeṣv ity anuṣaṅgaḥ ||23||



**sa tvām ahaṁ haniṣyāmi na me jīvan vimokṣyase |**

**ātatāyy asi durbuddhe mama rājya-haro ripuḥ ||24||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **rājya-haratvād ātatāyī | ato yajña-sthasyāpi te na pātakam ||24||



**śrīdharaḥ : **agnido garadaś caiva śastra-pāṇir dhanāpahaḥ | kṣetra-dāra-haraś caiva ṣaḍ ete hy ātatāyinaḥ || iti smṛteḥ | tvam ātatāyī, ataḥ savanasthasyāpi tava vadhe na doṣaḥ | nātatāyi-vadhe doṣo hantur bhavati kaścana ity ādi-vacanāt ||24||



**keśidhvaja uvāca—**

**khāṇḍikya saṁśayaṁ praṣṭuṁ bhavantam aham āgataḥ |**

**na tvāṁ hantuṁ vicāryaitat kopaṁ bāṇaṁ vimuṁ ca vā ||25||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **bāṇaṁ vety anvayaḥ ||25||



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**tataḥ sa mantribhiḥ sārdham ekānte sa-purohitaḥ |**

**mantrayāmāsa khāṇḍikyaḥ sarvair eva mahāmatiḥ ||26||**

**tam ūcur mantriṇo vadhyo ripur eṣa vaśaṁ gataḥ |**

**hate’smin pṛthivī sarvā tava vaśyā bhaviṣyati ||27||**

**khāṇḍikyaś cāha tān sarvān evam etan na saṁśayaḥ |**

**hate’smin pṛthivī sarvā mama vaśyā bhaviṣyati ||28||**



\(26-28\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**para-loka-jayas tasya pṛthivī sakalā mama |**

**na hanmi cel loka-jayo mama tasya vasundharā ||29||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **para-loka-jayas tasyeti dharmārthaṁ pravṛttasyāntarā-maraṇe'pi tat-phala-siddher iti bhāvaḥ | na hanmi cel loka-jaya ity upapanna-vadha-kṛta-cāpa-pratibandhābhāve pūrvair eva puṇyaiḥ para-loka-siddher iti bhāvaḥ ||29||



**nāhaṁ manye loka-jayād adhikā syād vasundharā |**

**para-loka-jayo’nantaḥ svalpa-kālo mahī-jayaḥ ||30||**

**tasmān nainaṁ haniṣyāmi yat pṛcchati vadāmi tat ||31||**



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**tatas tam abhyupetyāha khāṇḍikya-janako ripum |**

**praṣṭavyaṁ yat tvayā sarvaṁ tat pṛcchasva vadāmy aham ||32||**

**tataḥ sarvaṁ yathā-vṛttaṁ dharma-dhenu-vadhaṁ dvija |**

**kathayitvā sa papraccha prāyaścittaṁ hi tad-gatam ||33||**



\(30-33\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**sa cācaṣṭa yathā-nyāyaṁ dvija keśidhvajāya tat |**

**prāyaścittam aśeṣeṇa yad vai tatra vidhīyate ||34||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **yad vai tatra vidhīyata ity atra prāyaścittaṁ vājasaneyoktaṁ spṛṇomi homākhyam | iyaṁ hy ākhyāyikā vājasaneya-śākhāyāṁ keśi-gṛha-patinā upasamrājam anaḍuhaṁ śārdūlo jaghāna ity upakramya spṛte hutvety-ādi coktvā pṛthivyai te śarīraṁ spṛṇomi svāhā ity antā sa-prapañcam uktā āpastambena tu, yady anuḍvāhaṁ gharma-dogdhrīṁ vā śārdūlo hanyād arka-kṣīram ajā-kṣīram anya-dhenuṁ vāśritya pracaret ity-ādy-uktam ||34||



**śrīdharaḥ : **imam eva viṣayaṁ prastutya vājasaneyake spṛṇomi homākhyaṁ prāyaścittam uktaṁ, candrāt te manaḥ spṛṇomi svāhā | sūryāt te cakṣuḥ spṛṇomi svāhā | vātāt te prāṇaṁ spṛṇomi svāhā ity ādi | āpastambena coktam—yady anuḍvāhaṁ gharma-dogdhrīṁ vā śārdūlo hanyād arka-kṣīram ajā-kṣīram anya-dhenuṁ vāśritya pracaret ity-ādi | asya ca prāyaścittasya sphuṭatve'pi yathādeśa-kālāvasthā-viśeṣa-prāyaścitta-prakalpanaṁ khāṇḍikyād aparo na vettīti pūrvoktābhiprāyaḥ | tad āha yad vai tatra prāyaścittaṁ vidhīyate tad aśeṣaṁ yathā-nyāyaṁ keśidhvajāyācaṣṭeti ||34||



**viditārthaḥ sa tenaiva hy anujñāto mahātmanā |**

**yāga-bhūmim upāgamya cakre sarvāḥ kriyāḥ kramāt ||35||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**krameṇa vidhivad yāgaṁ nītvā so’vabhṛthāplutaḥ |**

**kṛta-kṛtyas tato bhūtvā cintayāmāsa pārthivaḥ ||36||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **yāgaṁ nītvā samāpya ||36||



**pūjitāś ca dvijāḥ sarve sadasyā mānitā mayā |**

**tathaivārthijano’py arthair yājito’bhimatair mayā ||37||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**yathārham asya lokasya mayā sarvaṁ viceṣṭitam |**

**aniṣpanna-kriyaṁ cetas tathāpi mama kiṁ yathā ||38||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tathāpi mamedaṁ cetaḥ aniṣpanna-kriyaṁ yathākṛta-kṛtyam iva bhavati kim iti cintā yathā-śabdaḥ sādṛśye ||38||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tathāpi yad aniṣpanna-kriyam akṛtakṛtyam ivāprasannaṁ cetaḥ kim iti tiṣṭhatīti cintayāmāsety anvayaḥ ||38||



**itthaṁ sañcintayann eva sasmāra sa mahīpatiḥ |**

**khāṇḍikyāya na datteti mayā vai guru-dakṣiṇā ||39||**

**sa jagāma tadā bhūyo ratham āruhya pārthivaḥ |**

**maitreya durga-gahanaṁ khāṇḍikyo yatra saṁsthitaḥ ||40||**

**khāṇḍikyo’pi punar dṛṣṭvā tam āyāntaṁ dhṛtāyudham |**

**tasthau hantuṁ kṛta-matis tam āha sa punar nṛpaḥ ||41||**



\(39-41\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**bho nāhaṁ te’parādhāya prāptaḥ khāṇḍikya mā krudhāḥ |**

**guror niṣkraya-dānāya mām avehi tvam āgatam ||42||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **niṣkrayo dakṣiṇā | niṣkayo iti ca pāṭhaḥ ||42||



**śrīdharaḥ : **bho khāṇḍikya \! mā krudhāḥ krodhaṁ mākārṣīḥ ||42||



**niṣpādito mayā yāgaḥ samyak tvad-upadeśataḥ |**

**so’haṁ te dātum icchāmi vṛṇīṣva guru-dakṣiṇām ||43||**



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**bhūyaḥ sa mantribhiḥ sārdhaṁ mantrayāmāsa pārthivaḥ |**

**guru-niṣkraya-kāmo’yaṁ kiṁ mayā prārthyatām iti ||44||**



\(43-44\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**tam ūcur mantriṇo rājyam aśeṣaṁ prārthayatām ayam |**

**śatrubhiḥ prārthayate rājyam anāyāsita-sainikaiḥ ||45||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **anāyāsitā yuddhādi-kleśam aprāpitāḥ sainikāḥ bhaṭāḥ yaiḥ ||45||



**prahasya tān āha nṛpaḥ sa khāṇḍikyo mahā-matiḥ |**

**svalpa-kālaṁ mahī-pālyaṁ mādṛśaiḥ prārthayate katham ||46||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**evam etad bhavanto’tra hy artha-sādhana-mantriṇaḥ |**

**paramārthaḥ kutra ko’tra yūyaṁ nātra vicakṣaṇāḥ ||47||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **atra rājya-cintāyām | atra saṁsāre kaḥ paramārthaḥ sa ca katham ity atrārthe yūyaṁ na vicakṣaṇāḥ ||47||



**śrīdharaḥ : **atra saṁsāre kaḥ paramārthaḥ sa ca kathaṁ bhavatīty arthe yūyaṁ na paṇḍitāḥ ||47||



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**ity uktvā samupetyainaṁ sa tu keśidhvajaṁ nṛpaḥ |**

**uvāca kim avaśyaṁ tvaṁ dadāsi guru-dakṣiṇām ||48||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**bāḍham ity eva tenoktaḥ khāṇḍikyas tam athābravīt |**

**bhavān adhyātma-vijñāna-paramārtha-vicakṣaṇaḥ ||49||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **adhyātmeti adhyātma-vijñānasya paramārthaḥ prayojanaṁ sa ca kleśa-nivṛttiḥ ||49||



**yadi ced dīyate mahyaṁ bhavatā guru-niṣkrayaḥ |**

**tat kleśa-praśamāyālaṁ yat karma tad udīraya ||50||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tat tasmāt | kleśa-praśamāya yad alaṁ tad udīrayety abravīt ity anvayaḥ ||50||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tat tarhi ||50||



|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe ṣaṣṭhe’ṁśe ṣaṣṭho’dhyāyaḥ ||



—o\)0\(o—



\(6.7\)



## brahma-yoga-nirṇayaḥ



**keśidhvaja uvāca—**

**na prārthitaṁ tvayā kasmād asmad-rājyam akaṇṭakam |**

**rājya-lābhād vinā nānyat kṣatriyāṇām atipriyam ||1||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **atha keśidhvajaḥ kleśaṁ mumukṣoḥ khāṇḍikyasya vairāgyaṁ parīkṣitum āha—na prārthitam iti | prajāpālanādeḥ kṣattra-dharmasya rājya-mūlatvāt tad-upekṣāyāṁ doṣāt kiṁ rājyaṁ na prārthitam iti bhāvaḥ ||1||



śrīdharaḥ :

khāṇḍikyāya dadau vidyāṁ karmiṇe gurave parām | 

keśidhvajo na tac citraṁ kim adeyaṁ mahātmanām ||



tattva-jijñāsave khāṇḍikyāya tattva-jñānam upadeṣṭuṁ keśidhvajas tasya viveka-vairāgya-parīkṣārtham āha—na prārthitam iti | akaṇṭakaṁ niṣpratipakṣaṁ rājyaṁ vinā prajā-paripālanādeḥ kṣatra-dharmasyāsiddheḥ | tat-siddhaye rāja-prārthanaiva yuktā, anyathā sva-dharma-hāni-prasaṅgād iti bhāvaḥ ||1||



**khāṇḍikya uvāca—**

**keśidhvaja nibodha tvaṁ mayā na prārthitaṁ yataḥ |**

**rājyam etad aśeṣaṁ te yatra gṛdhnanty apaṇḍitāḥ ||2||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **yataḥ kāraṇān na prārthitaṁ tac chṛṇv ity āha—keśidhvajeti ||2||



**śrīdharaḥ : **atrottaraṁ—keśidhvajety-ādi | yataḥ kāraṇāt tvadīyaṁ rājyaṁ mayā na prārthitam | tad idaṁ nibodha, śṛṇu | yatra rājye apaṇḍitāḥ avivekinaḥ bhoga-lipsava eva gṛdhnanti apekṣāṁ kurvanti ||2||



**kṣatriyāṇām ayaṁ dharmo yat prajā-paripālanam |**

**vadhaś ca dharma-yuddhena sva-rājya-paripanthinām ||3||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tad eva kāraṇam āha—kṣatriyāṇām iti sārdhena | satyaṁ rājye sati prajā-rakṣaṇādi-dharmaḥ ||3||


**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu sva-dharma-siddhaye paṇḍitānām api rājya-kāṅkṣā yuktevety uktaṁ tatrāha—kṣatriyāṇām iti | yat prajā-paripālanaṁ yaś ca sva-rājya-paripanthināṁ vadhaḥ, ayaṁ rājyādhikṛtānāṁ kṣatriyāṇāṁ dharmaḥ, na tu kṣatriya-mātrasya ||3||



**tatrāśaktasya me doṣo naivāsty apahṛte tvayā |**

**bandhāyaiva bhavaty eṣā hy avidyāpy akramojjhitā ||4||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **mama tv aśaktasya ca tatra rājye tvayāpahṛte ati tad-upekṣāyāṁ na dharma-lopa-doṣaḥ, anadhikārāt saty adhikāre tad-upekṣāyāṁ doṣa ity āha—bandhāyeti | akramojjhitā vidyamāne'py adhikāre tyaktā avidyā prajāpālanādi-kriyā bandhāya pāpāya | hi-śabdo hetau ||4||


**śrīdharaḥ : **atas tatreti | tatra mad-rājye tvayāpahṛte sati punar ātma-sātkartum aśaktasya mama prajā-paripālanādi-tyāge'pi doṣo naivāsti | tatrāsaktasyeti pāṭhe tatra rājye asaktasya anāsaktasya me doṣo nāstīty arthaḥ | rājyādhikārābhāvena tad-adhikṛta-dharme'py adhikāra-nivṛtteḥ, anyathā tu doṣaḥ syād eva na punar avidyā | asya karmaṇas tyāge kiṁ syād iti vaktuṁ śakyaṁ hi yasmād eṣā karma-mayī avidyāpi akramojjhitā nayāyena saty evādhikāre parityaktā satī bandhāya bhavaty evety arthaḥ ||4||



**janmopabhoga-lipsārtham iyaṁ rājya-spṛhā mama |**

**anyeṣāṁ doṣajā saiva dharmaṁ vai nānurudhyate ||5||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **asaktasyety etad vivṛṇoti—janmeti | anyeṣāṁ doṣajā rāgādi-doṣajā rājya-spṛhā na dharmānurodhinī kevalam alpopabhoga-lipsārthaṁ bhavati | iyaṁ na mamety anvayaḥ | janmopabhogeti pāṭhe anyeṣāṁ sambandhinī mama janmāntaropabhoga-lipsaiva | kutaḥ ? artham anurudhyate na dharmam iti asmin janmany upabhoga-lipsārtham eveti vā ||5||


**śrīdharaḥ :**evaṁ ca sati mama vā mantriṇāṁ vā tvad-rājye spṛhā dharmāya na bhavatīty āha—janmeti | yady evaṁ dharmaḥ, tadā mameyaṁ rājya-spṛhā rāja-dharmocita-cchatra-cāmarādi-janmāntaropabhoga-lipsārtham eva bhavati, na tu dharmārtham | anyeṣāṁ sacivādīnāṁ saiva tvad-rājya-spṛhā rāgādi-lobha-doṣajā, ato dharmam eva kevalaṁ nānurdhyate nānuvartate, api tu dharma-vañcanenārtha-śāstram evānuvartate ity arthaḥ ||5||



**na yācñā kṣatra-bandhūnāṁ dharmāyaitat satāṁ matam |**

**ato na yācitaṁ rājyam avidyāntargataṁ tava ||6||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tarhi palanādi-dharmārtham apahṛtasya rājyasya yācñā kartavyety atrāha—na yācñeti | kṣattra-bandhūnāṁ kṣatriya-śreṣṭhānām avidyāntargataṁ pālanādi-kartavyāntar-gatam ||6||


**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu tathāpi yācanā-mātreṇa rājyaṁ labdhvā mahān dharmaḥ kim iti na kriyate, tatrāha—na yācñeti | ato dharmatvād avidyāntargatatvāc ca tvadīyaṁ rājyaṁ mayā na prārthitam ||6||



**rājye gṛdhnaty avidvāṁso mamatvāhṛta-cetasaḥ |**

**ahaṁ-māna-mahā-pāna-madam attā na mādṛśāḥ ||7||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **yatra gṛdhnaty apaṇḍitā ity etad vivṛṇoti—rājya iti ||7||


**śrīdharaḥ : **ato yatra gṛdhnanty apaṇḍitā iti yad uktaṁ tad eva siddham ity āha—rājya iti || ahaṁ-māna eva mahā-pānaṁ tena yo madas tena mattāḥ ||7||



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**prahṛṣṭāḥ sādhv iti prāha tataḥ keśidhvajo nṛpaḥ |**

**khāṇḍikya-janakaṁ prītyā śrūyatāṁ vacanaṁ mama ||8||**


**śrīdharaḥ : **khāṇḍikyenoktaṁ śrutvā keśidhvajaḥ kiṁ kṛtavān ity apekṣāyām āha—prahṛṣṭa iti | prahṛṣṭaḥ sādhv iti pāṭhe tava buddhir iti śeṣaḥ ||8||



**keśidhvaja uvāca—**

**ahaṁ hy avidyayā mṛtyuṁ tartu-kāmaḥ karomi vai |**

**rājyaṁ yāgāṁś ca vividhān bhogaiḥ puṇya-kṣayaṁ tathā ||9||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **yoga-svarūpaṁ vakṣyan tad-antar-bhūtam adhyātma-yogādhigameneti śruti-vihitaṁ prakṛti-puruṣa-vivekaṁ vihitaṁ karma cāha—ahaṁ hīti | avidyayā varṇāśrama-vihita-karmaṇā mṛtyuṁ vidyotpatti-virodhi prārabdha-karma anyeṣām apy eṣa vināśaḥ iti śruteḥ ||9||



**śrīdharaḥ : **avidyā-maye'pi rājye sva-pravṛttau tavat kāraṇam āha—ahaṁ hīti | satyaṁ tvayoktam avidyāntargatatvād rājyam anupādeyam iti tac ca mamāpi tulyaṁ tathāpi aviyayā prajāpālanādi-karma-lakṣaṇayā sattva-śuddhyā kāma-krodhādi-lakṣaṇaṁ mṛtyuṁ saṁsāra-hetuṁ tartum icchann ahaṁ rājyādi karomi | avidyayā mṛtyuṁ tīrtvā vidyayāmṛtam aśnute ity ādi śruteḥ ||9||



**tad idaṁ te mano diṣṭyā vivekaiśvaryatāṁ gatam |**

**tac chrūyatām avidyāyāḥ svarūpaṁ kulanandana ||10||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **vivekākhyam aiśvaryaṁ viveka eva .ayatiaṁ yasya tad vivekaiśvaryaṁ tad-bhāvo vivekaiśvaryatā | karmākhyāvidyāyāḥ svarūpam āha—tac chrūyatām iti sārdhena ||10||


**śrīdharaḥ : **tava punas tad idaṁ manaḥ viveke aiśvaryaṁ sāmarthyaṁ yasya tasya bhāvo vivekaiśvaryatā tāṁ gataṁ prāptam upadeśādy-anapekṣaṁ svayam eva vivekādhikāratāṁ gataṁ prāptam etad diṣṭyā bhadram ity arthaḥ | vivekaiśvaryam āgatam iti tu pāṭhaḥ sugamaḥ | tad evaṁ śiṣyasya vivekādikaṁ parīkṣyābhinandya edānīṁ tena yat pṛṣṭaṁ tat kleśa-praśamāyālaṁ yat karma tad udīrayeti tad vaktuṁ prathamaṁ tāvad avidyākhyaṁ kleśa-svarūpaṁ darśayati—tac chrūyatām ity ādi sārdhena ślokena ||10||



**anātmany ātma-buddhir yā cāsve svam iti yā matiḥ |**

**saṁsāra-taru-sambhūti-bījam etad dvidhā sthitam ||11||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **anātmani dehe aham iti bhramaḥ | asve deha-poṣaka-dhārakādau vastuni svam iti saṁsāra-phalakaṁ kāmya-karma-vidyā saiva taruḥ tat-sambhūter bījam ||11||


**śrīdharaḥ : **anātmani dehādau sva-kṣetrādau ca ahaṁ-mameti yā matiḥ sā avidyā viparyaya-rūpā yā, anityāśuci-duḥkhānātmasu nitya-śuci-sukhātma-khyātir avidyā \[yo.sū. 2.5\] iti pātañjalam | tasyā anartha-hetutvam āha—etad dvidhā darśitam avidyā-svarūpaṁ saṁsāra-taru-sambhūteḥ bījatayā sthitam ||11||



**pañca-bhūtātmake dehe dehī moha-tamo-vṛtaḥ |**

**ahaṁ mamaitad ity uccaiḥ kurute kumatir matim ||12||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **etad dvividhaṁ ca bhramaṁ prapañcayati pañca-bhūtātmaka ity ādi caturbhiḥ | dehe pañca-bhūtātmake kumatir dehī idaṁ dehādy aham eveti, idaṁ kṣetrādi mameti ca matiṁ kurute | moha-tamaḥ pūrva-karma-vāsanā ||12||


**śrīdharaḥ : **dehādāv ahaṁ-mānasyāvidyātvam upapādayati—pañceti | pañca-bhūtātmake dehe dehī kumatiḥ viparyaya-matiḥ ahaṁ mamaitad iti matiṁ kurute | dvitīya-mati-śabdas tad-āvṛtty-arthaḥ | viparyāse hetuḥ—mohatamasā svarūpājñānenāvṛta iti | ajñāte hi vastu-svarūpe viparyāso bhavati ||12||



**ākāśa-vāyv-agni-jala-pṛthivībhyaḥ pṛthak sthite |**

**ātmany ātma-mayaṁ bhāvaṁ kaḥ karoti kalevare ||13||**


**śrīdharaḥ : **kumatitvam eva spaṣṭayati—ākāśeti | ākāśādibhyas tat-sākṣītayā ātmani pṛthak sthite sati tat-kārye dehe ātma-mayaṁ bhāvaṁ kaḥ kuryāt ? ||13||



**kalevaropabhogyaṁ hi gṛha-kṣetrādikaṁ ca kaḥ |**

**adehe hy ātmani prājño mamedam iti manyate ||14||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **adehe ātmani dehād anyasminn ātmani sati ||14||


**śrīdharaḥ : **mama pratyayasyāpi mithyātvaṁ spaṣṭayati kalevareti dvābhyām | adehe deha-vyatirikte ātmani sati dehopabhogyaṁ gṛhādi madīyam iti kaḥ prājño manyate ? ||14||



**itthaṁ ca putra-pautreṣu tad-dehotpāditeṣu kaḥ |**

**karoti paṇḍitaḥ svāmyam anātmani kalevare ||15||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **anātmani ātmano'nyasmin sati ||15||


**śrīdharaḥ : **kalevare anātmani sati tad-utpāditeṣu kaḥ svāmyaṁ karoti ? ||15||



**sarvaṁ dehopabhogāya kurute karma mānavaḥ |**

**dehaś cānyo yadā puṁsas tadā bandhāya tatparam ||16||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **uktenājñāna-dvayena dehopabhogārthaṁ karma karoti, tac ca bandhāya bhavatīty āha—sarvam iti | dehasyopabhogāya nātmanaḥ bandhāya dehāntarotpādanāya ||16||


**śrīdharaḥ : **tad eva deha-gehādiṣu ahaṁ mamābhimānayor avidyātvaṁ samarpitaṁ samarpitam, idānīṁ tat-pūrvakaṁ kartṛtva-bhoktṛtvādy api avidyāmayam evety āha—sarvam ity ādinā | dehaṁ ca yadā puṁsaḥ sakāśād anyaṁ manyate, tadā puṁso bhoga-sambandho nāsty eva | paraṁ kevalaṁ tat karma tasya bandhāyaiva bhavati ||16||



**mṛṇmayaṁ hi yathā gehaṁ lipyate vai mṛd-ambhasā |**

**pārthivo’yaṁ tathā deho mṛd-ambv-ālepana-sthitaḥ ||17||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **dehopabhogam eva darśayati—mṛṇmayam hīty-ādi dvayena ||17||


**śrīdharaḥ : **dehopabhogāyeti yad uktaṁ tad eva dṛṣṭāntena samarthayati mṛṇmayam ity ādi dvābhyām | mṛd-ambubhyām anna-pāna-rūpābhyām ālepanena sthitir yasya sa tathā ||17||



**pañca-bhūtātmakair bhogaiḥ pañca-bhūtātmakaṁ vapuḥ |**

**āpyāyate yadi tataḥ puṁso bhogo’tra kiṁ kṛtaḥ ||18||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**aneka-janma-sāhasrīṁ saṁsāra-padavīṁ vrajan |**

**moha-śramaṁ prayāto’sau vāsanā-reṇu-kuṇṭhitaḥ ||19||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **dehasya pārthivatva-pāñcabhautikatvoktiḥ mata-bhedena tad idam ubhaya-vidham ajñānam adhyātma-jñānena nirasyata ity āha—aneketi dvayena | vāsanā ajñāna-karmobhaya-vāsanā moha-śramam ajñānajaṁ duḥkham ||19||


**śrīdharaḥ : **bhogair bhujyamānair annādibhiḥ puṁso bandhāyety uktam | tatra hetum āha—aneketi | sahasram eva sāhasram aneka-janma-sāhasrāṇi yasyāṁ tāṁ saṁsāra-rūpāṁ padavīṁ mārgaṁ gacchann asau mohaḥ kartṛtvādy-abhiniveśaḥ, tat-kṛtaṁ śramaṁ prayātaḥ prāptaḥ | yataḥ vāsanā ahaṁ-mameti mithyājñāna-saṁskāraḥ saiva reṇu, tena kuṇṭhitaḥ channaḥ ||19||



**prakṣālyate yadā so’sya reṇur jñānoṣṇa-vāriṇā |**

**tadā saṁsāra-pānthasya yāti moha-śramaḥ śamam ||20||**


**śrīdharaḥ : **kadā tasya śramopaśama ity apekṣāyām āha—praksālyata iti | jñānātmakenoṣṇa-vāriṇā uṣṇodakena hi sukhenaiva antargato'pi malaḥ prakarṣeṇa kṣālyate yadā tadā saṁsāra-pānthasya moha-śramaḥ śamaṁ yāti ||20||



**moha-śrame śamaṁ yāte svasthāntaḥ-karaṇaḥ pumān |**

**ananyātiśayābādhaṁ paraṁ nirvāṇam ṛcchati ||21||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ananyātiśayam anyātiśaya-rahitam | abādham aduḥkhaṁ nirvāṇaṁ mokṣa-sukham ||21||


**śrīdharaḥ : **tataḥ kim ? ata āha—moha-śrama iti | na vidyate andhaḥ atiśayo yasmin tad-ananyāśayaṁ tac ca tad abādhaṁ ca nirupadravaṁ nirvāṇaṁ sukhaṁparaṁ mokṣākhyaṁ prāpnoti ||21||



**nirvāṇa-maya evāyam ātmā jñāna-mayo’malaḥ |**

**duḥkhājñāna-mayā dharmāḥ prakṛtes te tu nātmanaḥ ||22||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **nirvāṇam ātmanaḥ svarūpaṁ, na tu karma-phalavad aupādhikam ity āha—nirvāṇa-maya iti | nirvāṇa-maya evāyam ātmā jñāna-mayo'malaḥ, nirmala-sukha-rūpa-jñāna-rūpa evāyam ātmā | yathoktaṁ—



yathā na kriy jyotsnā malasyākṣālanān maṇeḥ |

doṣāprahāṇān na jñānam ātmanaḥ kriyate tathā || iti | 



na vijñātur vijñāter vipariklopo vidyate, sapadyāvirbhāvaḥ svena śabdāt, yāvad ātma-bhāvitvāt ity ādi |



āgantuka-caitanyādi-guṇaka ātmeti vādād eva bāhyaḥ prakṛtes te tu nātmana iti prāptāprāpta-vivekena prakṛti-sambandha-nibandhanatvāt uktaṁ na tv acetana-dharmāḥ | na hi dehasya kāraṇānāṁ vā sukhatvādy-anusandhāna-sambhavaḥ, puruṣaḥ prakṛti-stho hi bhuṅkte ity ādi-virodhaś ca ||22||


**śrīdharaḥ : **nanv evaṁ nirvāṇasyāgantukatve anityatā prasajyeta ? tatrāha—nivrāṇa-maya eveti ||22||



**jalasya nāgni-saṁsargaḥ sthālī-saṅgāt tathāpi hi |**

**śabdodrekādikān dharmāṁs tat karoti yathā nṛpa ||23||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **atra dṛṣṭāntam āha—jalasyeti | yathā svataḥ śītam ambu śabda-phenādi-rahitam evam ātmā svata eva nirmalānanta-jñānānandaḥ tasyāḥ saṅgād ātmāhaṁ-mānādi-dūṣitaḥ agni-saṁyukta-sthā strī-sthānīyā tāpa-traya-yuktā prakṛtiḥ | tathā prākṛtān dharmān kṣut-tṛṣṇādīn svakīyān manyate bhajate tena duḥkhādikaṁ jāyate ||23||


**śrīdharaḥ : **kathaṁ tasyātmano duḥkhādi-pratītiḥ ? tatrāha—jalasyety-ādi dvābhyām | agni-saṁsargeṇa taptāyāh sthālyāḥ saṅgād antaḥ sthitaṁ jalaṁ śabdam udrekaṁ ca ādi-śabdāc coṣam uṣṇatvādikaṁ ca yathā bhajate ||23||



**tathātmā prakṛteḥ saṅgād ahaṁ-mānādi-dūṣitaḥ |**

**bhajate prākṛtān dharmān anyas tebhyo hi so’vyayaḥ ||24||**


**śrīdharaḥ : **tathā prākṛte dehe sthita ātmā ahaṁ-mānādy-ātma-dharmān bhajae ||24||



**tad etat kathitaṁ bījam avidyāyā mayā tava |**

**kleśānāṁ ca kṣaya-karaṁ yogād anyan na vidyate ||25||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tat kleśa-praśamāyālam iti praśnasya prativacanam āha—kleśānām iti | yogāt \#\#-yogāt ||25||

**  
śrīdharaḥ : **avidyām upasaṁharaṁs tan-nivartakaṁ yogam upakṣipati—tad etad iti | avidyāyāḥ pañca-kleśākhyāyā bījaṁ moha-tamaḥ-saṁjñam ātmāvaraṇājñānam ||25||



**khāṇḍikya uvāca—**

**taṁ tu brūhi mahābhāga yogaṁ yogavid-uttama |**

**vijñāta-yoga-śāstrārthas tvam asyāṁ nimi-santatau ||26||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**keśidhvaja uvāca—**

**yoga-svarūpaṁ khāṇḍikya śrūyatāṁ gadato mama |**

**yatra sthito na cyavate prāpya brahma-layaṁ muniḥ ||27||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **brahma-layaṁ brahmaṇi layaṁ brahma-bhāvam ity arthaḥ | ye karmaṇā devān viyanti itivat | yad vā, mene cātmānam acyutam ||27||



**śrīdharaḥ : **atra yoge sthitaḥ ārūḍho muniḥ brahma-layaṁ prāpya na cyavate punar na aṁarati ||27||



**mana eva manuṣyāṇāṁ kāraṇaṁ bandha-mokṣayoḥ |**

**bandhāya viṣayāsaṅgi muktyai nirviṣayaṁ manaḥ ||28||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **atha yogasya svarūpaṁ karaṇaṁ viṣayaṁ phalaṁ cāha—mana evety-ādibhiḥ ||28||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yoge’vasthitir mano viṣaya-vaitṛṣṇyaṁ vinā na idhyatīty āśayenāha—mana iti ||28||



**viṣayebhyaḥ samāhṛtya vijñānātmā mano muniḥ |**

**cintayen muktaye tena brahma-bhūtaṁ pareśvaram ||29||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **vijñānāt prakṛti-puruṣeśvara-vailakṣaṇya-jñānāt tena mānasena cintayet iti | yoga-svarūpaṁ parameśvaram iti cintayet ||29||

**  
****śrīdharaḥ : **ato mumukṣur evaṁ kuryād ity āha—viṣayebhya iti | vijñānātmā viveka-jñāna-yuktaḥ pumān śabdādibhyo manaḥ pratyāhṛtya tena manaā param īśvaraṁ cintayet ||29||



**ātma-bhāvaṁ nayaty enaṁ tad brahma dhyāyinaṁ munim |**

**vikāryam ātmanaḥ śaktyā loham ākarṣako yathā ||30||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : phalam āha—**ātma-bhāvam** ity-ādinā | **vikāryam** iti anādy-avidyā-karma-vāsanā-dehair baddhasyātmano bhagavaj-jñānena tad-avasthā-nāśaḥ sarva-bhāvanā-nāśaś cātyantika-laya-śabda-vācyaṁ vikāryatvam | evaṁ vikāryam ātmānaṁ cintitaṁ tad brahmātma-bhāvaṁ nayati | ātmano bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ ātma-bhāvaḥ satya-kāmatvādiḥ jakṣan krīḍann ity ādi-vyāpāraś ca, brāhmeṇa jaiminir upanyāsādibhyaḥ \[ve.sū. 4.4.5\] ity ādi-sūtrair vyaktasya muktasya brahmaṇaḥ krīḍādīnām āvirbhāva uktaḥ | atrāpy uktaṁ nirvāṇa-maya evāyam ātmā \[vi.pu. 6.7.22\] ity-ādi | vakṣyati ca—prāpaṇīyas tathaivātmā prakṣīṇāśeṣa-bhāvanaḥ \[vi.pu. 6.7.93\] iti | ākarṣako maṇir āyaskāntaḥ ākarṣako hi loham ātma-bhāvaṁ nayati svasmin tiṣṭhati sthāpayati gacchati gamayati bhramati bhrāmayati, anukṛtes tasya ca kāma-rūpy anusañcaran vatso vā mātaraṁ chāyāvasatyam ity ādi-śruti-śataṁ ca | 



yad vā, doṣākārṣakatvād ākarṣaka ity ādir ucyate—



yathāgni-saṅgāt kanakam apadoṣaṁ prajāyate |

saṅkliṣṭaṁ vāsudevena manuṣyāṇāṁ tathā manaḥ | 

yathāgnir uddhata-śikhaḥ kakṣaṁ dahati sānilaḥ |

tathā citta-sthito viṣṇur yogināṁ sarva-kilbiṣam || \[vi.pu. 6.7.73-74\]



yatheṣikā-tulam agnau protaṁ pradūyate, evaṁ hāsya sarve pāpmānah pradūyante ity ādibhir bhagavato'gni-\#\# uktam | agnivad bhāvo hi kanakasya doṣa-vin\#\#āj jāyate, pūrvaṁ doṣaṁ saṁspṛṣṭaṁ tirohita-sva-prabhaṁ kanakam agnir hi sva-śaktyā sva-samāna-varṇaṁ karoti ||30||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tataḥ kim ? ata āha—ātma-bhāvam iti | cintitaṁ tad brahma evaṁ dhyāyinaṁ puruṣam ātma-bhāvam ātmaikyaṁ nayati vikāryaṁ vikārārhaṁ lohaṁ va-śaktyā ākarṣaḥ ayakānto yathā | ayaṁ tu dṛṣṭāntaḥ aṁyoga-mātre, na tu tad-aikye ||30||



**ātma-prayatna-sāpekṣā viśiṣṭā yā mano-gatiḥ |**

**tasyā brahmaṇi saṁyogo yoga ity abhidhīyate ||31||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : evaṁ saṅkṣipyoktaṁ yoga-\#\#āvaśeṣeṇa vistarato darśayati—ātma-prayatneti | viṣayeṣv anādi-vāsanā-vāsitatvāt paramātmano'tyantāpūrvatvāc ca durārohatvād ātma-prayatna-sāpekṣā viśiṣṭā ekā santatiś ceti vakṣyamāṇa-prakārā viśada-tath\#\#-pratyakṣatāpannā nirastāti\#\#hlāda-rūpā pūrvoktānanta-guṇa-kaṣāya-viśeṣa-viśiṣṭā vā yā mano-gatiḥ, tasyā brahmaṇi saṁyogaḥ yogaḥ | anenātma-paramātmanor yogo yoga iti pakṣo nirastaḥ ||31||



**śrīdharaḥ : **idānīṁ yoga-svarūpaṁ darśayati—ātmeti | ātmanaḥ prayatno yama-niyamādi-viṣayaḥ, tat-sāpekṣā tad-adhīnā viśiṣṭā sattva-mayī yā manaso vṛttiḥ, tayā brahmaṇy eva saṁyogo yogaḥ ||31||



**evam atyanta-vaiśiṣṭya-yukta-dharmopalakṣaṇaḥ |**

**yasya yogasya vai yogī mumukṣur abhidhīyate ||32||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : ukta-prakārātyanta-vaiśiṣṭya-yukto dharma-rūpo yogo yasya sa mumukṣur yogīty abhidhīyate | atra mokṣa-sādhanaṁ yogaḥ sa ca dharma-rūpa iti vadan vākyārtha-jñānaṁ mokṣa-sādhanaṁ jñānam avidheyam iti ca vādino nirasyati ||32||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yogino lakṣaṇam āha—evam iti | evam anena prakāreṇātyanta-vaiśiṣṭya-yukto dharma upalakṣaṇaṁ yasya yogasya sa yayāti sa eva yogī mumukṣuś ca | anya tu kevalaṁ dāmbhika ity arthaḥ ||32||868



**yoga-yuk prathamaṁ yogo yuñjamāno’bhidhīyate |**

**viniṣpanna-samādhis tu paraṁ brahmopalabdhimān ||33||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **idānīṁ yogino’vathā-bhedena traividhyam āha—yoga-yug iti | prathamaṁ yoga-niṣpatteḥ pūrvaṁ tad-arthaṁ yogābhyāṁ kurvan yoga-yug ity ucyate | paraṁ tataḥ paścāt brahmopalabdhimān an viniṣpanna-samādhiḥ kathyate ||33||



**yady antarāya-doṣeṇa dūṣyate cāsya mānasam |**

**janmāntarair abhyasato muktiḥ pūrvasya jāyate ||34||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tayoḥ pūrvasyāneka-janmasv abhyāsān muktiḥ | itarasya tatraivety āha—yady antarāyety-ādi dvayena | antarāyāḥ prakrānta-yogānāṁ yāvad dhāraṇam ālasyādayo daśa dhāraṇātaḥ paraṁ pratipādyāḥ ṣaṭ | tathā ca vāyu-saṁhitāyāṁ—



ālasyaṁ vyādhayas tīvrāḥ pramāda-sthāna-saṁśayaḥ |

anavasthita-citta-\#\# śraddhā bhrānti-darśanam ||

duḥkhāni daurmanasyaṁ ca viṣayeṣu ca lolatā |

daśaite yuñjatāṁ puṁsām antarāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

śānteṣv eteṣu vighneṣu yoga-saktasya yoginaḥ |

upasargāḥ pravartante divyāḥ ṣaṭ siddhi-sūcakāḥ |

pratibhā-śravaṇaṁ vārtā darśanāsvāda-vedanāḥ |

sūkṣme cāntarhite'tīte viprakṛṣṭe tv anāgate ||

pratibhā kathyate yo'rthe pratibhāṣo yathā-tatham |

śravaṇa sarva-śabdānāṁ śravaṇaṁ tv aprayatnataḥ ||

vārtā vārtāsu vijñānaṁ sarveṣām eva dehinām |

darśanaṁ nāma divyānāṁ darśanaṁ cāprayatnataḥ ||

tathā svādaś ca divyeṣu raseṣv āsvāda ucyate |

sparśanādhigamas tadvad vedanānām aviśrutā ||

gandhādīnāṁ ca divyānām ābrahma-bhavanāvadhi || iti |



tathā ahiṁsādi-phala-bhūtās tat-sannidhau vaira-tyāga ity ādinā patañjalinoktaḥ saṅgasyāpādikā siddhayo'ṣṭaiśvaryādyāś ca niṣkāmasyāntarāyāḥ, 



pratimādiṣv aśuddheṣu guṇeṣv āsakta-cetasām |

na siddhyet paramaiśvaryam akṣayaṁ sārvakāmikam || iti vāyūkteḥ ||34||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tayor muktau kañcid viśeṣam āha—yadīti dvābhyām | ālayaṁ vyādhaya tīvrāḥ pramādaḥ thāna-aṁśayaḥ | anavasthita-cittatvam aśraddhā bhrānti-darśanaṁ duḥkhāni daurmanayaṁ ca viṣayeṣu ca lolatety evam-ādy-antarāya-rūpeṇa pūrvaya yoga-yuk-aṁjñaya ||34||



**viniṣpanna-samādhis tu muktiṁ tatraiva janmani |**

**prāpnoti yogī yogāgni-dagdha-karma-cayo’cirāt ||35||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **yogāgni-dagdha karma-samūhaḥ ||35||



**brahmacaryam ahiṁsāṁ ca satyāsteyāparigrahān |**

**seveta yogī niṣkāmo yogyatāṁ sva-mano nayan ||36||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **yogāṅgeṣu prathamaṁ yama-niyamāv āha—brahmacaryam ity-ādi tribhiḥ | brahmacaryaṁ maithuna-tyāgaḥ | niṣiddha-dravyāṇām anādānam aparigrahaḥ ||36||



**śrīdharaḥ : **idānīṁ yama-niyamāna-prāṇāyāma-pratyāhāra-dhāraṇā-dhyāna-samādhaya ity aṣṭau yogāṅgāni krameṇa darśayiṣyan yama-niyamam āha—brahmacaryam ity-ādi tribhiḥ | svakīyaṁ mano brahma-praveśa-yogyatāṁ prāpayan ||36||



**svādhyāya-śauca-santoṣa-tapāṁsi niyatātmavān |**

**kurvīta brahmaṇi tathā parasmin pravaṇaṁ manaḥ ||37||**

**ete yamāḥ saniyamāḥ paṁ ca paṁ ca prakīrtitāḥ |**

**viśiṣṭa-phaladāḥ kāmyā niṣkāmāṇāṁ vimuktidāḥ ||38||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tapa upavāsādi | parasmin brahmaṇi manaḥ-prāvaṇyam eko guṇaḥ | viśiṣṭa-phaladāḥ sakāmānām ||37-38||



**śrīdharaḥ : **parasmin brahmaṇi manaḥ pravaṇaṁ kurvītety anena īśvara-praṇidhānākhyaṁ pañcamaṁ niyamaṁ darśayati ||37-38||



**ekaṁ bhadrāsanādīnāṁ samāsthāya guṇair yutam |**

**yamākhyair niyamākhyaiś ca yuñjīta niyato yatiḥ ||39||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **ādi-śabdena svastikādīni gṛhyante, bhadrāsanādīnāṁ lakṣaṇaṁ yājñavalkyenoktam ||39||



**śrīdharaḥ : **āsanam āha—ekam iti | yamākhyair niyamākhyaiś ca guṇair yutaḥ san | bhadrāsanādīnāṁ lakṣaṇam uktaṁ yogi-yājñavalkīye—



gulphau tu vṛṣaṇayādhaḥ sīvanyāḥ pārśvayoḥ kṣipet |

pārśve pādau ca hastābhyāṁ dṛḍhaṁ baddhvā suniścalam ||

bhadrāsanaṁ bhaved etat sarva-vyādhi-vināśanam || ity-ādi ||39||



**prāṇākhyam anilaṁ vaśyam abhyāsāt kurute tu yat |**

**prāṇāyāmaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sabījo’bīja eva ca ||40||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **sa-bījaḥ sa-garbhaḥ sālambanaḥ bhagavan-mūrti-dhyāna-mantra-japa-yuktaḥ | abījaḥ tad-vidhuraḥ ||40|| 



**śrīdharaḥ : **prāṇāyāmam āha—prāṇākhyam ity-ādi | sa-bījaḥ ālambano bhagavan-mūrti-dhyāna-mantra-japa-sahitaḥ ||40||



**paraspareṇābhibhavaṁ prāṇāpānau yathānilau |**

**kurutaḥ sad-vidhānena tṛtīyaḥ saṁyamāt tayoḥ ||41||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **recakādi-rūpeṇa prāṇāyāmaṁ tridhā darśayati—paraspareṇeti | prāṇena niśvāsena apānasya ucchvāsasyābhibhavo nirodhaḥ prathamaḥ prāṇāyāmo recakaḥ viparītaḥ | pūrakākhyo dvitīyaḥ sa vidhā teneti | sa prāṇāyāmaḥ tena uktena prakāra-dvayena dvidhā | sad-vidhāneneti pāṭhāntare'py evam evārthaḥ | tayor ucchvāsa-niśvāsayor yugapat saṁyamāt tṛtīyaḥ kumbhakākhyaḥ | ete trayo'pi pratyekaṁ mātrābhedās tridhā | yathoktam—



mātrā-dvādaśako mandaś caturviṁśati-mātrakaḥ |

madhyamaḥ prāṇa-saṁrodhaḥ ṣaṭ-triṁśan-mātra uttamaḥ ||

prasveda-kampanotthāna-janakās te yathā-kramam |

jānu pradakṣiṇīkṛtya na drutaṁ na vilambitam ||

aṅgulī-sphoṭanaṁ kuryāt sā mātreti prakīrtitā |

prāṇaḥ sva-dehajo vāyur āyāmas tan-nirodhanam ||

tad recakaḥ pūrakaś ca kumbhakaś ca tridhocyate |

nāsikā-puṭam aṅgulyā nipīḍyaikaṁ pareṇa tu |

audaraṁ receyed vāyuṁ tadāyaṁ recakaḥ smṛtaḥ |

bāhyena vāyunā dehaṁ dhṛtivat paripūrayet |

nāsā-puṭenāpareṇa pūraṇāt pūrako mataḥ |

na muñcati na gṛhṇāti vāyum antar-bahiḥ-sthitam ||

sampūrṇa-kumbhavat tiṣṭhed acalaḥ sa tu kumbhakaḥ |

recakādi-trayābhyāso nāsā-śodhana-pūrvakaḥ | 

svedotkramaṇa-paryantaḥ prokto yogānuśāsane |

agarbhaś ca sagarbhaś ca prāṇāyāmo dvidhā punaḥ |

japa-dhyānaṁ vinā garbhaḥ sagarbhas tat-samanvayāt ||

agarbhād garbha-saṁyuktaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ śatādhikaḥ || iti ||41||



**śrīdharaḥ : **dvividhasyāpi taya punas traividhyam āha—paraspareṇeti | niśvāse nāsikābhyāṁ nirgacchati yo vāyuḥ sa prāṇaḥ | ucchvāsenāntaḥ praviśati yaḥ, so’pānaḥ | tatra prāṇa-vṛttyā apāna-vṛtter abhibhavo nirodho recakākhyaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ | evam apāna-vṛttyā prāṇa-vṛtter abhibhavaḥ pūrakākhyaḥ | evam anena parasparābhibhava-prakāra-dvayena sa prāṇāyāmo dvidhā | anayor yugapat saṁyamāt kumbhakākhya tṛtīyaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ | yad vā, sa dvidhānenety ekam eva padaṁ tatra cāyam arthaḥ | sad-vidhānena sad-gurūpadiṣṭa-mārgeṇa recaka-pūrakābhyāṁ yat parasparābhibhūtaṁ dvayam | yaś ca kumbhakenobhayoḥ sahābhibhavaḥ | evam abhibhava-trayeṇaikaḥ prāṇāyāma iti ||41||



**tasya cālambanavataḥ sthūla-rūpaṁ dvijottama |**

**ālambanam anantasya yogino’bhyasataḥ smṛtam ||42||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **prāṇāyāmaṁ sa-bīja-nirbījatayā dvidhābhipretya tatra sa-bījasyālambanam āha—tasyeti | sthūla-rūpaṁ mūrtaṁ bhagavato rūpam iti vakṣyamāṇaṁ rūpasya sthūlatvaṁ bhagavat-svarūpāpekṣayā ||42||



**śrīdharaḥ : s**a-bījayālambanam āha—taya ceti | sthūlaṁ vakṣyamāṇaṁ hiraṇyagarbhādi-rūpam ||42||



**śabdādiṣv anuraktāni nigṛhyākṣāṇi yogavit |**

**kuryāc cittānukārīṇi pratyāhāra-parāyaṇaḥ ||43||**

**vaśyatā paramā tena jāyate’ticalātmanām |**

**indriyāṇām avaśyais tair na yogī yoga-sādhakaḥ ||44||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : pratyāhāram āha—śabdādiṣv iti ||43-44||



**śrīdharaḥ : **pratyāhāram āha—śabdādiṣv iti | cittānucārīṇi cittālambanād anyālambana-śūnyānīty arthaḥ ||43-44||



**prāṇāyāmena pavane pratyāhāreṇa cendriye |**

**vaśīkṛte tataḥ kuryāt sthitaṁ cetaḥ śubhāśraye ||45||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : prāṇāyāmena pavane pratyāhāreṇa cendriye vaśīkṛte sati cetaḥ śubhāśraye pūrvokta-bhagavat-sthūla-rūpe sthitaṁ kuryāt | anena ślokena dhāraṇoktā ||45||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tasmāt prāṇāyāma-pratyāhāra-pūrvakam eva dhārānām abhyased ity āha—prāṇāyāmeneti ||45||



**khāṇḍikya uvāca—**

**kathyatāṁ me mahābhāga cetaso yaḥ śubhāśrayaḥ |**

**yad ādhāram aśeṣaṁ tad dhanti doṣa-malodbhavam ||46||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tac cetaḥ doṣa-malodbhavaṁ doṣa-malayor udbhavaṁ doṣaḥ kalmaṣaṁ malaṁ rāgādi ||46||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yad-ādhāraṁ ceto doṣa-phalānām antarāyāṇām udbhavaṁ hanti, sa āśrayaḥ kathyatām ||46||



**kaśidhvaja uvāca—**

**āśrayaś cetaso brahma dvidhā tac ca svabhāvataḥ |**

**bhūpa mūrtam amūrtaṁ ca paraṁ cāparam eva ca ||47||869**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : atha śubhāśrayaṁ vakṣyan prathamaṁ heyam aśubhāśrayaṁ darśayati—āśraya iti | cetasa āśrayo brahma, tac ca svarūpato dvidhā mūrtam amūrtam a | mūrtaṁ sa-śarīraṁ hiraṇyagarbhādi-baddha-rūpam | amūrtam aśarīraṁ mukta-rūpaṁ paratvāparatve vyutkrameṇa tayor viśeṣaṇe brahmātmakatvāt tayor brahma-śabda-nirdeśaḥ anayor api bhagavad-rūpatvena dhyeyatva-prasaṅgāt tat-pratiṣedhāya prastāvaḥ ||47||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tam evāha—āśraya iti | ceta āśrayo brahmaiva, tac ca manda-madhyamottamādhikāriṇāṁ yathā-yogyaṁ mūrtāmūrta-parāpara-bhedena caturdhāvasthitam | krameṇa dhāraṇe viṣaye iti darśayitum brahmaṇaś cāturvidhyam āha—tac ca brahma mūrtāmūrtaṁ ceti dvidhā vabhāvataḥ vecchātaḥ mūrtaṁ mūrtimat amūrtaṁ tad-rahitaṁ, tat punaḥ pratyekaṁ paraṁ cāparaṁ ceti dvidhā | tatra parama-mūrtaṁ ṣaḍguṇeśvara-rūpam | paraṁ mūrtaṁ padmanābhādi-līlā-vigraha-rūpam | apara-mūrtaṁ hiraṇyagarbhādi-viśvarūpam ||47||



**trividhā bhāvanā bhūpa viśvam etan nibodhatām | **

**brahmākhyā karma-saṁjñā ca tathā caivobhayātmikā ||48||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **anantaroktaṁ mūrtāmūrtātmakam etad viśvaṁ trividhā bhāvanā bhāvanā-trayātmakam ity arthaḥ | tāṁ bhāvanāṁ nibodha brahmākhyety-ādi brahma-karmādi-viṣayatayā brahmādi-vyapadeśaḥ ||48||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tad evaṁ para-brahmaeśvara-līlā-mūrti-rūpatayā caturdhety uktam | tatra caturthaṁ viśvākhyaṁ rūpam āha—trividhety-ādinā | tirvidha-bhāvanāśraya-jīvātmakatvāt tad-upacāreṇa trividhā bhāvanety ucyate | tad dhi hareḥ thūlaṁ rūpaṁ, ataḥ para-rūpa-prāpty-upāsyatvāt | tatra prathamaṁ manaḥ andāryam iti bhāvaḥ | bhāvanā nāma jñāna-viśeṣajñā vānā | tāṁ trividhām api aṁjñayoddiśati—brahmākhyeti ||48||



**karma-bhāvātmikā hy ekā brahma-bhāvātmikā parā |**

**ubhayātmikā tathaivānyā trividhā bhāva-bhāvanā ||49||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : etad evāha—karma-bhāvātmiketi | bhāva-bhāvanā bhāvo mano-vyāpāraḥ, bhāvena bhāvanaā bhāva-bhāvanā bhāvaḥ padārtho vā ||49||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tām eva viṣaya-traividhyena vivinakti—brahma-bhāvātmiketi | bhāva-bhāvanā bhāvo vastu tad-viṣayā bhāvanā trividhā ||49||



**sanandanādayo ye tu brahma-bhāvanayā yutāḥ |**

**karma-bhāvanayā cānye devādyāḥ sthāvarāś carāḥ ||50||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **keṣāṁ kā bhāvaneti tatrāha—sanandanādaya iti | sthāvarāvarāḥ sthāvara-caraṇāḥ sthāvarāṇāṁ himavad-ādīnāṁ hi karmasv adhikāraḥ śrūyate | bilvā mārdaṅgikā hy āsan krīḍanty oṣadhayaḥ sadā iti ca ||50||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tatra vayaṁ brahmaiva bhavāmaḥ, vayaṁ karmaiva kurmaḥ, vayaṁ punar-ubhayam idam anuandadhma ity evaṁ trividha-bhāvanā-yuktān jīvān udāharati—anandanādaya iti dvābhyām ||50||



**hiraṇyagarbhādiṣu ca brahma-karmātmikā dvidhā |**

**bodhādhikāra-yukteṣu vidyate bhāva-bhāvanā ||51||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **saṁsāra-daśāyām adhikāra-bodha-yukteṣu bhāvanā-trayānvaya ity āha—bodhādhikārīti | adhikāro nāma yat phala-sādhanatvāt mad-artham idaṁ karmeti karmaṇy aiśvarya-bodhaḥ ||51||



**śrīdharaḥ : **bodhaḥ svarūpa-viṣayaḥ | adhikāraś ca sargādi-viṣayaḥ, tad-yukteṣu tad-ubhayānusandhānātmikā dvidhā bhāvanā vidyate ||51||  
 

**akṣīṇeṣu samasteṣu viśeṣa-jñāna-karmasu |**

**viśvam etat-paraṁ cānyad bheda-bhinna-dṛśāṁ nṛṇam ||52||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **viśvam etad uktam artha-rūpaṁ viśeṣa-jñāna-karmasv akṣīṇeṣv ity āha—akṣīṇeṣv iti | viśeṣa-jñānaṁ deva-manuṣyādi-bheda-bhinnatayātmānusandhānaṁ tat-tad-abhimānānurūpaṁ karma viśeṣa-karma | atha parākhyaṁ mūrta-rūpam āha—paraṁ cānyad ity ādinā paramātmana ity antena | bheda-bhinna-dṛśām iti pañcamy-arthe ṣaṣṭhī ye pūrva-śloke akṣīṇa-samasta-viśeṣa-jñāna-karmāṇa uktāḥ, tebhyo bheda-bhinna-dṛgbhyo brahma-sanakādibhyo'nyat tat-parākhyam ||52||



**śrīdharaḥ :**brahma-bhāvanāvanto’pi anandanādayo jīvā eva dehānusandhānānivṛtter ity āśayenāha—akṣīṇeṣv iti | viśeṣa-jñāna-hetuṣu karmasu niḥśeṣam akṣīṇeṣu astu viśvam etad anyat paraṁ brahma cānyad bhāti, bhedena bheda-kareṇa ahaṅkāreṇa bhinna-dṛśām abhyaste’pi dhyātṛ-dhyeya-bheda-darśitvāt sthūla-viśvāntaḥ-pātina evety arthaḥ ||52||



**pratyastamita-bhedaṁ yat sattā-mātram agocaram |**

**vacasām ātma-saṁvedyaṁ taj jñānaṁ brahma-saṁjñitam ||53||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : anyatvam upapādayati—pratyastamiteti | pratyastamita-bhedam aśarīratvena jāty-ādi-bheda-rahitam | ata eva vacasām agocaram sattā-mātram | apakṣayādi-vikara-pañcaka-rahitam | ātma-saṁvedyaṁ svayaṁ-prakāśaṁ jñānaṁ jñāna-guṇaika-nirūpaṇīyaṁ tad-guṇa-sāratvāt iti hy uktam | jñāna-svarūpatvaṁ tv ātma-saṁvedyam ity anena darśitaṁ brahmātmakatvāt brahma-saṁjñitam ity uktaṁ yad evaṁ rūpaṁ jñānaṁ tad brahma-saṁjñitam ity anvayaḥ ||53||



**śrīdharaḥ :**śuddha-brahma-svarūpam āha—pratyastamiteti dvābhyām | pratyastamitaḥ pravilīno bhedo yasmin, tat vacasām agocaram sva-saṁvedyaṁ svānubhava-gamyam ||53||



**tac ca viṣṇoḥ paraṁ rūpam arūpākhyam anuttamam |**

**viśva-svarūpa-vairūpya-lakṣaṇaṁ paramātmanaḥ ||54||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : \+\+\+



**śrīdharaḥ :**viśva-rūpād vairūpyaṁ vailakṣaṇyam eva lakṣaṇaṁ yasya taj jñānaṁ paramātmano viṣṇoḥ paraṁ rūpam ity anvayaḥ ||54||



**na tad yoga-yujā śakyaṁ nṛpa cintayituṁ yataḥ |**

**tataḥ sthūlaṁ hare rūpaṁ cintayed viśva-gocaram ||55||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tad-yoga-yujā yogena prakrāntena cintayituṁ na śakyaṁ tena sthūla-rūpaṁ cintyam ity āha—tata iti | sthūlaṁ pūrvoktam baddha-rūpam ||55||



**śrīdharaḥ :**nanu tarhi śreṣṭhatvād idam eva cintayituṁ yuktam ? tatrāha—neti yoga-yujā prathamābhyāsinā ||55||



**hiraṇyagarbho bhagavān vāsudevaḥ prajāpatiḥ |**

**maruto vasavo rudrā bhāskarās tārakā grahāḥ ||56||**

**gandharva-yakṣa-daity-ādyāḥ sakalā deva-yonayaḥ |**

**manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ śailāḥ samudrāḥ sarito drumāḥ ||57||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **vistareṇa tad eva darśayati—hiraṇyagarbha ity ādinā mūrt\#\# rūpam ity antena ||56||



**śrīdharaḥ : **sthūla-rūpaṁ prapañcayati—hiraṇyagarbha ity-ādi pañcabhiḥ ||56-57||



**bhūpa bhūtāny aśeṣāṇi bhūtānāṁ ye ca hetavaḥ |**

**pradhānādi-viśeṣāntaṁ cetanācetanātmakam ||58||**



**śrīdharaḥ :**viśeṣāntaṁ pṛthivy-antam ||58||  
 

**eka-pādaṁ dvi-pādaṁ ca bahu-pādam apādakam |**

**mūrtam etad dhare rūpaṁ bhāvanā-tritayātmakam ||59||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **śloka-dvayasyaikānvayaḥ | bhāvanā-tritayātmakam etat sarvam ity uktam | etat sthūla-rūpaṁ cintayituṁ śakyam api bhāvanā-tritayātmakam | ato'śuddhatvād aśubhāśraya iti bhāvaḥ | idaṁ viśvam iti viśvam etan nibodhatām ity uktasyopasaṁhāraḥ | jagad etac carācaram ity ādi viṣṇoḥ śakti-samanvitam ity antam ekaṁ vākyam | evaṁ-vidham etaj jagad viṣṇoḥ śaktitvena samanvitaṁ śakti-śarīram | aṁśa iti paryāyaḥ | śarīratayā tat-saṁkalpa-śaktyā vyāptam iti ca asmac-charīravat | kecit etat sarvam iti hiraṇyagarbhādi idaṁ viśvam iti sanandanādi-jagad etad iti sura-narādi ca parāmṛśya idaṁ tritayaṁ viṣṇoḥ śakti-samanvitam iti yojayanti tat-pakṣe bhāvanā-tritayātmakam ity asya pūrveṇottareṇa vā sambandhaḥ ||59||



**śrīdharaḥ :**etāni sarvāṇi carācarāṇi yasmiṁs taj jagad idam idaṁ-kārāspadaṁ viśvākhyaṁ mūrtaṁ hare rūpam ity anvayaḥ ||59||



**etat sarvam idaṁ viśvaṁ jagad etac carācaram |**

**para-brahma-svarūpasya viṣṇoḥ śakti-samanvitam ||60||**



**śrīdharaḥ :**etac ca tattvato viṣṇoḥ svarūpam iti cintanīyaṁ, kintu tac-chakti-vyāptam ity āha—śakti-samanvitam iti ||60||



**viṣṇu-śaktiḥ parā proktā kṣetra-jñākhyā tathāparā |**

**avidyā-karma-saṁjñānyā tṛtīyā śaktir iṣyate ||61||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tatra parā viṣṇu-śaktiḥ pratyastamitety-ādinoktā kṣetrajñākhyā **aparā** hiraṇyagarbha ity ādinoktety āha—viṣṇu-śaktir iti | atha yāgādi-karmākhyam avidyā-paryāyaṁ viṣṇoḥ śakty-antaram āha—**avidyā** iti ||61||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kāsau śaktiḥ yayā vyāptam ? ity ata āha—**viṣṇu-śaktiḥ** viṣṇoḥ svarūpa-bhūtā **parā** cit-svarūpā śaktiḥ | parama-pada-para-brahma-para-tattvādy-ākhyā proktā | pratyastamita-bhedaṁ yat sattā-mātram ity atra prāg uktaṁ svarūpam eva kāryonmukhaṁ śakti-śabdenoktam | idānīṁ parama-śakti-vyāptaṁ bhāvanā-trayātmakaṁ kṣetrajña-svarūpaṁ prapañcayiṣyann āha—**kṣetrajñākhyā iti** | vyāpya-vyāpaka-bheda-hetu-bhūtaṁ viṣṇoḥ śakty-antaram āha—**avidyā iti** | avidyeti karmeti ca saṁjñā yayāḥ sā | tathā ca māyopalakṣyate, hetu-hetumator avidyā-karmaṇor ekīkṛtyoktiḥ, saṁsāra-lakṣaṇa-kāryaikyāt ||61||



**yayā kṣetraja-śaktiḥ sā veṣṭitā nṛpa sarvagā |**

**saṁsāra-tāpān akhilān avāpnoty atisantatān ||62||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tat-svarūpam āha—yayeti | sarvagā karma-nimitta-sarva-śarīragā ||62||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tad evam āha—yayeti | vatutaḥ sarva-gatā api ā kṣetrajña-śaktiḥ yayā avidyayā veṣṭitā āśliṣṭā atī bhedaṁ prāpya karmabhiḥ aṁāra-tāpān prāpnotīty arthaḥ ||62||



**tayā tirohitatvāc ca śaktiḥ kṣetra-jña-saṁjñitā |**

**sarva-bhūteṣu bhūpāla tāratamyena vartate ||63||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tayety-ādi | tāratamyena jñānānanda-tāratamyena ||63||



**śrīdharaḥ : **jīvanāṁ nyūnādhika-bhāve’pi aiva hetur ity āha—tayeti ||63||



**aprāṇavatsu svalpā sā sthāvareṣu tato’dhikā |**

**sarīsṛpeṣu tebhyo’pi hy atiśaktyā patattriṣu ||64||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tāratamyam eva darśayati—aprāṇavatv iti | śilā-kāṣṭhādiṣu ā kṣetrajña-śaktiḥ valpā jñānānandinā, na tu svarūpeṇa | arīṛpeṣu tebhyo’py adhiketi śeṣaḥ | atiśaktyā ati-jñāna-śaktyā adhikety arthaḥ ||64||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tāratamyam evāha—aprāṇavatv ity-ādi ārdhaiś caturbhiḥ | aprāṇavatu anabhivyakta-prāṇeṣu valpā atyantam alpā, thāvareṣu alpā alpato’dhikā, arīṛpeṣu kṣudra-jantuṣu tato’py adhikā, patattriṣu atiśaktyā adhika-śaktyā lakṣyate ||64||



**patattribhyo mṛgās tebhyas tac-chaktyā paśavo’dhikāḥ |**

**paśubhyo manujāś cātiśaktyā puṁsaḥ prabhāvitāḥ ||65||**



**śrīdharaḥ :**patattribhya iti | tac-chaktyā ātmano jñāna-śaktyā prabhāvitāḥ prabhūtāḥ kṛtāḥ ||65||



**tebhyo’pi nāga-gandharva-yakṣādyā devatā nṛpa ||66||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **tataḥ śakrād atiśayitaḥ prajāpatiḥ ||66||



**śakraḥ samasta-devebhyas tataś cāti prajāpatiḥ |**

**hiraṇyagarbho’pi tataḥ puṁsaḥ śakty-upalakṣitaḥ ||67||**

**etāny aśeṣa-rūpāṇi tasya rūpāṇi pārthiva |**

**yatas tac-chakti-yogena yuktāni nabhasā yathā ||68||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **etāny aprāṇavad-ādīni hiraṇyagarbhāntāy aśeṣa-rūpāṇy aviśeṣeṇa asya śarīrāṇīty āha—etānīti | tatra hetum āha—yata iti | yathā hi jīvasya śarīraṁ jīva-saṅkalpa-vyāptaṁ, evaṁ cetanācetanātmakaṁ sarvaṁ bhagavac-chakti-yogena vyāptaṁ niyāmyaṁ dhāryaṁ ca atas tac-charīraṁ śakti-yogeneti śakti-rūpo yogaḥ śakti-yogaḥ śakti-sāmarthyaṁ yogaḥ saṅkalpaḥ | nabhasā yatheti saṅkalpa-nairantaryam uktaṁ mahātmā bhūta-bhāvanaḥ, yathākāśaḥ sthito nityam ity ādi ||68||



**śrīdharaḥ : **asaṅgatve’pi sarva-vyāptau dṛṣṭānto nabhasā yatheti ||68|| 



**dvitīyaṁ viṣṇu-saṁjñasya yogi-dhyeyaṁ mahā-mate |**

**amūrtaṁ brahmaṇo rūpaṁ yat sad ity ucyate budhaiḥ ||69||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **evaṁ bhāvanā-trayātmakaṁ bhagavato mūrtaṁ rūpam uktam | idānīṁ mukta-rūpam amūrtaṁ rūpam ity āha—dvitīyam iti | yat sad ity ucyate sattā-mātram ity ucyate | yogi-dhyeyaṁ niṣpanna-yogena dhyātuṁ tad-viṣṇu-saṁjñasya brahmaṇo mūrtaṁ dvitīyaṁ rūpam ity anvayaḥ ||69||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tad evaṁ mūrtayo rūpayoḥ madhye sthūla-rūpaṁ prapañcitam | amūrtayos tu prathamaṁ rūpaṁ brahmoktaṁ, dvitīyam amūrtaṁ sac-chabdādi-vācyam īśvarākhyaṁ rūpam āha—dvitīyam iti | yogi-dhyeyam ārūḍha-yogibhiś cintyam ||69||



**samastāḥ śaktayaś caitā nṛpa yatra pratiṣṭhitāḥ |**

**tad viśvarūpa-vairūpyaṁ rūpam anyad dharer mahat ||70||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **athokta-śakti-trayasyāstra-bhūṣaṇādi-rūpeṇa nityāśraya-bhūtaṁ jagad eka-kāraṇatayoktaṁ bhagavad-rūpaṁ śubhāśrayatvaṁ vaktum āha—samastā iti | viśva-rūpa-vairūpyam ukta-viśva-rūpa-vailakṣaṇyaṁ rūpam śarīram | anyat dravyāntaram | āditya-varṇaṁ tamasaḥ parastāt, amṛto hiraṇyagarbhaḥ vidyutaḥ puruṣād adhi, mahā-rajataṁ vāsaḥ puṇḍārīkam evam akṣiṇī rukma-varṇaṁ kartāram īśaṁ rūkmābham ity ādi-vacana-siddhaṁ mahat sthūlaṁ guṇato'pi mahattvaṁ vivakṣitam | evaṁvidhaṁ rūpam asyāstīti siddham ||70||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tad eva viśinaṣṭi—samastā iti | etāḥ kārya-mayyaḥ amatāḥ śaktayo yatra īśvare sarva-kāraṇa-bhūte pratiṣṭhitāḥ | ata eva viśva-rūpaṁ viśvaṁ rūpyate yena tat | mahat sarvotkṛṣṭam ||70||



**samasta-śakti-rūpāṇi yat karoti nareśvaraḥ |**

**deva-tiryaṅ-manuṣyākhyā ceṣṭāvanti svalīlayā ||71||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **samasta-śakty-āśrayaṁ tad-rūpaṁ bhagavān eve jagad-upakārāya sva-līlayā deva-tiryaṅ-manuṣyādi-ceṣṭāvanti devādy-avatāra-rūpāṇi karotīty āha—samastety-ādi-dvayena | samasta-śaktīti pada-cchedaḥ samastāḥ śaktayaḥ yasmin tat tathoktam | manvantareṣv aśeṣeṣu devatvenādhitiṣṭhati iti | pratikalpaṁ caturdaśa-devāvatārāḥ trimūrti-madhya-gata-viṣṇv-ādayaś ca matsyādayaś tirya-avatārā rāmādayo manuṣyāvatārāḥ sva-līlayā na tu prayojanāntareṇa | deva-tiryaṅ-manuṣyākhya-ceṣṭāvantīti ca pāṭhaḥ ||71||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tata eṣām āvirbhāvam āha—samasteti | samasta-śakti-yuktāni rūpāṇi | tad eva prakaṭayati—devādy-anurūpa-ceṣṭā-yuktāni devaḥ upendrādiḥ | tiryak matsyādiḥ | manuṣyo rāmādiḥ | ādi-śabdān miśro nṛsiṁhādiḥ ||71||



**jagatām upakārāya na sā karma-nimittajā |**

**ceṣṭā tasyāprameyasya vyāpiny avyāhatātmikā ||72||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **kiṁ ca, jagatām iti | jagatām upakārāya na karma-phala-bhogāya sā janmādi-rūpā ceṣ;a tatra janma rūpā deva-manuṣyādi-sarva-jāti-vyāpinī, yathāha—bahudhā vijāyate iti karma-rūpā vṛndāvana-gokula-kāliya-hrdādi-vyāpinī avyāhatātmikā | rāvaṇa-śiśupāla-bāṇa-śakra-śarvādibhir apratihatā na sā kārmanimittjety anena tri-bhāvanātītatvād avatārāṇām api śubhāśrayatvaṁ darśitam ||72||



**śrīdharaḥ : **līlety uktaṁ samarthayate—jagatām iti | karma-nimittāj jātā hi ceṣṭā paricchinnā sapratighātā ca sā tu karma-nimittajā na bhavati | ataḥ vyāpinī aparicchinnā avyāhatātmikā ca | ataḥ sā ceṣṭā svatantrasyāprameyasyeśvarasya līlaivety arthaḥ ||72||



**tad-rūpaṁ viśvarūpasya tasya yoga-yujā nṛpa |**

**cintyam ātma-viśuddhy-arthaṁ sarva-kilbiṣa-nāśanam ||73||870**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **yadyapy anantasyānanta-baddha-mukta-rūpāṇi santi, tathāpi vyūha-vibhavādi-rūpeṇa sthitaṁ tad eva bhagavato rūpaṁ cintyam ity āha—tad-rūpam iti | sarva-kilbiṣa-nāśanaṁ sarva-karma-kṣaya-karaṁ yata evaṁ vilakṣaṇaṁ yoga-yujābhyāsa-vaśena cintayituṁ śakyaṁ ca ||73||



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhavaty evaṁ pratute kim āyātam ? tatrāha—tad-rūpam iti caturbhiḥ | pūrvokteṣu tad-rūpaṁ tṛtīyaṁ līlā-vigraha-rūpam ||73||



**yathāgnir uddhata-śikhaḥ kakṣaṁ dahati sānilaḥ | **

**tathā citta-sthito viṣṇur yogināṁ sarva-kilbiṣam ||74|| **



**śrīdharaḥ : kakṣaṁ** śuṣka-tṛṇam ||74||



**tasmāt samasta-śaktīnām ādhāre tatra cetasaḥ |**

**kurvīta saṁsthitiṁ sā tu vijñeyā śuddha-dhāraṇā ||75||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tasmāt tatra rūpe dhāraṇāṁ kuryād ity āha—**tasmād** iti | **ādhāra**-śuddhyā **dhāraṇāyāḥ śuddhiḥ** ||75||



**śrīdharaḥ : samasta-śaktīnām ādhāre** āśraye tatra avatāra-rūpe **cetasaḥ** **sthitiṁ kurvīta **||75||



**śubhāśrayaḥ sa cittasya savargasya tathātmanaḥ |871**

**tribhāva-bhāvanātīto muktaye yogināṁ nṛpa ||76||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **śubhāśrayatve tri-bhāva-bhāvanātītatvam | hetum āha—śubhāśraya iti | śuddhāśraya iti ca pāṭhaḥ | svataḥ sarva-gatasya cañcalasya vilakṣaṇa-viṣaye acalātmanaḥ sarva-vilakṣaṇatvāt sa śubhāśrayaḥ | avatāra-rūpāṇy api bhāvanā-trayātītatve mukti-hetutayā ca śubhaśraya iti smṛty-ādibhir uktam—evaṁ yo vetti tattvataḥ | yādṛśe vā manaḥ-sthairyaṁ rūpe badhnāti cakriṇaḥ | nṛsiṁha-vācanādīnām ity-ādinā śaunakaḥ | śrī-sātvate—



daśendriyānanaṁ ghoraṁ yo mano-rajani-caram | 

viveka-śara-jālena śamaṁ nayati yoginām |

dhyeyaḥ sa eva viśvātmā ato'tha jalada-prabhaḥ |

rakta-rājīva-nayano dhanuḥ-śara-karāṅkitaḥ || 



ity-ādinā pratyāvirbhāvam uktam ||76||



**śrīdharaḥ : **sarvagatasyātmanaḥ para-brahmaṇo'py āśrayaḥ pratiṣṭhā | tad uktaṁ bhagavatā gītāsu—



brahmaṇo hi pratiṣṭhāham amṛtasyāvyayasya ca |

śāśvatasya ca dharmasya sukhasyaikāntikasya ca || \[gītā 14.27\] iti |



tribhāva-bhāvanātītaḥ asaṁsāritvāt ||76||



**anye tu puruṣa-vyāghra cetaso ye vyapāśrayāḥ |**

**aśuddhās te samastās tu devādyāḥ karma-yonayaḥ ||77||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : etad-vyatiriktāḥ pūrvoktā baddha-muktā ye te aśubhāśrayā ity āha—anye tv iti | atrāpi śaunakaḥ, 



ābrahma-stava-paryantā jagad-antar-vyavasthitāḥ |

prāṇinaḥ karma-janitāḥ saṁsāra-vaśa-vartinaḥ |

yatas tato na te dhyāne dhyāninām upakārakāḥ |

avidyāntargatāḥ sarve te hi saṁsāra-gocarāḥ |

paścād udbhūta-bodhāś ca dhyānenaivopakārakāḥ |

naisargiko na vai bodhas teṣām apy antato yataḥ |

tasmāt tad amalaṁ brahma nisargād eva bodhavat |

dhyeyam ity ādi |



mahābhārate, brahmāṇaṁ śiti-kaṇṭhaṁ ca ity ādi | etad-antās tu gatayo brahmādyāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ ity ādi manuḥ | karma-yonitvam aśuddhi-hetuḥ ||77||



**śrīdharaḥ : **anyadevatā-nindayā bhagavan-mūrti-dhāraṇām eva dṛḍhīkaroti—anye tv ity ādi dvābhyām ||77||



**mūrtaṁ bhagavato rūpaṁ sarvopāśraya-niḥspṛham |**

**eṣā vai dhāraṇā jñeyā yac cittaṁ tatra dhāryate ||78||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : atha dhāraṇāyā dhyānasya cāśraya-rūpam āha—mūrtam iti | mūrte bhagavato rūpa iti ca pāṭhaḥ | mūrte sthūle ||78||



**śrīdharaḥ :**sarveṣv apy āśrayeṣu āśrayaṇīyeṣv artheṣu niḥspṛhaṁ paramānanda-rūpatvāt citta-viśeṣaṇam ||78||



**tac ca mūrtaṁ hare rūpaṁ yad vicintyaṁ narādhipa |**

**tac chrūyatām anādhārā dhāraṇā nopapadyate ||79||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **anādhārā viśiṣṭālambana-rahitā ||79||



**prasanna-vadanaṁ cāru-padma-patra-nibhekṣaṇam |**

**sukapolaṁ suvastīrṇa-lalāṭa-phalakojjvalam ||80||**



na katame* na vyākhyātam.*



**sama-karṇānta-vinyasta-cāru-kuṇḍala-bhūṣaṇam |**

**kambu-grīvaṁ suvistīrṇa-śrīvatsāṅkita-vakṣasam ||81||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kambu-grīvaṁ rekhā-trayāṅkita-kandharaṁ, suvistīrṇaṁ śrīvatsāṅkitaṁ vakṣo yasya tam ||81||



**valī-tri-bhaṅginā magna-nābhinā codareṇa ca |**

**pralambāṣṭa-bhujaṁ viṣṇum atha vāpi caturbhujam ||82||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : trayo bhaṅgā yasya tat tribhaṅgi balibhis tribhaṅginā ||82||



**śrīdharaḥ : **viṣṇuṁ trayo bhaṅgās taraṅgākārā yasmin tat tribhaṅgi balibhiḥ tribhaṅginā magnā nimnā nābhir yasya tasmiṁs tathā-bhūtenodareṇa copalakṣitam ||82||



**sama-sthitoru-jaṅghaṁ ca svastikāṅghri-karāmbujam |**

**cintayed brahma-bhūtaṁ taṁ pīta-nirmala-vāsasam ||83||**

**kirīṭa-cāru-keyūra-kaṭakādi-vibhūṣitam ||84||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **brahma-bhūtaṁ dhṛta-kāṭhinyam iva dhanībhūtaṁ brahma-mūrtim ||83||



**śārṅga-cakra-gadā-khaḍga-śaṅkhākṣa-valayānvitam |**

**varadābhaya-hastaṁ ca mudrikā-ratna-bhūṣitam ||85||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : atha dhāraṇāṁ viṣaya-bhedena caturdhā darśayati—śārṅgety-ādinā | aṣṭa-bhujatva-pakṣe śārṅgādīni ṣaṭ ṣaṇṇāṁ dhāryāṇi śiṣṭa-bhujayoḥ padma-bāṇau varābhaye vā | caturbhujatve śaṅkha-cakra-gadābjāni tatra śārṅgety-ādinā tāṁ tadety antena astra-bhūṣaṇa-pratyaṅga-pradhānāṅga-catuṣṭaya-viṣayā prathamā dhāraṇoktā | astra-pradhāneyaṁ dhāraṇā ||85||



**śrīdharaḥ : **akṣa-valayam akṣa-mālā aṣṭa-bhujatvaṁ śiṣṭayor bhujayoḥ padma-bāṇau varābhaye vā | caturbhujatve śaṅkha-cakra-gadābjānvitam ||85||



**cintayet tanmayo yogo samādhāyātma-mānasam |**

**tāvad yāvad dṛḍhībhūtā tatraiva nṛpa dhāraṇā ||86||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**vrajatas tiṣṭhato’nyad vā svecchayā karma kurvataḥ |**

**nāpayāti yadā cittāt siddhāṁ manyeta tāṁ tadā ||87||872**



**śrīdharaḥ : **dhāraṇā-dārḍhya-lakṣaṇam āha—vrajata iti | cittād yadā mūrtir nāpayāti, tadā tāṁ dhārānāṁ siddhāṁ dṛḍhāṁ manyeta ||87||



**tataḥ śaṅkha-gadā-cakra-śārṅgādi-rahitaṁ budhaḥ |**

**cintayed bhagavad-rūpaṁ praśāntaṁ sākṣa-sūtrakam ||88||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : tataḥ śaṅkhyety-ādinā sākṣa-sūtrakam ity antena śaṅkhādy-astra-rahita-sākṣa-sūtra-kirīṭādi-bhūṣaṇa-pratyaṅga-pradhānāṅga-viṣayā dvitīyoktā | iyaṁ bhūṣaṇa-pradhānā ||88||



**śrīdharaḥ : **mūrti-dhāraṇām evāyudha-bhūṣaṇādi-parityāgenālambana-saukṣmya-tāratamyenāha—tata iti ||88||



**sā yadā dhāraṇā tadvad avasthānavatī tataḥ |**

**kirīṭa-keyūra-mukhair bhūṣaṇai rahitaṁ smaret ||89||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : kirīṭety-ādinā bhūṣaṇa-rahita-pratyaṅga-pradhānāṅga-viṣayā tṛtīyoktā | iyaṁ pratyaṅga-pradhānā ||89||



**śrīdharaḥ : **avasthānavatī dṛḍhā ||89||



**tad-ekāvayavaṁ devaṁ cetasā hi punar budhaḥ |**

**kuryāt tato’vayavini praṇidhāna-paro bhavet ||90||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : tad-ekāvayavam ity ādinā pradhānāṅga-viṣayā caturthī dhāraṇoktā | āyudha-bhūṣaṇa-pratyaṅgeṣu abhyāsena sudṛḍhaṁ gṛhīteṣu punas tad ekāvayavaṁ teṣāṁ pratyaṅgānāṁ pradhānāvayava-yuktaṁ devaṁ cetasā kuryāt cintayed ity arthaḥ | iyam ekāvayava-pradhānā | atha dhyānam āha—tato'vyavinīti | tato dhāraṇāntaram astra-bhūṣaṇa-pratyaṅga-pradhānāṅgānām āśraye gomukhākāre'vayavini astrādy-anuṣāṅgeṇa dhyāna-paro bhavet ||90||



**śrīdharaḥ : **ekāvayavaṁ pāda-gulphādi-nānāvayava-niṣṭhaṁ citta-dārḍhyam | ekatra niyojya ekāvayavaṁ cetasā kuryāt | tad uktaṁ bhāgavate—



tat sarva-vyāpakaṁ cittam ākṛṣyaikatra dhārayet |

nānyāni cintayed bhūyaḥ susmitaṁ bhāvayen mukham \[bhā.pu. 11.14.43\] iti |



tad evaṁ līlā-dhāraṇaiva sthūla-sūkṣma-krameṇa caturdhoktā | idānīṁ tat-kṛtata evaśarīra-dhāraṇām āha | prasanna-cāru-vadanam ity ādinoktāvayavā yena līlā-mūrtinā āviṣkṛtās tasmin avayavini | yad vā, avayavā līlāvatārā yena gṛhītāḥ, tasmin praṇidhānaṁ citta-sthairyaṁ tat-paro bhavet ||90||



**tad-rūpa-pratyayā caikā santatiś cānya-niḥspṛhā |**

**tad-dhyānaṁ prathamair aṅgaiḥṣaḍbhir niṣpādyate nṛpa ||91||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** :dhyāna-lakṣaṇam āha—tad-rūpeti | tad-rūpa-pratyaya iti ca pāṭhaḥ | tad-rūpa-pratyaye dhāraṇā-siddha-rūpa-viṣaya-pratyaye ekā asadṛśī anya-niḥspṛhā vijātīya-pratyayānantaritā yā santatiḥ pravāhaḥ tad dhyānaṁ ṣaḍbhir aṅgair yamādibhiḥ | evam upāsana-sopāna-krameṇārūḍha-divya-viṣayam idaṁ dhyānam | pūrvatra tasya cālambanavata iti prastutaḥ sālambano yogaḥ | astra-bhūṣaṇādhyāye hy astra-bhūṣaṇa-maya-sarva-śakty-āśraya-divya-vigrahaḥ sa-bīja-yoga-viṣaya iti spaṣṭam uktam—sālambano mahā-yogaḥ sabīja \[vi.pu. 1.22.62\] ity-ādinā ||91||



**śrīdharaḥ : **idānīṁ dhyānam āha—tad-rūpeti | tad-rūpasyaiva dhāraṇā siddhasyaiva vastunaḥ pratyayo yasyāṁ santatau sā ekāvicchinnā santatiḥ | anya-niḥspṛhā viṣayāntareṇa avyavadhīyamānā vijātīya-pratyayānantarita-sajātīya-pratyaya-pravāho dhyānam ity arthaḥ | yac ca prathamair yamādibhir dhāraṇāntaiḥ ṣaḍbhir aṅgair niṣpādyate ||91||



**tasyaiva kalpanā-hīnaṁ svarūpa-grahaṇaṁ hi yat |**

**manasā dhyāna-niṣpādyaṁ samādhiḥ so’bhidhīyate ||92||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : atha dhyāna-paryanta-saptāṅga-janyaṁ nirbīja-yogākhyaṁ bhagavat-svarūpa-viṣayaṁ samādhim āha—tasyaiveti | tasyaiva vigrahādi-viśiṣṭatayā dhyānasyaiva kalpanā nāma-rūpa-varṇāpakṣaya-vināśādayaḥ ayaṁ samādhiḥ pūrvādhyāye para-vidyety uktaṁ vivekaja-jñānam | idaṁ cāstra-bhūṣaṇādi-viśiṣṭa-divya-vigrahavata eva bhagavato'stra-bhūṣaṇādhyāyādiṣu | bibharti puṇḍarīkākṣasyaiva parameśvaraḥ | kalā-muhūrtādi-mayaś ca kālaḥ \[vi.pu. 4.1.84\] ity-ādibhiḥ pratipāditatvāt | astrādīnāṁ rāhityenottarottara-dhyānasya vacanam anyathā tasyāśakyatvāt, na tu tyājyatvāt teṣām astrādi-viśiṣṭa-vigrahavata eva prāpyatvāt tat-kratu-nyāyena teṣām api dṛḍhaṁ dhyeyatva-vacanāc ca ||92||



**śrīdharaḥ :**tasyaiva dhyeyasya kalpanā-hīnaṁ dhyātṛ-dhānya-dhyeyābhedaṁ yathā bhavati, evaṁ yat svarūpa-grahaṇaṁ tad-ekākāratayāvasthānaṁ jñāna-sādhyaṁ samādhiḥ | tad āha patañjaliḥ—



\[eka-\]deśa-bandhaś cittasya dhāraṇā || tatra pratyayaikatānatā dhyānam || tad evārtha-mātra-nirbhāsaṁ svarūpa-śūnyam iva samādhiḥ ||3|| \[yo.sū. 3.1-3\] iti ||92||



**vijñānaṁ prāpakaṁ prāpye pare brahmaṇi pārthiva |**

**prāpaṇīyas tathaivātmā prakṣīṇāśeṣa-bhāvanaḥ873 ||93||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** : uktasya samādhi-rūpa-jñānasya bheṣajaṁ bhagavat-prāptir ity uktam | para-brahma-prāpti-phalam āha—vijñānam iti | idaṁ vijñānaṁ prāpye pare brahmaṇi prāpakaṁ, tathaiva brahmavat bhāvanā-traya-rahito bhagavad-upāsaka ātmā prāpaṇīyaḥ prāpayitavyaḥ, brahma-vid āpnoti paraṁ \[tai.u. 2.1\], vidyayāmṛtatvam aśnute \[ī.u. 11\], bhaktyā tv ananyayā śakyaḥ \[gītā 11.54\], bhaktyā mām abhijānāti \[gītā 18.55\], tat-prāpti-hetur jñānaṁ ca \[vi.pu. 6.5.60\]ity ādi ||93||



**śrīdharaḥ :**niṣpanna-samādher mukti-prakāram āha—vijñānam iti | samādhi-janya-svarūpa-sākṣātkāro vijñānam | prakṣīṇāḥ aśeṣāh pūrvoktāḥ tisro bhāvanā yasya saḥ ||93||



**kṣetrajñaḥ karaṇī jñānaṁ karaṇaṁ tasya tena tat |**

**niṣpādya mukti-kāryaṁ vai kṛta-kṛtyo nivartate ||94||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ** :idaṁ jñānaṁ na kevalaṁ brahma-prāpaka-mātraṁ kiṁ tu mukti-kāraṇam apīty āha—kṣetrajña iti | kṣetrajña anādi-kāla-kṣetra-rūpa-māyā-guṇa-traya-tirohita-svarūpa-rūpaḥ karaṇī karaṇavān samādhi-rūpaṁ jñānaṁ karaṇaṁ taj jñānaṁ tena karaṇatvena tasya kṣetrajñasya mukti-kāryaṁ niṣpādya kṛtakṛtyaṁ nivartate, muktim akṛtvā na nivartata ity arthaḥ ||94||



**śrīdharaḥ : **idaṁ jñānaṁ na kevalaṁ brahma-prāpaka-mātraṁ, kiṁ tu mukti-kāraṇam apīty āha—kṣetrajña iti | kṣetrajñaḥ anādi-kāla-kṣetra-rūpa-māyā-guṇa-traya-tirohita-sva-svarūpaḥ karaṇī karaṇavān samādhi-rūpaṁ jñānaṁ karaṇaṁ taj-jñānam tena karaṇatvena tasya kṣetrajñasya mukti-kāryaṁ niṣpādya kṛta-kṛtyaṁ nivartate, muktim akṛtvā na nivartata ity arthaḥ ||94||



**tad-bhāva-bhāvam āpannas tato’sau paramātmanā |**

**bhavaty abhedī bhedaś ca tasyājñāna-kṛto bhavet ||95||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **mukti-svarūpam āha—tad-bhāva-bhāvam iti | tad-bhāva-bhāvam āpannaḥ tasya parasya brahmaṇo bhāvāḥ apahata-pāpmatvādayo dharmāḥ tāsāṁ bhāvam āvirbhāvam āpannaḥ praptaḥ tadāsau paramātmanā abhedī bhavati | jñānānandādy-ākārair eka-prakāro bhavatīty arthaḥ | bhedo devādi-rūpaḥ, tad-anvayo'sya karma-rūpājñāna-kṛtaḥ, nirañjanaḥ paramaṁ sāmyam upaiti \[mu.u. 3.1.3\], brahmaṇo mahimānam āpnoti, paraṁ jyotir upasampadyavena rūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate, sampadyāvirbhāvaḥ svena-śabdād,mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ \[gītā 14.2\] ity-ādeḥ | svarūpaikya-pakṣe tu dvitīyo bhāva-śabdo nirarthakaḥ | abhedī bhavatīty aya ca punar-uktiḥ, anyad dravyaṁ hi naiti tad-dravyatāṁ yataḥ iti cokta-virodhaḥ ||95||



**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu tarhi vijñānenaiva vyavadhānāt katham ātma-brahmaikyam ? tatrāha—tad-bhāva-bhāvam iti | nanu jñānino'pi bheda-pratītir aty eva | anyathopadeśādy-asiddheḥ ? tatrāha—bhedaś ceti | bādhita eva kathañcid anuvartita ity arthaḥ | tasmād ajñānaṁ tat-kāryaṁ ca saṁsāraṁ vinā svayam eva jñāna-kārya-mano-vṛtti-hatatvād dagdhendhanānalavat ||95||



**vibheda-janake’jñāne nāśam atyantikaṁ gate |**

**ātmano brahmaṇo bhedam asantaṁ kaḥ kariṣyati ||96||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **etad eva vivṛṇoti—vibheda-janaka iti | vibhedo deva-manuṣyādi-rūpaḥ ātmani jñānaika-rūpe devādi-vividha-rūpa-vividha-bheda-hetu-bhūta-karmākhyājñāne para-brahma-darśanenātyantika-nāśaṁ gate sati paramād brahmaṇa ātmano devādi-rūpaṁ bhedaṁ kaḥ kariṣyati ? na ko'pi kariṣyatīty arthaḥ | yathāha śaunakaḥ—catur-vidho hi bhedo'yaṁ mithyā-jñāna-nibandhanaḥ iti ||96||



**śrīdharaḥ : **ajñāne vinaṣṭe sati na punaḥ saṁsāra-praroha-śaṅkety āha—vibhedeti ||96||



**śrī-jīva-govāminaḥ paramātma-sandarbhaḥ \(37\) : **devatva-manuṣyatvādi-lakṣaṇo **vi**śeṣato yo **bhedas** tasya **janake**’py **ajñāne nāśaṁ gatebrahmaṇaḥ** paramātmanaḥ sakāśād **ātmano** jīvaya yo **bhedaḥ** svābhāvika, taṁ **bhedam asantaṁ kaḥ kariṣyati** ? api tu santaṁ vidyamānam eva sarva eva kariṣyatīty arthaḥ | uttaratra pāṭhenāsantam ity etasya vidheyatvād anyārthaḥ kaṣṭa-sṛṣṭa eveti mokṣa-daśāyām api tad-aṁśatvāvyabhicāraḥ svābhāvika-śaktitvād eva | ata evāvidyā-vimokṣa-pūrvaka-svarūpāvasthiti-lakṣaṇāyāṁ muktau tal-līnaya tat-sādharmyāpattir bhavati, nirañjanaḥ paramaṁ sāmyam upaiti \[mu.u. 3.1.3\] ity-ādi-śrutibhyaḥ, 



idaṁ jñānam upāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ | 

svarge’pi nopajāyate pralaye na vyathanti ca || \[gītā 14.2\] iti śrī-gītopaniṣadbhyaś ca ||96||



**ity uktas te mayā yogaḥ khāṇḍikya paripṛcchataḥ |**

**saṅkṣepa-vistarābhyāṁ tu kim anyat kriyatāṁ tava ||97||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**khāṇḍikya uvāca—**

**kathite yoga-sad-bhāve sarvam eva kṛtaṁ mama |**

**tavopadeśenāśeṣo naṣṭaś citta-malo yataḥ ||98||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **yogasya sad-bhāve yogādye kathite sati mama citta-malo'haṁ-mamatādir naṣṭaḥ yataḥ ||98||



**mameti yan mayā coktam asad etan na cānyathā |**

**narendra gadituṁ śakyam api vijñeya-vedibhiḥ ||99||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **kathita ity ādi-śloke mameti-vacanasyāhaṅkāra-mama-kāra-hetu-bhūta-citta-mala-nāśa-vacanena vyāhatiṁ pariharati—mameti | yadyapy ahaṁ-mamatva-hetu-citta-mala-nāśe saty ahaṁ-mamatva-nāśād ahaṁ-mameti-śabda-prayogo na yujyate, tathāpi vijñeya-vedibhiḥ sākṣā-kṛta-paramārthair api tat-prayogaṁ vinā na gadituṁ śakyam ||99||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kuto mama tavopadeśenety etad vacanaṁ vidyata ity ata āha—mameti | mameti yan mayā proktam etad asad eva bādhitānuvṛttyā proktam | anyathā tu vijñeya-vedibhiḥ avagataparamārthair gaditum api na śakyaṁ, kutaḥ punaḥ prārabdha-karma-bhogas teṣām ity arthaḥ ||99||



**ahaṁ mamety avidyeyaṁ vyavahāras tathānayoḥ |**

**paramārthas tv asaṁlāpo gocare vacasāṁ na yaḥ ||100||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **etad eva vivṛṇoti—ahaṁ-mameti | ahaṁ mameti iyaṁ buddhir avidyā anyathā-jñānaṁ tathā vyavahāraḥ pumān strī gaur ayaṁ vājīty-ādi vyavahāro'py anayā avidyayā dvaitādvaitayor abhedaḥ bhrama-kṛta ity arthaḥ | paramārthaḥ avdināśyātmāsaṁlāpyaḥ aja-mahiṣādi-viśeṣa-rahitatayā tat-tac-chabdair anirdeśyaḥ | tatra hetuḥ—gocare vacasāṁ na yaḥ iti ||100||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tat spaṣṭayati—ahaṁ mameti ||100||



**tad gaccha śreyase sarvaṁ mamaitad bhavatā kṛtam |**

**yad vimukti-prado yogaḥ proktaḥ keśidhvajāvyayaḥ ||101||**



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**yathārhaṁ pūjayā tena khāṇḍikyena sa pūjitaḥ |**

**ājagāma puraṁ brahmaṁs tataḥ keśi-dhvajo nṛpa ||102||**



\(101-102\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**khāṇḍikyo’pi sutaṁ kṛtvā rājānaṁ yoga-siddhaye |**

**vanaṁ jagāma govinde viniveśita-mānasaḥ ||103||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **rājānaṁ vana-durga-mantri-bhṛtyādi-svāminaṁ sutaṁ kṛtvā ||103||



**tatraikānta-matir bhūtvā yamādi-guṇa-saṁyutaḥ |**

**viṣṇv-ākhye nirmale brahmaṇy avāpa nṛpatir layam ||104||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **layaḥ nāma-rūpa-karmaṇām ātyantika-nāśaḥ, 



yathā nadyaḥ syandamānāḥ samudre

’staṁ gacchanti nāma-rūpe vihāya |

tathā vidvān nāma-rūpād vimuktaḥ 

parāt paraṁ puruṣam upaiti divyam || \[mu.u. 3.2.8\] iti |



śva iva romāṇi vidhūya pāpaṁ \[chā.u. 8.13.1\], bhidyate hṛdaya-granthiḥ \[mu.u. 2.2.8\], nirañjanaḥ paramaṁ sāmyam upaiti \[mu.u. 3.1.3\] ity-ādeḥ ||104||



**keśidhvajo vimukty-arthaṁ sva-karma-kṣapaṇonmukhaḥ |**

**bubhuje viṣayān karma cakre cānabhisaṁhitam ||105||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **anabhisandhitam anabhisaṁhitaṁ phalam ||105||



**śrīdharaḥ : **mukty-arthaṁ videha-kaivalyārtham anabhisaṁhitaṁ phalābhisandhi-śūnyaṁ loka-saṅgrahārthaṁ karma cakre ||105||



**sakalyāṇopabhogaiś ca kṣīṇa-pāpo’malas tathā |**

**avāpa siddhim atyantāṁ tāpa-kṣaya-phalāṁ dvija ||106||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **amalaḥ kṣapita-prārabdha-karma-viśeṣaḥ ||106||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kṣīṇa-pāpaḥ kṣīṇa-prārabdha-karmā ||106||



|| iti viṣṇu-purāṇe ṣaṣṭhe’ṁśe saptamo’dhyāyaḥ ||



—o\)0\(o—



\(6.8\)





**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**ity eṣa kathitaḥ samyak tṛtīyaḥ pratisañcaraḥ |**

**ātyantiko vimuktir yā layo brahmaṇi śāśvate ||1||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **yā vimuktiḥ eṣa brahmaṇy ātyantiko layas tṛtīyaḥ pratisañcara itthaṁ kathitaḥ ||1||



**śrīdharaḥ : **anantarādhyāya-trayoktātyantika-layopasaṁhāra-pūrvakam āditaḥ sa-praśaṁsaṁ sarva-purāṇārtham upasaṁharann āha—itīty-ādiś caturbhiḥ ||1||



**sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṁśa-manvantarāṇi ca |**

**vaṁśānucaritaṁ caiva bhavato gaditaṁ mayā ||2||**

**purāṇaṁ vaiṣṇavaṁ caitat sarva-kilbiṣa-nāśanam |**

**viśiṣṭaṁ sarva-śāstrebhyaḥ puruṣārthopapādakam ||3||**

**tubhyaṁ yathāvan maitreya proktaṁ śuśrūṣave’vyayam |**

**yad anyad api vaktavyaṁ tat pṛcchādya vadāmi te ||4||**



**śrī-maitreya uvāca—**

**bhagavan kathitaṁ sarvaṁ yat pṛṣṭo’si mayā mune |**

**śrutaṁ caitan mayā bhaktyā nānyat praṣṭavyam asti me ||5||**

**vicchinnāḥ sarva-sandehā vaimalyaṁ manasaḥ kṛtam |**

**tvat-prasādān mayā jñātā utpatti-sthiti-saṁkṣayā ||6||**



\(2-6\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**jñātaś caturvidho rāśiḥ śaktiś ca trividhā guro |**

**vijñātā caiva kārtsnyena trividhā bhāva-bhāvanā ||7||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **trividho rāśiḥ sṛṣṭi-pālana-pralaya-hetavo brahma-dakṣādiḥ, viṣṇu-manv-ādi, rudra-kālāntakādir iti trayo rāśayaḥ | caturvidha iti pāṭhe bhagavatā saha puṁ-pradhāna-vyakta-kālākhyā hi viṣṇu-śaktiḥ | parety-ādy-uktā trividhā śaktiḥ ||7||



**śrīdharaḥ : **caturvidho rāśiḥ, 



catur-vibhāgaḥ saṁsṛṣṭau caturdhā saṁsthitaḥ sthitau | 

pralayaṁ ca karoty ante caturbhedo janārdanaḥ || \[vi.pu. 1.22.22\]



iti prathamāṁśe uktaḥ | pūrvādhyāyoktā hi para-tattveśvara-tad-avatāra-jagad-rūpā trividhā śaktiḥ,



viṣṇu-śaktiḥ parā proktā kṣetra-jñākhyā tathāparā |
