avidyā-karma-saṁjñānyā tṛtīyā śaktir iṣyate || \[vi.pu. 6.5.61\]



ity uktvā trividhā bhāva-bhāvanā brahma-bhāvanā karma-bhāvanā ubhaya-bhāvanā ceti ||7||



**tvat-prasādān mayā jñātaṁ jñeyam anyair alaṁ dvija |**

**yad etad akhilaṁ viṣṇor jagan na vyatiricyate ||8||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **viṣṇor na vyatiricyate tad-ātmakatvena pṛthak siddhy-anarhaṁ jñātam iti śeṣaḥ ||8||



**śrīdharaḥ : **yad viṣṇor na vyatiricyate taj jñeyaṁ jñātam ity anvayaḥ ||8||



**kṛtārtho’ham asandehas tvat-prasādān mahā-mune |**

**varṇa-dharmādayo dharmā viditā yad aśeṣataḥ ||9||**

**pravṛttaṁ ca nivṛttaṁ ca jñātaṁ karma mayākhilam |**

**prasīda vipra-pravara nānyat praṣṭavyam asti me ||10||**

**yad asya kathanāyāsair yojito’si mayā guro |**

**tat kṣamyatāṁ viśeṣo’sti na satāṁ putra-śiṣyayoḥ ||11||**



\(9-11\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**

**etat te yan-mayākhyātaṁ purāṇaṁ veda-sammatam |**

**śrute’smin sarva-doṣotthaḥ pāpa-rāśiḥ praṇaśyati ||12||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **doṣotthaḥ na kevalaṁ buddhi-kṛtaḥ rāgādi-kṛto'pi ||12||



**śrīdharaḥ : **vedaiḥ sammitaṁ tulyaṁ sarva-vedārtha-sāroktaṁ sarve doṣā niṣiddhāḥ kriyāḥ tad-utthāḥ ||12||



**sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṁśa-manvantarāṇi ca |**

**vaṁśānucaritaṁ kṛtsnaṁ mayātra tava kīrtitam ||13||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **vaiśiṣṭya-pradarśanāya kārtsnyena purāṇāṅgāny uktānīti jñāpanārthaṁ punas tāny anvāha—sargaś ceti ||13||



**śrīdharaḥ : **kṛtsna-purāṇoktānuvāda-pūrvakaṁ tac-chravaṇādi-phalaṁ prapañcayati—sargaś cety -ādinā ||13||



**atra devās tathā daityā gandharvoraga-rākṣasāḥ |**

**yakṣa-vidyādharāḥ siddhāḥ kathyante’psarasas tathā ||14||**

**munayo bhāvitātmānaḥ kathyante tapasānvitāḥ |**

**cāturvarṇyaṁ tathā puṁsāṁ viśiṣṭa-caritāni ca ||15||**



\(14-15\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**puṇyāḥ pradeśā medinyāḥ puṇyā nadyo’tha sāgarāḥ |**

**parvatāś ca mahā-puṇyāś caritāni ca dhīmatām ||16||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **dhīmatāṁ jñānināṁ caritāni ||16||



**varṇa-dharmādayo dharmā veda-śāstrāṇi kṛtsnaśaḥ |**

**yeṣāṁ saṁsāmānyādhikaraṇt sadyaḥ sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyante ||17||**

**utpatti-sthiti-nāśānāṁ hetur yo jagato’vyayaḥ |**

**sa sarva-bhūtaḥ sarvātmā kathyate bhagavān hariḥ ||18||**



\(17-18\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**avaśenāpi yan nāmni kīrtite sarva-pātakaiḥ |**

**pumān vimucyate sadyaḥ siṁha-trastair vṛkair iva ||19||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **avaśenāpi yadṛcchayāpi yasya nāmni kīrtite sati yathā akasmād āgataṁ siṁhaṁ dṛṣṭvā hariṇam avaruvantaṁ vṛkāḥ taṁ visṛjya palāyante tadvat ||19||



**yan-nāma-kīrtanaṁ bhaktyā vilāyanam anuttamam |**

**maitreyāśeṣa-pāpānāṁ dhātūnām iva pāvakaḥ ||20||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhaktyā tat-kīrtane phalam āha—yan-nāmeti | dvādaśābdādi-prāyaścittaiḥ pāpam eva vinaṅkṣyati, tat-saṁskāras tv avaśiṣyate | idaṁ tv aśeṣāṇāṁ saṁskārāṇāṁ pāpānāṁ vilāyanaṁ vināśakaṁ na cānyena niḥśeṣa-pāpa-kṣayaḥ syād iti dṛṣṭāntenāha—yathā dhātūnāṁ suvarṇādīnām uttejana-takṣaṇa-prakṣālanādikaṁ dhātv-antara-saṁyogajaṁ nāśayati kiṁ, kiṁtu pāvaka eva, tathā sarvottamam idam evety arthaḥ ||20||



**kali-kalmaṣam atyugraṁ narakārti-pradaṁ nṛṇām |**

**prayāti vilayaṁ sadyaḥ sakṛd yatrānusaṁsmṛte ||21||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **hari-smṛteḥ phalam āha—kali-kalmaṣam iti | yatra yasmin viṣṇau hiraṇyagarbhādibhiḥ sahitam etad brahmāṇḍaṁ meorḥ paramāṇur yathā tathā atyantam alpaṁ yasya sa viṣṇur atra kīrtitam iti saptamenānvayaḥ ||21||



**hiraṇyagarbha-devendra-rudrādityāśvi-vāyubhiḥ |**

**pāvakair vasubhiḥ sādhyair viśvedevādibhiḥ suraiḥ ||22||**

**yakṣa-rakṣoragaiḥ siddhair daitya-gandharva-dānavaiḥ |**

**apsarobhis tathā tārā-nakṣatraiḥ sakalair grahaiḥ ||23||**

**saptarṣibhis tathā dhiṣṇyair dhiṣṇyādhipatibhis tathā |**

**brāhmaṇādyair manuṣyaiś ca tathaiva paśubhir mṛgaiḥ ||24||**

**sarīsṛpair vihaṅgamaiś ca palāśādyair mahīruhaiḥ |**

**vanāgni-sāgara-sarit-pātālaiḥ sadharādibhiḥ ||25||**

**śabdādibhiś ca sahitaṁ brahmāṇḍam akhilaṁ dvija |**

**meror ivāṇur yasyaitad yan-mayaṁ ca dvijottama ||26||**

**sa sarvaḥ sarvavit sarva-svarūpo rūpa-varjitaḥ |**

**bhagavān kīrtito viṣṇur atra pāpa-praṇāśanaḥ ||27||**



\(22-27\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**yad aśvamedhāvabhṛthe snātaḥ prāpnoti vai phalam |**

**mānavas tad avāpnoti śrutvaitan muni-sattama ||28||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **anyadīyāśvamedhe'vabhṛthe snāto yat phalaṁ prāpnoti tad sakalam idaṁ purāṇaṁ prasaṅgataḥ kiñcit śrutvā prāpnotīty arthaḥ ||28||



**prayāge puṣkare caiva kurukṣetre tathārṇave |**

**kṛtopavāsaḥ prāpnoti tad asya caraṇāravindān naraḥ ||29||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **prayāgādau kṛta-māsopavāsādinā yat prāpnoti tad asyaika-deśa-śravaṇāt prāpnotīty arthaḥ ||29||



**yad agnihotre suhute varṣeṇāpnoti mānavaḥ |**

**mahā-puṇya-phalaṁ vipra tad asya caraṇāravindāt sukṛt ||30||**

**yaj jyeṣṭha-śukla-dvādaśyāṁ snātvā vai yamunā-jale |**

**mathurāyāṁ hariṁ dṛṣṭvā prāpnoti puruṣaḥ phalam ||31||**

**tad āpnoty akhilaṁ samyag adhyāyaṁ yaḥ śṛṇoti vai |**

**purāṇasyāsya viprarṣe keśavārpita-mānasaḥ ||32||**



\(30-32\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**yamunā-salila-snātaḥ puruṣo muni-sattama |**

**jyeṣṭhā-mūle site pakṣe dvādaśyāṁ samupoṣitaḥ ||33||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **mathurāyāṁ hariṁ dṛṣṭvā yat phalaṁ paramāṁ ca gatiṁ prāpnotīty ukte tatra kiṁ phalaṁ prāpnotīty apekṣāyām āha—yamunā-salila ity-ādi dvābhyām | jyeṣṭhā-nakṣatraṁ pūrṇimā-yuktaṁ mūlaṁ prvṛtti-hetur yasyāsau jyeṣṭhā-mūlaḥ jyeṣṭha-āsaḥ tasmin śukla-pakṣe ||33||



**samabhyarcyācyutaṁ samyaṅ mathurāyāṁ samāhitaḥ |**

**aśvamedhasya yajñasya prāpnoty avikalaṁ phalam ||34||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**ālokya rddhi-mathāny eṣām unnītānāṁ sva-vaṁśajaiḥ |**

**etat kilocur anyeṣāṁ pitaraḥ sapitāmahāḥ ||35||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **atrārthe pitṛ-gītāḥ pramāṇayann āha—ālokyety-ādi caturbhiḥ ||35|



**kaccid asmat-kule jātaḥ kālindī-salilāplutaḥ |**

**arcayiṣyati govindaṁ mathurāyām upoṣitaḥ ||36||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**jyeṣṭhā-mūle site pakṣe yenaiva vayam apy uta |**

**parām ṛddhim avāpsyāmas tāritāḥ sva-kulodbhavaiḥ ||37||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **kenaivaṁ vayam apy uteti kena vā puruṣeṇa evaṁ mathurāyāṁ kṛta-govinda-pūjanena vayaṁ tāritāḥ parām ṛddhim apavarga-rddhim avāpsyāmaḥ ||37||



**jyeṣṭhā-mūle site pakṣe samabhyarcya janārdanam |**

**dhanyānāṁ kulajaḥ piṇḍān yamunāyām pradāsyati ||38||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**tasmin kāle samabhyarcya tatra kṛṣṇaṁ samāhitaḥ |**

**dattvā piṇḍaṁ pitṛbhyaś ca yamunā-salilāplutaḥ ||39||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **samādhānena kīrtanād yat phalam uktaṁ tad eva samāhtaḥ san śrutvāpi prāpnotīty āha—tasmin kāla ity-ādi dvābhyām ||39||



**yad āpnoti naraḥ puṇyaṁ tārayan sva-pitāmahān |**

**śrutvādhyāyaṁ tad āpnoti purāṇasyāsya bhaktitaḥ ||40||**

**etat saṁsāra-bhīrūṇāṁ paritrāṇam anuttamam |**

**śrāvyāṇāṁ paramaṁ śrāvyaṁ pavitrāṇām anuttamam ||41||**

**duḥkha-praṇāśanaṁ nṝṇāṁ sarva-duṣṭa-nibarhaṇam |**

**maṅgalaṁ maṅgalānāṁ ca putra-sampat-pradāyakam ||42||**



\(40-42\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**idam ārṣaṁ purā prāha ṛbhave kamalodbhavaḥ |**

**ṛbhuḥ priyavratāyāha sa ca bhṅuraye’bravīt ||43||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **etat purāṇa-sampradāyaṁ kathayann āha—idam ārṣam ity-ādinā | ṛṣir nārāyaṇaḥ | tena proktam ārṣam ||43||



**bhāguriḥ stambhamitrāya dadhīcāya sa coktavān |**

**sārasvatāya tenoktaṁ bhṛguḥ sārasvatena ca ||44||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhṛguḥ prāptavān iti śeṣaḥ ||44||



**bhṛguṇā purukutsāya narmadāyai sa coktavān |**

**narmadā dhṛtarāṣṭrāya nāgāyāpūraṇāya ca ||45||**

**tābhyām ca nāgarājāya proktaṁ vāsukaye dvija |**

**vāsukiḥ prāha vatsāya vatsaś cāśvatarāya vai ||46||**

**kambalāya ca tenoktam elā-putrāya tena vai ||47||**

**pātālaṁ samanuprāptas tato vedaśirā muniḥ |**

**prāptavān etad akhilaṁ sa ca pramataye dadau ||48||**

**dattaṁ pramatinā ca taj jātukarṇāya dhīmate |**

**jātukarṇena caivoktam anyeṣāṁ puṇya-karmaṇām ||49||**



*na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**pulastya-vara-dānena mamāpy etat smṛtiṁ gatam |**

**mayāpi tubhyaṁ maitreya yathāvat kathitaṁ tv idam ||50||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ :**mamāpyetat smṛtiṁ gatam iti mahyaṁ sārasvatena ceti \[vi.pu. 1.2.9\] pūrvam uktam upajīvyocyate \[?\} | \#\# kṛta-yuge sarva-purāṇānāṁ saṁgraha-rūpasya \#\# dakṣādi \#\# kutsāntaḥ sampradāyaḥ parāśarasya tretāyāṁ \#\# viṣṇu-purāṇaṁ kurvataḥ prāg-ukta-kāla-dairghya-\#\#—cchede punaḥ parāśara-rṣi-dṛṣṭyaiva tat purāṇaṁ brahmaṇaiva ṛg aspaṣṭam



**tvam apy etac chinīkāya kaler ante vadiṣyasi ||51||**

**ity etat paramaṁ guhyaṁ kali-kalmaṣa-nāśanam |**

**yaḥ śṛṇoti naro bhaktyā sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ||52||**

**samasta-tīrtha-snānāni samastāmara-saṁstutiḥ |**

**kṛtā tena bhaved etad yaḥ śṛṇoti dine dine ||53||**

**kapilādāna-janitaṁ puṇyam atyanta-durlabham |**

**śrutvaitasya daśādhyāyān avāpnoti na saṁśayaḥ ||54||**



\(51-54\) *na katareṇa vyākhyātam.*



**yas tv etat sakalaṁ śṛṇoti puruṣaḥ kṛtvā manasy acyutaṁ**

**sarvaṁ sarva-mayaṁ samasta-jagatām ādhāram ātmāśrayam |**

**jñāna-jñeyam anādi-manda-rahitaṁ sarvāmarāṇāṁ hitam **

**sa prāpnoti na saṁśayo’sty avikalaṁ yad vāji-medhe phalam ||55||**



viṣṇucittaḥ : aspaṣṭam



**śrīdharaḥ : **kṛtvā manasyacyutamity-ādeḥ śrotṛviśeṣaṇavadvājimedha ityatrānuṣaṅga, ato'yamarthaḥ evambhūtamacyutaṁ manasi kṛtvā aśvamedha kṛta yat phalaṁ tat sakalaṁ prāpnotīti | tataś ca pūrvoktādekadeśa śravaṇakīrtanādeḥ samastaśravaṇe phalabhūyastavamuktaṁ bhavati ||55||



**yatrādau bhagavāṁś carācara-gurur madhye tathānte ca saḥ**

**brahma-jñāna-mayo’cyuto’khila-jagan-madhyānta-sarga-prabhuḥ |**

**tat sarvaṁ puruṣaḥ pavitram amalaṁ śṛṇvan paṭhan vācayan**

**prāpnoty asti na tat-phalaṁ tribhuvaneṣv ekānta-siddhir hariḥ ||56||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **pavitraramaṁ pavitreṣu śreṣṭhaṁ śṛnvan paṭhan yat prāpnoti, na tat kutrāpyasti | yasmādekāntā niyatā sarvapāpakṣayādidvārā saddhirvimuktiḥ yasmāt tat prāpyaphalam | na ca harilakṣaṇaphalam svargādilokeṣvastīty arthaḥ ||56||



**yasmin nyasta-matir na yāti narakaṁ svargo’pi yac-cintane**

**vighno yatra niveśitātma-manasāṁ874 brāhmo’pi loko’lpakaḥ |**

**muktiṁ cetasi yaḥ sthito’mala-dhiyāṁ puṁsāṁ dadāty avyayaḥ**

**kiṁ citraṁ yad aghaṁ prayāti vilayaṁ tatrācyute kīrtite ||57||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **aspaṣṭam mano-niveśena dhyānaṁ, bhagavati cetaḥ-sthitiḥ samādhiḥ ||57||



**śrīdharaḥ : **hari-kīrtana-mātreṇasarva-pāpa-kṣayo bhavatīti yad uktaṁ tat kaimutya-nāyenopapādayati**—yasmin **iti** | **nyastā nikṣiptā matir yena acyutaika-citta iti yāvat | sa-pramāda-kṛtair aghair narakaṁ na yāti | tasmin pāpa-saṁśleṣābhāvāt | yasya cintane kriyamāṇaṁ svarga-prāptir api vighna-prāyā yasmin niveśitaḥ ātmā manaś ca sa samādhinā yena tasya brahma-loko'py atitucchaḥ | yathā-kathaṁcid api yaś cetasi sthito mukim eva dadāti yadaivaṁ svārthaṁ kevalaṁ mano-mātreṇācyuta-niṣṭhānām īdṛśaṁ phala-gauravaṁ tadā tan-nāma-kīrtanena pareṣām apy aghaṁ vilayaṁ prayāti svakīyāgha-nāśaḥ kiṁ citram ity arthaḥ ||57||



**yajñair yajña-vido yajanti satataṁ yajñeśvaraṁ karmiṇo**

**yaṁ vai brahma-mayaṁ parāvara-mayaṁ dhyāyanti ca jñāninaḥ |**

**yaṁ sañcintya na jāyate na mriyate no vardhate hīyate **

**naivāsan na ca sad bhavaty ati tataḥ kiṁ vā hareḥ śrūyatām ||58||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **na jāyate iti | śarīra-parigraho janma tat-tyāgo maraṇam | vṛddhi-hrāso jñānataḥ naivāsan na ca sad iti kāraṇatva-kāryatva-nirāsaḥ | tataḥ hareḥ ati atikrameṇa kiṁ vā śrūyatāṁ tad adhikaṁ na kiñcit śrūyata ity arthaḥ ||58||



**śrīdharaḥ : **ato harir eva śrotavyaḥ sarva-pūjyatvād ity āha—yajñair ity ādi dvābhyām | naivāsan na ca sad iti kāryaṁ kāraṇaṁ ca na bhavati | pitṛ-putrādi-bhāvena saṁsarati tato harer ati atikrameṇa kiṁ śrūyatām ||58||



**kavyaṁ yaḥ pitṛ-rūpa-dhṛg-vidhi-hutaṁ havyaṁ ca bhuṅkte vibhur**

**devatve bhagavān anādi-nidhanaḥ svāhā-svadhā-saṁjñite |**

**yasmin brahmaṇi sarva-śakti-nilaye875 mānāni no mānināṁ **

**niṣṭhāyai prabhavanti hanti kaluṣaṁ śrotraṁ sa yāto harir ||59||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **sva-nāmādi-dvārā harir eva śrotavya ity āha—kavyam iti | mānināṁ pramāṇavatāṁ mānāni niṣṭhāyai paricchedāya na prabhavanti na samarthāni bhavanti ||59||



**śrīdharaḥ : **vipramukhe vidhinā hutaṁ kavyaṁ devatvena vartamāno havyaṁ ca yo bhuṅkte mānāni yasmin niṣṭhāyai paricchedāya na samarthāni sva-prakāśatvāt | hariḥ śrotraṁ prāptaḥ kaluṣaṁ hanti tasmāt sa eva śrotavya ity arthaḥ ||59||



**nānto’sti yasya na ca yasya samudbhavo’sti**

**vṛddhir na yasya pariṇāma-vivarjitasya |**

**nāpakṣayaṁ ca samupaitya vikalpa-svastu**

**yas taṁ nato’smi puruṣottamam ādyam īḍyam ||60||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **atha śāstraṁ samāpayiṣyann īśvara-puruṣa-pradhāna-vyaktāni maṅgalāya praṇamati—nānto'stīty-ādi-caturbhiḥ | tatrāyaṁ prathama-ślokaḥ śubhāśrayatvenokta-divya-vigraha-viśiṣṭeśvara-viṣayaḥ | kālo'pīśvare'natar-bhūtaḥ ||60||



**śrīdharaḥ : **purāṇa-samāptau bhagavataḥ sṛṣṭy-ādy-upayogāya pratipāditaṁ parameśvara-puruṣa-pradhāna-vyaktākhya-rūpa-catuṣṭayaṁ praṇamati—nāta ity ādi caturbhiḥ | vikāri-vikalpaṁ vastu brahmaiva yataḥ kālo'pi īśvarāntar-bhūtaḥ, taṁ nato'smi ||60|||



**tasyaiva yo’nuguṇa-bhug bahudhaika eva **

**śuddho’py aśuddha iva bhāti hi mūrti-bhedaiḥ876 |**

**jñānānvitaḥ sakala-sattva877-vibhūti-kartā **

**tasmai nato’smi puruṣāya sadāvyayāya ||61|| **



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **dvitīyena ślokena tasya puruṣa-rūpaṁ namaskaroti—tasyaiveti | yaḥ puruṣaḥ tasyaivānuguṇa-bhuk śeṣa-bhūta ity arthaḥ | ekaḥ devādi-bheda-rahitaḥ jñānaika-svarūpaḥ svataḥ śuddho'pi prākṛta-deheṣv ātma-bhramāt tad-dharma-yuktatayā bhānād aśuddha iva bhāti | jñānānvitaḥ jñāna-dharmakaḥ tanv-ādīnāṁ mahad-ādīnāṁ vibhūter vistarasya karma-dvārā kartā | sakala-tattva-vibhūti-karteti ca pāṭhaḥ ||61||



**śrīdharaḥ : **tasyaivānu parameśvarāt samanataraṁ puruṣa eka eva, tathāpi bahudhā brahmādi-rūpeṇa śuddho'py aśuddha iva sṛṣṭy-ādiṣv āsakta iva mūrti-vibhāgānāṁ dakṣādi-manv-ādi-rūpāṇāṁ bhedaiḥ sarva-sattvānāṁ vibhūti-kartā vistāra-kṛt ||61||



**jīva-gosvāmī :**atra tasyaiva anu pūrvoktāt parameśvarāt samanantaram | bahudhā brahmādi-rūpeṇa | aśuddha iva sṛṣṭy-ādiṣv āsakta iva | mūrti-vibhāgānāṁ dakṣādi-manv-ādi-rūpāṇāṁ bhedaiḥ | sarva-sattvānāṁ vibhūti-kartā vistāra-kṛt iti svāmī | \(paramātma-andarbha 1\)



**jñāna-pravṛtti-niyamaikya-mayāya puṁso**

**bhoga-pradāna-paṭave triguṇātmakāya |**

**avyākṛtāya bhava-bhāvana-kāraṇāya **

**vande svarūpa-bhavanāya sadājarāya ||62||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **pradhāna-svarūpam āha—jñāneti | jñāna-pravṛtti-niyamāḥ sattvādīnāṁ kāryāni niyamaḥ stambho jñāna-saṅkocaś ca eṣām aikyam | ekatra layaḥ tad-rūpāya guṇa-sāmyāvasthāyāṁ hi tat-tat-kāryāṇi na bhāv3i avyākṛtāya anudbhūta-mahad-ādy-avasthāya pradhānāyety arthaḥ | bhava-bhāvana-kāraṇāya bhavaḥ saṁsāraḥ, tad-bhāvanasya karmaṇaḥ kāraṇāya svarūpa-bhavanāya svarūpeṇa bhavanaṁ yasya tat svarūpa-bhavanaṁ svataḥ-siddhāya ādi-rahitāyety arthaḥ ||62||



**śrīdharaḥ : **jñānaṁ ca pravṛttiś ca tayor niyamaś ca tayoḥ saṅkocaḥ tadaikya-mayāya | tatra hetuḥ—triguṇātmakāyeti | triguṇa-svarūpa-bhāvanāya triguṇa-svarūpa-bhūtāyeti vā avyākṛta-svarūpaṁ vande ||62||



**vyomānilāgni-jala-bhū-racanāmayāya**

**śabdādi-bhogya-viṣayopanaya-kṣamāya |**

**puṁsaḥ samasta-karaṇair upakārakāya**

**vyaktāya sūkṣma-bṛhad-ātmavate nato’smi ||63||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **tasyaiva vyaktākhyaṁ rūpam āha-vyometi | sūkṣma-bṛhad-ātmavate sūkṣmaṁ mahad-ādi bṛhat pṛthivy-ādi | ātmā atra ātma-śabdaḥ svarūpa-vacanaḥ ||63||



**śrīdharaḥ : **vyaktāya prapañca-svarūpāya sūkṣmeṇa brahma-svarūpeṇa | vimalāya pāṭhāntare sūkṣme avyakte vilayo yasyety arthaḥ | sūkṣma-bṛhad-ātmavata iti pāṭhe sūkṣmaṁ mahad-ādi bṛhat pṛthivy-ādi ātma-śabdaḥ svarūpa-vācī ||63||



**iti vividham ajasya yasya rūpaṁ**

**prakṛti-parātma-mayaṁ sanātanasya |**

**pradiśatu bhagavān aśeṣa-puṁsāṁ**

**harir apajanma-jarādikāṁ sa siddhim ||64||**



**viṣṇucittaḥ : **athaivam upapāditāt svetara-samasta-cid-acid-vastu-śarīrāt puruṣottamāt sarva-puṁsāṁ parama-puruṣārthaṁ mokṣam āśāsānaḥ purāṇaṁ pūrayati—itīti | iti ukta-prakāreṇa prakṛti-parātma-mayaṁ prakṛtir vyaktāvyaktātmikā tasyāḥ param aprākṛta-divya-śarīram ātmā puruṣaḥ | prakṛti-parātmavata iti ca pāṭhaḥ | atra prakṛti-puruṣayoḥ parasmād bhedaḥ tayor jagad-brahmā-samānādhikaraṇya-nibandhanaṁ tad-rūpatvam | aśeṣa-puṁsām iti nirdeśāt ātmanāṁ paraspara-bhedaḥ bhagavataḥ apajanma-jarādika-siddhi-pradeṣṭṛtva-vacanena sa eva mokṣa-prada ity-ādy-uktam ity anusandheyam ||64||



iti śrī-rāmānuja-yatīśvara-caraṇa-saroja-cañcarīka-śrī-viṣṇucittārya-prasādite śrī-viṣṇu-mahā-purāṇa-vyākhyāne ṣaṣṭhāṁśe'ṣṭamo'dhyāyaḥ ||



iti śrī-viṣṇu-mahā-purāṇe viṣṇucittīya-vyākhyānaṁ samāptam ||



**śrīdharaḥ : **idānīm ukta-catuḥ-svarūpād bhagavataḥ samasta-jīvānām etat-purāṇa-śravaṇādi-dvārā mokṣam āśāsānaḥ purāṇaṁ nigamayati—itīti | iti prakṛti-parātma-mayaṁ prakṛtir vyaktāvyakta-rūpā, para īśvara ātmā puruṣaḥ tan-mayaṁ, apagata-janma-jarādikāṁ mokṣa-lakṣaṇāṁ siddhiṁ pradiśatv ity āśīrvādaḥ ||64|| 



iti śrīmad-viṣṇu-bhakta-śiroratna-śrīdhara-svāmi-viracitātma-prakāśākhya-śrī-viṣṇu-mahā-purāṇa-vyākhyāyāṁ ṣaṣṭhāṁśe'ṣṭamo'dhyāyaḥ ||8||



iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe ṣaṣṭhe’ṁśe aṣṭamo’dhyāyaḥ 



—o\)0\(o—



\(6.9\)





ayam adhyāyo nāga-saṁskaraṇe na prāpyate. tasya viṣṇu-cittīya-vyākhyā nāsti. anyataḥ śrīdharīya-vyākhyā prāptā.

## śiṣya-paramparā-kathanaṁ, viṣṇu-purāṇasya māhātmyam upasaṁhāraś ca 



**parāśara uvāca—**

**ity eṣa kathitaḥ samyak tṛtīyaḥ pratisañcaraḥ |**

**ātyantikī vimuktir yā layo brahmaṇi śāśvataḥ ||1||**

**sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṁśo manvantarāṇi ca |**

**vaṁśānucaritaṁ caiva bhavato gaditaṁ mayā ||2||**

**purāṇaṁ vaiṣṇavaṁ ceitat sarva-kilbiṣa-nāśanam |**

**viśiṣṭaṁ sarva-śāstrebhyaḥ puruṣārthaupapādikam ||3||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **anantarādhyāyoktātyantika-layopaṁhāra-pūrvakam ādita tat praśaṁan sarva-purāṇārtham upaṁharann āha—itīti caturbhiḥ | brahmaṇi laya-rūpā yā vimuktiḥ sa evātyantikaḥ pratisañcaraḥ kathita ity anvayaḥ ||1-3||



**tubhyaṁ yathāvan maitreya proktaṁ śuśrūṣave’vyayam |**

**yad anyad api vaktavyaṁ tat pṛcchādya vadāmi te ||4||**



**maitreyauvāca—**

**bhagavan kathitaṁ sarvaṁ yat pṛṣṭo’si mayā mune |**

**śrutaṁ caitan mayā bhaktyā nānyat praṣṭavyam asti te ||5||**

**vicchinnāḥ sarva-sandehā vaimalyaṁ manasaḥ kṛtam |**

**tvat-prasādān mayā jñātā utpatti-sthiti-saṁyamāḥ ||6||**

**jñātaś caturvidho rāśiḥ śaktiś ca trividhā guro |**

**vijñātā cāpi kārtsyena trividhā bhāva-bhāvanā ||7||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **caturvidho rāśiḥ |



catur-vibhāgaḥ an ṛṣṭau caturdhā saṁsthitaḥ sthitau |

pralayaṁ ca karoty ante caturbhedo janārdanaḥ || \[vi.pu. 1.22.22\] iti prathamāṁśokteḥ ||7||



**tvat-prasādān mayā jñātaṁ jñeyam anyair alaṁ dvija |**

**yathaitad akhilaṁ viṣṇor jagan na vyatiricyate ||8||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **yathā jagad viṣṇor vyatiricyate, tathā jñātam ity anvayaḥ ||8||



**kṛtārtho’smy apasandehas tvat-prasādān mahā-mune |**

**varṇa-dharmādayo dharmā viditā yad aśeṣataḥ ||9||**

**pravṛttaṁ ca nivṛttaṁ ca jñātaṁ karma mayākhilam |**

**prasīda vipra-pravara nānyat praṣṭavyam asti me ||10||**

**yad asya kathanāyāsair yojito’si mayā guro | **

**tat kṣamyatāṁ viśeṣo’sti na sutāṁ putra-śiṣyayoḥ ||11||**



**parāśara uvāca—**

**etat te yan mayākhyātaṁ purāṇaṁ veda-sammitam |**

**śrute’smin sarva-doṣottha-pāpa-rāśiḥ praśāmyati ||12||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **vedaiḥ ammitaṁ tulitaṁ, sarva-vedārtha-āroktaiḥ | sarve doṣā niṣiddhāḥ kriyāḥ tad-utthaḥ ||12||



**sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṁśo manvantarāṇi ca |**

**vaṁśānucaritaṁ kṛtsnaṁ mayātra tava kīrtitam ||13||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kṛtna-purāṇārthānuvāda-pūrvakaṁ tac-chravaṇādi-phalaṁ prapañcayati—argaś cety -ādinā ||13||



**atra devās tathā daityā gandharvoraga-rākṣasāḥ |**

**yaksā vidyādharāḥ siddhāḥ kathyante’psarasas tathā ||14||**

**munayā bhāvitātmānaḥ kathyante tapasānvitāḥ |**

**cāturvarṇyaṁ yathā puṁsāṁ viśiṣṭa-caritā narāḥ ||15||**

**puṇyāḥ pradeśā medinyāḥ puṇyā nadyo’tha sāgarāḥ |**

**parvatāś ca mahā-puṇyāś caritāni ca dhīmatām ||16||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **dhīmatāṁ jñānināṁ caritāni ca ||16||



**varṇa-dharmādayo dharmā veda-dharmāś ca kṛtsnaśaḥ |**

**yeṣāṁ saṁcaraṇāravindān sadyaḥ sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ||17||**

**utpatti-sthiti-nāśānāṁ hetur yo jagato’vyayaḥ |**

**sa sarva-bhūtaḥ sarvātmā kathyate bhagavān hariḥ ||18||**

**avaśenāpi yan-nāmni kīrtite sarva-pātakaiḥ |**

**pumān vimucyate sadyaḥ siṁha-trastair vṛkair iva ||19||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **avaśenāpi yadṛcchayāpi yaya nāmni kīrtite ati | yathākamād āgatam iṁhaṁ dṛṣṭvā tratā hariṇam avarundhanto vṛkāḥ taṁ viṛjya palāyante, tadvat ||19||



**yan-nāma kīrtite bhaktyā vilāpanam anuttamam |**

**maitreyāśeṣa-pāpānāṁ dhātūnām iva pāvakaḥ ||20||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhaktyā tat-kīrtane phalam āha—yan-nāmeti | dvādaśābda-prāyaścittaiḥ pāpam eva vinaśyati, tat-aṁkāra tu viśiṣyate | idaṁ tv aśeṣṇ sa-aṁkārāṇāṁ pāpānāṁ vilāpanaṁ vināśakam | na cānyena niḥśeṣa-pāpa-kṣayaḥ yād iti dṛṣṭāntenāha—yathā dhātūnām uvarṇādīnām udvartana-lakṣaṇa-prakṣālanādi dhātv-antara-aṁyogajaṁ malaṁ na nāśayati, kintu pāvaka eva, ataḥ sarvottamam idam evety arthaḥ ||20||



**kali-kalmaṣam atyugraṁ narakārti-pradaṁ nṛṇām |**

**prayāti vilayaṁ sadyaḥ sakṛd yatrānusaṁsmṛte ||21||**

**hiraṇyagarbha-devendra-rudrādityā-śiva-vāyubhiḥ |**

**kinnarair vasubhiḥ sādhyair viśvadevādibhiḥ suraiḥ ||22||**

**yakṣa-rakṣo-gaṇaiḥ siddhair daitya-gandharva-dānavaiḥ |**

**apsarobhis tathā tārā-nakṣatraiḥ sakalair grahaiḥ ||23||**

**saptarṣibhis tathā dhiṣṇyair dhiṣṇyādhipatibhis tathā |**

**brāhmaṇādyair manuṣyaiś ca tathaiva paśubhir mṛgaiḥ ||24||**

**sarīsṛpair vihaṅgaiś ca pretādyaiḥ samahīruhaiḥ |**

**vanādri-sāgara-sarit-pātālaiḥ sa-dharādibhiḥ ||25||**

**śabdādibhiś ca sahitaṁ brahmāṇḍam akhilaṁ dvija |**

**meror ivāṇur yasyaitad yan-mayaṁ ca dvijottama ||26||**

**sa sarvaḥ sarva-vit sarva-svarūpo rūpa-varjitaḥ |**

**kīrtyate bhagavān viṣṇur atra pāpa-praṇāśanaḥ ||27||**

**yad aśvamedhāvabhṛthe snātaḥ prāpnoti ca phalam |**

**sakalaṁ tad avāpnoti śrutvaitan muni-sattama ||28||**

**prayāte puṣkare caiva kurukṣetre tathārbude |**

**kṛtopavāsaḥ prāpnoti tad asya caraṇāravindāntaraḥ ||29||**

**yad agnihotraṁ suhute varṣeṇāpnoti vai phalam |**

**sakalaṁ samavāpnoti tad asya caraṇāravindāt sakṛt ||30||**

**yaj jyaiṣṭha-śukla-dvādaśyāṁ snātvā vai niyatendriyaḥ |**

**mathurāyāṁ hariṁ dṛṣṭvā prāpnoti paramāṁ gatim ||31||**

**tad āpnoti phalaṁ samyak samādhānena kīrtanāt |**

**purāṇasyāsya viparṣe keśavārpita-mānasaḥ ||32||**

**samabhyarcyācyutaṁ samyaṅ mathurāyāṁ samāhitaḥ |**

**aśvamedhasya yajñasya prāpnoty avikalaṁ phalam ||33||**

**yamunā-salile snātaḥ puruṣo muni-sattama |**

**jyeṣṭā-mūle’male pakṣe dvādaśyām upavāsa-kṛt ||34||**

**ālokyarddhim athānyeṣām unnītānāṁ sva-vaṁśajaiḥ |**

**etat kilocur anyeṣāṁ pitaraḥ sapitāmahāḥ ||35||**

**kaścid asmat-kule jātaḥ kālindī-salilāplutaḥ |**

**arcayiṣyati govindaṁ mathruāyām upoṣitaḥ ||36||**

**jyeṣṭhā-mūle878 site pakṣe yenaivaṁ vayam apy uta |**

**parām ṛddhim avāpsyāmas tāritāḥ sva-kulodbhavaiḥ ||37||**

**jyeṣṭhā-mūle site pakṣe samabhyarcya janārdanam |**

**dhanyānāṁ kulajaḥ piṇḍān yamunāyāṁ pradāsyati ||38||**

**tasmin kāle samabhyarcya tatra kṛṣṇaṁ samāhitaḥ |**

**dattvā piṇḍān pitṛbhyaś ca yamunā-salilāplutaḥ ||39||**



śrīdharaḥ : samādhānena kīrtanād yat phalam uktaṁ, tad eva amāhitaḥ an śrutvāpi prāpnotīty āha—tasmin kāle iti tribhiḥ ||39||



**yad āpnoti naraḥ puṇyaṁ tārayan sa pitāmahān |**

**śrutvādhyāyaṁ tad āpnoti purāṇasyāsya bhaktimān ||40||**

**etat saṁsāra-bhīrūṇāṁ paritrāṇam anuttamam |**

**duḥsvapnāśanaṁ nṛṇāṁ sarva-duṣṭa-nivarhaṇam ||41||**

**idam ārṣaṁ purā prāha ṛbhave kamalodbhavaḥ |**

**ṛbhuḥ priyavratāyāha sa ca bhāguraye’bravīt ||42||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **etat purāṇa-sampradāyaṁ kathayann āha—idam ārṣam ity-ādinā | ṛṣir nārāyaṇaḥ, tena proktam ārṣam ||42||



**bhāguriḥ stavamitrāya dadhīcāya sa coktavān |**

**sa vai sārasvate prādād bhṛguḥ sārasvatād api ||43||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **bhṛguḥ prāptavān iti śeṣaḥ ||43||



**bhṛguṇā purukutsāya narmadāyai sa coktavān |**

**narmadā dhṛtarāṣṭrāya nāgāya pūraṇāya ca ||44||**

**tābhyām ca nāgarājāya proktaṁ vāsukaye dvija |**

**vāsukiḥ prāha vatsāya vatsaś cāśvatarāya vai ||45||**

**kambalāya ca tenoktam elāpatrāya tena ca |**

**pātālaṁ samanuprāptas tato vedaśirā muniḥ ||46||**

**prāptavān etad akhilaṁ sa vai pramataye dadau |**

**dattaṁ pramatinā caiva jātūkarṇāya dhīmate ||47||**

**jātūkarṇena caivoktam anyeṣāṁ puṇya-śālinām |**

**vaiśiṣṭa-vara-dānena mamāpy etat smṛtiṁ gatam ||48||**

**mayāpi tubhyaṁ maitreya yathāvat kathitaṁ tv idam |**

**tvam apy etac chamīkāya kaler ante gadiṣyasi ||49||**

**ity etat paramaṁ guhyaṁ kali-kalmaṣa-nāśanam |**

**yaḥ śṛṇoti naraḥ pāpaiḥ sa sarvair dvija mucyate ||50||**

**pitṛ-pakṣa-manuṣyebhyaḥ samastāmara-saṁstutiḥ |**

**kṛtā tena bhaved etad yaḥ śṛṇoti dine dine ||51||**

**kapilādāna-janitaṁ puṇyamaty-anta-durlabham |**

**śrutvaitasya daśādhyāyān879 avāpnoti na saṁśayaḥ ||52||**

**yas tv etat sakalaṁ śṛṇoti puruṣaḥ kṛtvā manasy acyutaṁ**

**sarvaṁ sarva-mayaṁ samasta-jagatām ādhāram ātmāśrayam |**

**jñānaṁ jñeyam anantam ādya-rahitaṁ sarvāmarāṇāṁ hitaṁ**

**sa prāpnoti na saṁśayo’sty avikalaṁ yad-vājimedhe phalam ||53||**

**yatrādau bhagavāṁś carācara-gurur madhye tathānte ca saḥ**

**brahma-jñāna-mayo’cyuto’khila-jagan-madhyānta-sarva-prabhuḥ |**

**tac chṛṇvan puruṣaḥ pavitra-paramaṁ bhaktyā paṭhan dhārayan**

**prāpnoty asti na tat samasta-bhuvaneṣv ekānta-siddhir hariḥ ||54||**

**yasmin nyasta-matir na yāti narakaṁ svargo’pi yac cintane**

**vighno yatra niveśitātma-manaso brāhmo’pi loko’lpakaḥ |**

**muktiṁ cetasi yaḥ sthito’mala-dhiyāṁ puṁsāṁ dadāty avyayaḥ**

**kiṁ citraṁ yad aghaṁ prayāti vilayaṁ tatrācyute kīrtite ||55||**

**yajñair yajña-vido yajanti satataṁ yajñeśvaraṁ karmiṇo**

**yaṁ yaṁ brahma-mayaṁ parāpara-mayaṁ dhyāyanti ca jñāninaḥ |**

**yaṁ ca prāpya na jāyate na mriyate no vardhate hīyate**

**naivāsanna ca sad bhavaty ati tataḥ kiṁ vā hareḥ śrūyatām ||56||**

**kavyaṁ yaḥ pitṛ-rūpa-dhṛg vidhi-hutaṁ havyaṁ ca bhuṅkte prabhuḥ**

**devatve bhagavān anādi-nidhanaḥ svāhā-svadhā-saṁjñitam |**

**yasmin brahmaṇi sarva-śakti-nilaye mānāni no mānināṁ**

**niṣṭhāyai prabhavanti hanti kaluṣaṁ śrotraṁ sa yāto hariḥ ||57||**



**śrīdharaḥ :**vipra-mukhaiḥ vidhinā hutaṁ kayvaṁ devatve vartamāne havyaṁ ca yo bhuṅkte, mānināṁ mānāni yasmin niṣṭhāyai paricchedāya na samarthāni sva-prakāśatvāt, sa hariḥ śrotraṁ prāptaḥ kaluṣaṁ hanti, tasmāt sa eva śrotavya ity arthaḥ ||57||



**nānto’sti yasya na ca yasya samudbhavo’sti**

**vṛddhir na yasya pariṇāma-vivarjitasya |**

**nāpakṣayaṁ ca samupaitya vikalpa-vastu**

**yas taṁ nato’smi puruṣottamam ādyam īśam ||58||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **idānīṁ purāṇa-amāptau bhagavataḥ ṛṣṭy-ādy-upayogitayā pratipāditaṁ parameśvara-puruṣa-pradhāna-vyaktākhyaṁ rūpa-catuṣṭayaṁ praṇamati—nānta iti caturbhiḥ ślokaiḥ | avikalpaṁ vatu brahmaiva ya tam ||58||



**tasyaiva yo’nuguṇa-bhug bahudhaika eva**

**śuddho’py aśuddha iva mūrti-vibhāga-bhedaiḥ |**

**jñānānvitaḥ sakala-sattva-vibhūti-kartā **

**tasmai nato’smi puruṣāya sadāvyayāya ||59||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **kālo’pi īśvare’ntar-bhūtaḥ, tayaivānu parameśvarāt amanantaraḥ bahudhā brahmādi-rūpeṇa aśuddha iva ṛṣṭy-ādiṣv ākta iva mūrti-vibhāgānāṁ dakṣādi-manv-ādi-rūpāṇāṁ bhedaiḥ sarva-attvānāṁ vibhūti-kartā vitāra-kartā ||59||



**jñāna-pravṛtti-niyamaikya-mayāya puṁso**

**bhoga-pradāna-paṭave triguṇātmakāya |**

**avyākṛtāya bhava-bhāvana-kāraṇāya**

**vande svarūpam abhavāya sadājarāya ||60||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **jñānaṁ ca pravṛttiś caitayor niyamaḥ aṅkocaḥ tad-eka-mayāya, tatra hetuḥ—tri-guṇātmakāya iti | svarūpa-bhavāyeti pāṭhe ṣaṣṭhy-arthe caturthī | avyākṛtaya svarūpaṁ vande | pūrva-pāṭhe tu karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī avyākṛtaṁ vanda ity arthaḥ ||60||



**vyomānilāgni-jala-bhū-racanā-mayāya**

**śabdādi-bhoga-viṣayopanaya-kṣamāya |**

**puṁsaḥ samasta-karaṇair upakārakāya **

**vyaktāya sūkṣma-vimalāya sadā nato’smi ||61||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **vyaktāya parampar-varūpāya | ūkṣmeṇa brahma-varūpeṇa vimalāya | pāṭhāntare ūkṣme avyakte vilayo yayety arthaḥ ||61|| 



**iti vividham ajasya yasya rūpaṁ**

**prakṛti-parāt samayaṁ sanātanasya |**

**pradiśatu bhagavān aśeṣa-puṁsāṁ**

**harir apajanma-jarādikāṁ sa siddhim ||62||**



**śrīdharaḥ : **idānīm ukta-catuḥ-varūpād bhagavataḥ amata-jīvānām etat purāṇādi-dvāreṇa mokṣam āśānaḥ purāṇārthaṁ nigamayati—itīti | prakṛti-paramātma-mayaṁ prakṛtiḥ vyaktāvyakta-varūpāḥ, para īśvaraḥ, ātmā puruṣaḥ, tan-mayam apagata-janma-jarādi-lakṣaṇām iddhiṁ pradiśatv ity āśīrvādaḥ ||62||



iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe ṣaṣṭhe’ṁśe navamo’dhyāyaḥ 



—o\)0\(o—



|| samāptam idaṁ śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇam ||



—o\)0\(o—


[^1]: apaccarād
[^2]: Check here. This word \(*pravekṣyati*\) was added to complete the sense.

[^12]: cetasā \(ka\) |

[^65]: ātma-vināśāya iti jīva-gosvāminaḥ pāṭhaḥ.
[^66]: druhyos tu tanayo babhruḥ ||1|| tataḥ setuḥ, setu-putra āradvān nāma, tad-ātmajo gāndhāraḥ, tato dharmaḥ, dharmād dhṛtaḥ, dhṛtād durgamaḥ, tataḥ pracetāḥ, pracetasaḥ putra-śatam adharma-bahulānāṁ mlecchānām udīcyādīnām ādhipatyam akarot ||2||
[^67]: . śraute smārte dharme


[^68]: . ādi-mayasyānta-mayasya sarva-mayasya brahma-mayasyātma-svarūpiṇaḥ iti \* |
[^69]: . jagat iti eva-śabda-sthāne iti \*.
[^70]: . prabuddhānām iti \*.
[^71]: 

    Although with different numbers, after this śloka *kha* it includes the following verses:
    
    
    
    **śṛṇuyād ya imaṁ bhaktyā manuvaṁśamanukramāt |**
    
    **tasya pāpamaśeṣaṁ vai praṇaśyatyamalātmanaḥ ||66||**
    
    
    
    **dhanadhānyarddhimatulā prāpnotyavyāhatendriyaḥ |**
    
    **śrutvaivamakhilaṁ vaṁśaṁ praśastaṁ śaśisūryayoḥ ||67||**
    
    
    
    **ikṣvāku-jahnu-māndhātṛ-sagarā-vikṣitān raghūna |**
    
    **yayāti-nahuṣādyāṁśca jñātvā niṣṭhāmupāgatān |**
    
    **mahābalān mahāvīryānantadhanasañcayān ||68||**
    
    
    
    **kṛtān kālena balinā kathāśeṣān narādhipān |**
    
    **śrutvā na putradārādau gṛhakṣetrādike tathā |**
    
    **dravyādau ca kṛtaprajño mamatvaṁ kurute naraḥ ||69||**
    
    
    
    **taptaṁ tapo yaiḥ puruṣa-pravīrair udbāhubhir varṣa-gaṇān anekān |**
    
    **iṣṭāś ca yajñā balino'tivīryāḥ kṛtāstu kālena kathāvaśeṣāḥ ||70||**
    
    
    
    **śrīdharaḥ : **na ca teṣāṁ tapaḥ prabhāvādyabhāvāt kathāvaśeṣatvamityāha, taptam iti ||70|| 
    
    
    
    **pṛthuḥ samastān pracacāra lokānavyāhato yo'rividāricakra |**
    
    **sa kālavātābhihato vinaṣṭaḥ kṣiptaṁ yathā śālmalitūlamagnau ||71||**
    
    
    
    **śrīdharaḥ : **tānevāha—pṛthur iti dvābhyām ||71||
    
    
    
    **yaḥ kārtavīryo bubhūje samastān dvīpān samākramya hatāricakraḥ | kathāprasaṅge tvabhidhīyamānaḥ sa eva saṅgalpavikalpahetuḥ ||72||**
    
    
    
    **śrīdharaḥ : **saṅkalpavikalpayoḥ keṣāñcit saṅkalpasya tatheti pratyayasya, keṣāñcid vikalpasya kimāsīnna veti sandehasya, heturnimittaṁ, saṁkalpasya manaso vikalpahetuḥ ||72||
    
    
    
    **daśānanā-vikṣita-rāghavāṇāmaiśvayakramudbhāsitadiṅmukhānām | bhasmāpi jātaṁ na kathaṁ kṣaṇenamrūbhaṅgapātena dhigantakasya ||73||**
    
    
    
    **śrīdharaḥ : **udbhāsitāni diṅmukhāni yaiḥ | udbhāsitadigvitānamiti pāṭhe aiśvaryaviśeṣaṇam | teṣāṁ rāvaṇādīnāmaiśvaryam antakasya bhrūbhaṅgapātena kathaṁ bhasma na jātaṁ, kintu jātameva, tasmādaivaśvaryaṁ dhik | yadvā kāṣṭhaṁ dagdhamapi bhasma bhavati, aiśvaryaṁ bhasmāpi na jātaṁ kiñcidavaśiṣṭamapi kathaṁ na jātaṁ? tasmāt dhik ||73||
    
    
    
    **kathāśarīratvamavāpa yad vai māndhātṛnāmā bhuvi cakravartī |**
    
    **śrutvāpi taṁ ko'pi karoti sādhumarmatvamātmanyapi mandacetāḥ ||74||**
    
    
    
    **śrīdharaḥ : **ātmanyahaṅkārāspade dehe'pi kiṁ punaḥ putradārādau ||74|| 
    
    
    
    **bhagīrathādyāḥ sagaraḥ kakutstho daśānano rāghava lakṣmaṇau ca | yudhiṣṭhirādyāśca babhūvurete**
    
    **satyaṁ na mithyā kva nu te na vidmaḥ ||75||**
    
    
    
    **śrīdharaḥ : **bhagīrathādyāḥ satyaṁ jātāḥ, kintu kva te iti na vidmaḥ, kālenādarśanaṁ nītā ity arthaḥ | atra rāghavadīnāṁ grahaṇaṁ lokadṛṣṭyā vairāgyārtham ||75|| 
    
    
    
    **ye sāmprataṁ ye ca nṛpā bhaviṣyāḥ proktā mayā vipravarogravīryāḥ |**
    
    **ye te tathānye ca tathābhidheyāḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti yathaiva pūrve ||76||**
    
    
    
    **śrīdharaḥ : **tathā anye'nuktāstathābhidheyāḥ kathāmātrāvaśeṣā bhaviṣyantītyarthaḥ ||76||
    
    
    
    **etad viditvā na nareṇa kāryaṁ mamatvamātmanyapi paṇḍitena |**
    
    **tiṣṭhantu tāvat tanayātmajādyāḥ kṣetrādayo ye tu śarīrato'nye ||77||**
    
    
    
    **śrīdharaḥ : **etadaśaṁtātparyārthaṁ saṁkṣipyāha—etad iti | tanayādayastiṣṭhantu mamatvaṁ sutarāṁ na kāryamity arthaḥ ||77|| 
    
    
    
    iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ caturthāṁśe catuviṁśo'dhyāyaḥ ||
    
    
    
    caturthāṁśaḥ sampūrṇa
    
    
    
    **iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe caturthāṁśe catuviṁśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ||**

[^857]: māa iti manuṣyāṇāṁ iti śeṣaḥ | pitṝṇāṁ pitṛ-loka-gatānāṁ aho-rātraḥ | abdaḥ vataraḥ manuṣyāṇāṁ iti śeṣaḥ | tridivaukaāṁ devānāṁ ahorātraḥ | dve caturyuga-ahare manuṣyāṇāṁ iti śeṣaḥ | brahmaṇaḥ ahorātraḥ ekaika iti śeṣaḥ ||
[^858]: . tatra \(BP\)
[^859]: vārtha-hāniṁ na mānavāḥ.

[^867]: brahma-bhūtena śakyate
